|p20  jAmayo adhvarIyatAm pR^i~NcatIr madhunA paya iti
|p21  yo 'madhavyo yasho 'rtor bubhUShed
|p22  amUr yA upa sUrye yAbhir vA sUryaH saheti tejaskAmo brahmavarcasakAmo
|p23  'po devIr upa hvaye yatra gAvaH pibanti na iti pashukAmas
|p24  tA etAH sarvA evAnubruvann anuprapadyetaiteShAM kAmAnAm avaruddhyA
|p25  etAn kAmAn avarunddhe ya evaM vedai/mA
|p26  agman revatIr jIvadhanyA iti
     sAdyamAnAsv anvAha vasatIvarIShv ekadhanAsu cA/gmann
|p27  Apa ushAtIr barhir edam iti sannAsu. sa etayA paridadhAti

|c21
|p1  shiro vA etad yaj~Nasya yat prAtaranuvAkaH, prANApAnA upAMshvantaryAmau,
     vajra eva vA.N. nAhutayor upAMshvantaryAmayor hotA vAcaM visR^ijeta
|p2  yad ahutayor upAMshvantaryAmayor hotA vAcaM visR^ijeta,
     vAcA vajreNa yajamAnasya prANAn vIyAD ya enaM tatra brUyAd:
     vAcA vajreNa yajamAnasya prANAn vyagAt, prANa enaM hAsyatIti,
     shashvat tathA syAT tasmAn nAhutayor upAMshvantaryAmayor hotA vAcaM visR^ijeta
|p3  prANaM yacha svAhA tvA suhava sUryAyety upAMshum anumantrayeta,
     tam abhiprAnet: prANa prANam me yachety.
     ApanAM yacha svAhA tvA suhava sUryAyety antaryAmam anumantrayeta,
     tam abhyapAned: apAnApAnam me yacheti.
     vyAnAya tvety upAMshusavanaM grAvANam abhimR^ishya vAcaM visR^ijata
|p4  AtmA vA upAMshusavana,
     Atmany eva tad dhotA prANAn pratidhAya vAcaM visR^ijate sarvAyuH sarvAyutvAya
|p5  sarvam Ayur eti ya evAM veda

|c22
|p1  tad AhuH: sarpe+t \ na sarpe+t iti \ sarped iti haika Ahur,
     ubhayeShAM vA eSha devamanuShyANAm bhakSho yad bahiShpavamAnas,
     tasmAd enam abhisaMgachanta iti vadantas
|p2  tat-tan nAdR^ityaM
|p3  yat sarped, R^icam eva tat sAmno 'nuvartmAnaM kuryAd. ya enaM tatra brUyAd:
     anuvartmA nvA ayaM hotA sAmagasyAbhUd, udgAtari yasho 'dhAd,
     acyoShTAyatanAc, cyoShyata AyatanAd iti, shashvat tathA syAt
|p4  tasmAt tatraivAsIno 'numantrayeta
|p5  yo devAnAm iha somapItho yaj~Ne barhiShi vedyA+m \ tasyApi bhakShayAmasIty
|p6  evam u hAsyAtmA somapIthAd anantarito bhavaty
|p7  atho brUyAn: mukham asi mukham bhUyAsAm iti
|p8  mukhaM vA etad yaj~Nasya yad bahiShpavamAno
|p9  mukhaM sveShu bhavati, shreShThaH svAnAm bhavati ya evAM vedA/surI
|p10  vai #dirghajihvI devAnAm prAtaHsavanam avAleT, tad vyamAdyat.
     te devAH prAjij~NAsanta, te #mitrAvaruNAv abruvan:
     yuvam idaM niShkurutam iti. tau tathety abrUtAM,
     tau vai vo varaM vR^iNAvahA iti. vR^iNAthAm iti. tAv etam eva varam avR^iNAtAm:
     prAtaHsavane payasyAM. sainayor eShAcyutA, varavR^itA hy enAyos.
     tad yad asyai vimattam iva tad asyai samR^iddhaM,
     vimattam iva hi tau tayA nirakurutAm

|c23
|p1  devAnAM vai savanAni nAdhriyanta. ta etAn puro.lAshAn apashyaMs,
     tAn anusavanaM niravapan savanAnAM dhR^ityai,
     tato vai tAni teShAm adhriyanta
|p2  tad yad anusavanam puro.lAshA nirupyante, savanAnAm eva dhR^ityai;
     tathA hi tAni teShAm adhriyanta
|p3  puro vA etAn devA akrata yat puro.lAshAs, tat puro.lAshAnAm puro.lAshatvaM
|p4  tad Ahur: anusavanam puro.lAshAn nirvaped, aShTAkapAlam prAtaHsavana,
     ekAdashakapAlam mAdhyaMdine savane, dvAdashakapAlaM tR^itIyasavane;
     tathA hi savanAnAM rUpaM tathA chandasAm iti
|p5  tat-tan nAdR^ityam.
     aindrA vA ete sarve nirupyante yad anusavanam puro.lAsAs,
     tasmAt tAn ekAdashakapAlAn eva nirvapet
|p6  tad Ahur:
     yato ghR^itenAnaktaM syAt tataH puro.lAshasya prAshnIyAt somapIthasya guptyai,
     ghR^itena hi vajreNendro #vR^itram ahann iti
|p7  tat-tan nAdR^ityaM. havir vA etad yad utpUtaM,
     somapItho vA eSha yad utpUtaM. tasmAt tasya yata eva kutash ca prAshnIyAt.
     sarvato vA etAH svadhA yajamAnam upakSharanti yad etAni havIMShy:
     AjyaM dhAnAh karambhaH parivApaH puro.lAshaH payasyeti
|p8  sarvata evainaM svadhA upakSharanti ya evaM veda

|c24
|p1  yo vai yaj~NaM haviShpa.NktiM veda, haviShpa.NktinA yaj~Nena rAdhnoti.
     dhAnAH karambhaH parivApaH puro.lAshaH payasyety eSha vai yaj~No
     haviShpa.Nktir, haviShpa.NktinA yaj~Nena rAdhnoti ya evaM veda
|p2  yo vai yaj~Nam akSharapa.NktiM vedAkSharapa.NktinA yaj~Nena rAdhnoti.
     su mat pad vag da ity eSha vai yaj~No 'kSharapa.Nktir,
     akSharapa.NktinA yaj~Nena rAdhnoti ya evaM veda
|p3  yo vai yaj~NaM narAshaMsapa.NktiM veda,
     narAshaMsapa.NktinA yaj~Nena rAdhnoti.
     dvinArAshaMsam prAtaHsavanaM dvinArAshaMsAm mAdhyaMdinaM savanaM
     sakR^innArAshaMsaM tR^itIyasavanam, eSha vai yaj~No narAshaMsapa.Nktir.
     narAshaMsapa.NktinA yaj~Nena rAdhnoti ya evaM veda
|p4  yo vai yaj~NaM savanapa.NktiM veda, savanapa.NktinA yAj~Nena rAdhnoti.
     pashur upavasathe trINi savanAni pashur anUbandhya
     ity eSha vai yaj~NaH savanapa.NktiH,
     savanapa.NktinA yaj~Nena rAdhnoti ya evaM veda
|p5  harivA~M Indro dhAnA attu, pUShaNvAn karambhaM, sarasvatIvAn bhAratIvAn,
     parivApa, IndrasyApUpa iti haviShpaiiktya yajatyviShpa.NktyA yajaty
|p6  R^iksAme vA Indrasya harI
|p7  pashavaH #pUShAnnaM karambhaH
|p8  sarasvatIvAn bhAratIvAn iti, vAg eva #sarasvatI prANo #bharataH
|p9  parivApa IndrasyApUpa ity, annam eva parivApa, indriyam apUpa
|p10  etAsAm eva tad devatAnAM yajamAnaM sAyujyaM sarUpatAM salokatAM gamayati.
     gachati shreyasaH sAyujyaM, gachati shreShThatAM ya evaM veda
|p11  havir #agne vIhIty anusasavanam puro.lAshasviShTakR^ito yajaty
|p12  #avatsAro vA etenAgneH priyaM dhAmopAgachat, sa paramaM lokam ajayad
|p13  upAgneH priyaM dhAma gachati, jayati paramaM lokaM ya evaM veda
     yash caivaM vidvAn etayA haviShpa.NktyA yajate yajatIti ca yajatIti ca

|c25 {adhyAya 9, khaNDaH 1-8}
|p1  devA vai somasya rAj~No 'grapeye na samapAdayann.
     aham prathamaH pibeyam aham prathamaH pibeyam ity evAkAmayanta.
     te sampAdayanto 'bruvan: hantAjim AyAma,
     sa yo na ujjeShyati sa prathamaH somasya pAsyatIti. tatheti.
     ta Ajim Ayus, teShAm AjiM yatAm abhisR^iShTAnAM #vAyur mukham
     prathamaH pratyapadyatAthendro 'tha #mitrAvaruNAv athAshvinAu
|p2  so 'ved #indro #vAyum ud vai jayatIti, tam anuparApatat:
     saha nAv, athojjayAveti.
     sa nety abravId, aham evojjeShyAmIti.
     tR^itIyam me, 'thojjayAveti. neti haivAbravId, aham evojjeShyAmIti.
     turIyam me, 'thojjayAveti. tatheti. taM turIye 'tyArjata,
     tat turIyabhAg #indro 'bhavat tribhAg #vAyus
|p3  tau sahaivendravAyU udajayatAM saha #mitrAvaruNau sahAshvinau,
     ta eShAm ete yathojjitam bhakShA:
     #indravAyvoH prathamo 'tha #mitrAvaruNayor athAshvinoH
|p4  sa eSha indraturIyo graho gR^ihyate yad aindravAyavas
|p5  tad etad R^iShiH pashyann abhyanUvAca: niyutvA~M indrasArathir iti
|p6  tasmAd dhApy etarhi bharatAH satvanAM vittim prayanti,
     turIye haiva saMgrahItAro vadante 'munaivAnUkAshena,
     yad ada #indraH sArathir iva bhUtvodajayat

|c26
|p1  te vA ete prANA eva yad dvidevatyA
|p2  vAk ca prANash caindravAyavash, cakShush ca manash ca maitrAvaruNaH,
     shrotraM cAtmA cAshvinAs
|p3  tasya haitasyaindravAyavasyApy eke 'nuShTubhau
     puronuvAkye kurvanti gAyatryau yAjye
|p4  vAk ca vA eSha prANAsh ca graho yad aindravAyavas,
     tad api chandobhyAM yathAyathaM klapsyete iti
|p5  tat-tan nAdR^ityaM. vyR^iddhaM vA etad yaj~Ne kriyate
     yatra puronuvAkyA jyAyasI yAjyAyai.
     yatra vai yAjyA jyAyasi, tat samR^iddham, atho yatra sAme.
     yasyo tat kAmAya tathA kuryAt prANasya ca vAcash cAtraiva tad upAptaM
|p6  vAyavyA pUrvA puronuvAkyaindravAyavy uttaraivaM yAjyayoH.
     sA yA vAyavyA tayA prANaM kalpayati, #vAyur hi prANo.
     'tha yaindravAyavI tasyai yad aindram padaM tena vAcaM kalpayati,
     vAg ghy aindry. upo taM kAmam Apnoti yaH prANe ca vAci ca,
     na yaj~Ne viShamaM karoti

|c27
|p1  prANA vai dvidevatyA, ekapAtrA gR^ihyante tasmAt prANA ekanAmAno,
     dvipAtrA hUyante tasmAt prANA dvandvaM
|p2  yenaivAdhvaryur yajuShA prayachati, tena hotA pratigR^ihNAty
|p3  eSha vAsuH purUvasur iha vasuH purUvasur mayi vasuH purUvasur
     vAkpA vAcam me pAhIty aindravAyavam bhakShayaty
|p4  upahUtA vAk saha prANenopa mAM vAk saha prANena hvayatAm;
     upahUtA R^iShayo daivyAsas tanUpAvAnas tanvas tapojA,
     upa mAm R^iShayo daivyAso hvayantAM tanUpAvAnas tanvas tapojA iti
|p5  prANA vA R^iShayo daivyAsas tAnUpAvAnas tanvas tapojAs,
     tAn eva tad upahvayata
|p6  eSha vasur vidadvasur iha vasur vidadvasur mayi vasur vidadvasush
     cakShuShpAsh cakShur me pAhIti maitrAvaruNam bhakShayaty.
     upahUtAM cakShuH saha manasopa mAM cakShuH saha manasA hvayatAm;
     upahUtA R^iShayo daivyAsas tanUpAvAnas tanvas tapojA,
     upa mAm R^iShayo daivyAso hvayantAM tanUpAvAnas tanvas tapojA iti.
     prANA vA R^iShayo daivyAsas tanUpAvAnas tanvas tapojAs,
     tAn eva tad upahvayata
|p7  eSha vasuH saMyadvasur iha vasuH saMyadvasur mayi vasuH saMyadvasuH
     shrotrApAH shrotram me pAhIty AshvinAm bhakShayaty.
     upahUtaM shrotraM sahAtmanopa mAM shrotraM sahAtmanA hvayAtam,
     upahUtA R^iShayo daivyAsas tanUpAvAnas tanvas tapojA,
     upa mAm R^iShayo daivyAso hvayantAM tanUpAvAnas tanvas tapojA iti.
     prANA vA R^iShayo daivyAsas tanUpAvAnas tanvas tapojAs,
     tAn eva tad upahvayate
|p8  purastAt pratya~Ncam aindravAyavam bhakShayati, tasmAt purastAt prANApAnau.
     purastAt pratya~Ncam maitrAvaruNam bhakShayati, tasmAt purastAc cakShuShI.
     sarvataH parihAram Ashvinam bhakShayati,
     tasmAn manuShyAsh ca pashavash ca sarvato vAcaM vadantIM shR^iNvanti

|c28
|p1  prANA vai dvidevatyA,
     anavAnaM dvidevatyAn yAjet prANAnAM saMtatyai prANAnAm avyavachedAya
|p2  prANA vai dvidevatyA,
     na dvidevatyAnAm anuvaShaTkuryad
|p3  yad dvidevatyAnAm anuvaShaTkuryAd asaMsthitAn prANAn saMsthApayet,
     saMsthA vA eShA yad anuvaShaTkAro. ya enaM tatra brUyAd:
     asaMsthitan prANAn samatiShThipat prANa enam hAsyatIti,
     shashvat tathA syAt. tasmAn na dvidevatyAnAm anuvaShaTkuryAt
|p4  tad Ahur: dvir AgUrya maitrAvaruNo dviH preShyati,
     sakR^iid AgUrya hotA dvir vaShaTkaroti: kA hotur AgUr iti
|p5  prANA vai dvidevatyA, AgUr vajras.
     tad yad hotAntareNAguretAgurA vajreNa yajamAnasya prANAn vIyAd.
     ya enAM tatra brUyAd:
     AgurA vAjreNa yajamAnasya prANAn vyagAt prANa enaM hAsyatIti,
     shashvat tathA syAt. tasmAt tatra hotAntareNa nAgureta/tho
|p6  mano vai yaj~Nasya maitrAvaruNo, vAg yaj~Nasya hotA.
     manasA vA iShitA vAg vadati; yAM hy anyamanA vAcaM vadaty,
     asuryA vai sA vAg adevajuShTA. tad yad evAtra maitrAvaruNo dvir Agurate,
     saiva hotur AgUH

|c29
|p1  prANA vA R^ituyAjAs. tad yad R^ituyAjaish cAranti,
     prANAn eva tad yajamAne dadhati
|p2  Sha.l R^ituneti yajanti, prANam eva tad yajamAne dadhati
|p3  catvAra R^itubhir iti yajanty, apAnam eva tad yajamAne dadhati
|p4  dvir R^itunety upariShTAd, vyAnam eva tad yajamAne dadhati
|p5  sa vA ayam prANas tredhA vihitaH: prANo 'pAno vyAna iti.
     tad yad R^ituna R^itubhir R^ituneti yajanti,
     prANAnAM saMtatyai prANAnAm avyavachedAya
|p6  prANA vA R^ituyAjA. nartuyAjAnAm anuvaShaTkuryAd,
     asaMsthitA vA R^itava, ekaika eva
|p7  yad R^ituyAjAnAm anuvaShaTkuryAd asAMsthitAn R^itUn saMsthApayet,
     saMsthA vA eShA yad anuvaShaTkAro. ya enaM tatra brUyAd:
     asaMsthitAn R^itUn samatiShThipad duShShamam bhaviShyatIti,
     shashvat tathA syAt. tasmAn nartuyAjAnAm anuvaShaTkuryAt

|c30
|p1  prANA vai dvidevatyAH, pashava i.lA. dvidevatyAn bhakShayitve.lAm upahvayate.
     pashavo vA i.lA, pashUn eva tad upahvayate, pashUn yajamAne dadhAti
|p2  tad Ahur: avAntare.lAm pUrvAm prAshnIyA+t \ hotR^icamasam bhakShaye+t iti \
|p3  avAntare.lAm eva pUrvAm prAshnIyAd, atha hotR^icamasam bhakShayed
|p4  yad vAva dvidevatyAn pUrvAn bhakShayati,
     tenAsya somapIthaH pUrvo bhakShito bhavati.
     tasmAd avantare.lam eva pUrvAm prAshnIyAd, atha= hotR^icamasam bhakShayet.
     tad ubhayato 'nnAdyam parigR^ihNAti somapIthAbhyAm, annAdyasya parigR^ihItyai
|p5  prANA vai dvidevatyA, AtmA hotR^icamaso.
     dvidevatyAnAM saMsravAn hotR^icamase samavanayaty,
     Atmany eva tad dhotA prANAn samavanayate sarvAyuH sarvAyutvAya
|p6  sarvam Ayur eti ya evaM veda

|c31
|p1  devA vai yad eva yaj~Ne 'kurvaMs tad asurA akurvaMs,
     te samAvadvIryA evAsan na vyAvartanta.
     tato vai devA etaM tUShNIMshaMsam apashyaMs, tam eShAm asurA nAnvavAyaMs.
     tUShNIMsAro vA eSha yat tUShNIMshaMso
|p2  devA vai yaM-yam eva vajram asurebhya udayachaMs,
     taM-tam eShAm asurAH pratyabudhyanta.
     tato vai devA etaM tUShNIMshaMsaM vajram apashyaMs, tam ebhya udayachaMs,
     tam eShAm asurA na pratyabudhyanta. tam ebhyaH prAharaMs,
     tenainAn apratibuddhenAghnaMs. tato vai devA abhavan, parAsurA
|p3  bhavaty AtmanA, parAsya dviShan pApmA bhrAtR^ivyo bhavati, ya evaM veda
|p4  te vai devA vijitino manyamAnA yaj~Nam atanvata, tam eShAm asurA abhyAyan:
     yaj~Naveshasam eShAM kariShyAma iti.
     tAn samantam evodArAn pariyattAn udapashyaMs, te 'bruvan:
     saMsthApayAmemaM yaj~NaM, yaj~NaM no 'surA mA vadhiShur iti. tatheti.
     taM tUShNIMshaMse saMsthApayan:
     bhUr #agnir jyotir jyotir #agnir ity Ajyapra:uge saMsthApayann:
     #indro jyotir bhuvo jyotir #indra iti niShkevalyamarutvatIye saMsthApayan:
     #sUryo jyotir jyotiH svaH #sUrya iti vaishvadevAgnimArute saMsthApayaMs.
     tam evaM tUShNIMshaMse saMsthApayaMs,
     tam evAM tUShNIMshaMse saMsthApya tenAriShTenodR^icam Ashnuvata
|p5  sa tadA vAva yaj~NaH saMtiShThate, yadA hotA tUShNIMshaMsaM shaMsati
|p6  sa ya enaM shaste tUShNIMshaMsa upa vA vaded anu vA vyAharet, tam brUyAd:
     eSha evaitAm Artim AriShyati.
     prAtar vAva vayam adyemaM shaste tUShNIMshaMse saMsthApayAmas.
     taM yathA gR^ihAn itaM karmaNAnusamiyAd, evam evainam idam anusamima iti.
     so ha vAva tAm Artim R^ichati,
     ya evaM vidvAn saMshaste tUShNIMshaMsa upa vA vadaty anu vA vyAharati.
     tasmAd evaM vidvAn saMshaste tUShNIMshaMse nopavaden, nAnuvyAharet

|c32
|p1  cakShUMShi vA etAni savanAnAM yat tUShNIMshaMso.
     bhUr #agnir jyotir jyotir #agnir iti prAtaHsavanasya cakShuShI,
     #indro jyotir bhuvo jyotir #indra iti mAdhyaMdinasya savanasya cakShuShI,
     #sUryo jyotir jyotiH svaH #sUrya iti tR^itIyasavanasya cakShuShI
|p2  cakShuShmadbhiH savanai rAdhnoti,
     cakShuShmadbhiH savanaiH svargaM lokam eti ya evaM veda
|p3  cakShur vA etad yaj~Nasya yat tUShNIMshaMsa. ekA satI vyAhR^itir dvedhocyate,
     tasmAd ekaM sac cakShur dvedhA
|p4  mUlaM vA etad yaj~Nasya yat tUShNIMshaMso.
     yaM kAmayetAnAyatanavAn syAd iti, nAsya yaj~Ne tUShNIMshaMsaM shaMsed,
     unmUlam eva tad yaj~Nam parAbhavantam anu parAbhavati
|p5  tad u vA AhuH: shaMsed evApi vai tad R^itvije 'hitAM,
     yad dhotA tUShNIMshaMsaM na shaMsaty.
     R^itviji hi sarvo yaj~NaH pratiShThito yaj~Ne yajamAnas,
     tasmAc chaMstavyaH shaMstavyaH

|c33 {adhyAya 10, khaNDaH 1-9}
|p1  brahma vA AhAvaH, kShatraM nivid, viT sUktam.
     Ahivayate 'tha nividaM dadhAti, brahmaNy eva tat kShatram anuniyunakti.
     nividaM shastvA sUktaM shaMsati. kShatraM vai nivid viT sUktaM,
     kShatra eva tad visham anuniyunakti
|p2  yaM kAmayeta: kShatreNainaM vyardhayAnIti,
     madhya etasyai nividaH sUktaM shaMset. kShatraM vai nivid viT sUktaM,
     kShatreNaivainaM tad vyardhayati
|p3  yaM kAmayeta: vishainaM vyardhayAnIti,
     madhya etasya sUktasya nividaM shaMset. kShatraM vai nivid viT sUktaM,
     vishaivainaM tad vyardhayati
|p4  yam u kAmayeta: sarvam evAsya yathApUrvam R^iju k.lptaM syAd ity,
     AhvayetAtha nividaM dadhyAd atha sUktaM shaMset. so sarvasya k.lptiH
|p5  #prajApatir vA idam eka evAgra Asa. so 'kAmayata:
     prajAyeya bhUyAn syAm iti.
     sa tapo 'tapyata, sa vAcam ayachat,
     sa saMvatsarasya parastAd vyAharad dvAdashakR^itvo.
     dvAdashapadA vA eShA nivid, etAM vAva tAM nividaM vyAharat,
     tAm sarvANi bhUtAny anvasR^ijyanta
|p6  tad etad R^iShiH pashyann abhyanUvAca:
     sa pUrvayA nividA kavyatAyor imAH prajA ajanayan manUnAm iti
|p7  tad yad etAm purastAt sUktasya nividaM dadhAti, prajAtyai
|p8  prajAyate prajayA pashubhir ya evaM veda

|c34
|p1  #agnir deveddha iti shaMsaty. asau vA #agnir deveddha, etaM hi devA indhata.
     etam eva tad etasmi~Ml loka AyAtayaty
|p2  #agnir manviddha iti shaMsaty. ayaM vA #agnir manviddha,
     imaM hi manuShyA indhate. 'gnim eva tad asmi~Ml loka AyAtayaty
|p3  #agniH suShamid iti shaMsati.
     #vAyur vA #agniH suShamid, #vAyur hi svayam AtmAnaM saminddhe svayam
     idaM sarvaM yad idaM kiMca. #vAyum eva tad antarikShaloka AyAtayati
|p4  hotA devavR^ita iti shaMsaty. asau vai hotA devavR^ita,
     eSha hi sarvato devair vR^ita, etam eva tad etasmi~Ml loka AyAtayati
|p5  hotA manuvR^ita iti shaMsaty. ayaM vA #agnir hotA manuvR^ito,
     'yaM hi sarvato manuShyair vR^ito. 'gnim eva tad asmi~Ml loka AyAtayati
|p6  praNIr yaj~NAnAm iti shaMsati. #vAyur vai praNIr yaj~NAnAM.
     yadA hi prANity, atha yaj~No 'thAgnihotraM.
     #vAyum eva tad antarikShaloka AyAtayati
|p7  rathIr adhvarANAm iti shaMsaty.
     asau vai rathIr adhvarANAm,
     eSha hi yathaitac carati rathIr ivaitam eva tad etasmi~Ml loka AyAtayaty
|p8  atUrto hoteti shaMsaty.
     ayaM vA #agnir atUrto hotemaM ha na kash cana tirya~NcaM taraty.
     #agnim eva tad asmi~Ml loka AyAtayati
|p9  tUrNir havyavA.l iti shaMsati.
     #vAyur vai tUrNir havyavAD, #vAyur hIdaM sarvam sadyas tarati
     yad idaM kiMca, #vAyur devebhyo havyaM vahati.
     #vAyum eva tad autarikShaloka AyAtayaty
|p10  A devo devAn vakShad iti shaMsaty. asau vai devo devAn Avahaty,
     etam eva tad etasmi~Ml loka AyAtayati
|p11  yakShad #agnir devo devAn iti shaMsaty.
     ayaM vA #agnir devo devAn yajaty, #agnim eva tad asmi~Ml loka AyAtayati
|p12  so 'dhvarA karati jAtavedA iti shaMsati.
     #vAyur vai jAtavedA, #vAyur hIdaM sArvaM karoti yad idaM kiMca.
     #vAyum eva tad antarikShaloka AyAtayati

|c35
|p1  pra vo devAyAgnaya ity anuShTubhaH
|p2  prathame pade viharati, tasmAt stry UrU viharati
|p3  samasyaty uttare pade, tasmAt pumAn UrU samasyati.
     tan mithunam, mithunam eva tad ukthamukhe karoti prajAtyai
|p4  prajAyate prajayA pashubhir ya evaM veda
|p5  pra vo devAyAgnaya ity evAnuShTubhaH.
     prathame pade viharati, vajram eva tat parovarIyAMsaM karoti.
     samasyaty evottare pade.
     ArambhaNato vai vajrasyANimAtho daNDasyAtho parashor.
     vajram eva tat praharati dviShate bhrAtR^ivyAya vadhaM,
     yo 'sya stR^ityas tasmai startavai

|c36
|p1  devAsurA vA eShu lokeShu samayatanta.
     te vai devAH sada evAyatanam akurvata, tAn sadaso 'jayaMs.
     ta AgnIdhraM samprApadyanta, te tato na parAjayanta.
     tasmAd AgnIdhra upavasanti na sadasy, AgnIdhre hy adhArayanta.
     yad AgnIdhre 'dhArayanta tad AgnIdhrasyAgnIdhratvaM
|p2  teShAM vai devAnAm asurAH sadasyAn agnIn nirvApayAM cakrus.
     te devA AgnIdhrAd eva sadasyAn agnIn viharanta,
     tair asurarakShAMsy apAghnata.
     tathaivaitad yajamAnA AgnIdhrAd eva sadasyAn agnIn viharanty,
     asurarakShAMsy eva tad apaghnate
|p3  te vai prAtar Ajyair evAjayanta Ayan.
     yad Ajyair evAjayanta AyaMs tad AjyAnAm AjyatvaM
|p4  tAsAM vai hotrANAm AyatInAm AjayantInAm achAvAkIyAhIyata.
     tasyAm #indrAgnI adhyAstAm.
     #indrAgnI vai devAnAm ojiShThau baliShThau sahiShThau sattamau
     pArayiShNutamau. tasmAd aindrAgnam achAvAkaH prAtaHsavane
     shaMsatIndragnI hi tasyAm adhyAstAM
|p5  tasmAd u purastAd anye hotrakAH sadaH prasarpanti pashcAchAvAkaH,
     pashceva hi hIno 'nusaMjigamiShati
|p6  tasmAd yo brAhmaNo bahvR^ico vIryavAn syAt so 'syAchAvAkIyAM kuryAt,
     tenaiva sAhInA bhavati

|c37
|p1  devaratho vA eSha yad yaj~Nas, tasyaitAv antarau rashmI yad Ajyapra:uge.
     tad yad Ajyena pavamAnam anushaMsati pra:ugeNAjyaM,
     devarathasyaiva tad antarau rashmI viharaty alobhAya
|p2  tAm anukR^itim manuShyarathasyaivAntarau rashmI viharanty alobhAya
|p3  nAsya devaratho lubhyati na manuShyaratho ya evaM veda
|p4  tad Ahur: yathA vAva stotram evaM shastram. pAvamAnIShu sAmagAH stuvata,
     AgneyaM hotAjyaM shaMsati: katham asya pAvamAnyo 'nushastA bhavantIti
|p5  yo vA #agniH sa #pavamAnas
|p6  tad apy etad R^iShiNoktam: agnir R^iShiH pavamAna ity
|p7  evam u hAsyAgneyIbhir eva pratipadyamAnasya pAvamAnyo 'nushastA bhavanti
|p8  tAd Ahur: yathA vAva stotram evaM shastraM.
     gAyatrIShu sAmagAH stuvata, AnuShTubhaM hotAjyaM shaMsati:
     katham asya gAyatryo 'nushastA bhavantIti
|p9  sampadeti brUyat
|p10  saptaitA anunShTubhas, tAs triH prathamayA trir uttamayaikAdasha bhavanti.
     virAd. yAjyA dvAdashI. na vA ekenAkShareNa chandAMsi viyanti na dvAbhyAM.
     tAH Sho.lasha gAyatryo bhavanty
|p11  evam u hAsyAnuShTubbhir eva pratipadyamAnasya gAyatryo 'nushastA bhavanty
|p12  agna indrash ca dAshuSho duroNa ity AgnendryA yajati
|p13  na vA etAv #indrAgnI santau vyajayetAm,
     Agnendrau vA etau santau vyajayetAM.
     tad yad AgnendryA yajati, vijityA eva
|p14  sA virAT trayastriMsadakShara bhavati. trayastriMshad vai devA:
     aShTau #vasava, ekAdasha #rudrA, dvAdashAdityAH, #prajApatish ca #vaShaTkArash ca.
     tat prathama ukthamukhe devatA akSharabhAjaH karoty,
     akSharam-akSharam eva tad devatA anuprapibanti,
     devapAtreNaiva tad devatAs tR^ipyanti
|p15  tad Ahur: yathA vAva shastram evaM yAjyAgneyaM hotAjyaM shaMsaty,
     atha kasmAd AgnendryA yajatIti
|p16  yA vA Agnendry aindrAgnI vai sA,
     sendrAgnam etad ukthaM graheNa ca tUShNIMshaMsena ce/ndrAgnI
|p17  A gataM sutaM gIrbhir nabho vareNyam \
     asya pAtaM dhiyeShitety aindrAgnam adhvaryur grAhaM gR^ihNAti,
     bhUr #agnir jyotir jyotir #agnir #indro jyotir bhuvo jyotir #indraH #sUryo
     jyotir jyotiH svaH #sUrya iti hotA tUShNIMshaMsaM shaMsati:
     tad yathaiva shastram evaM yAjyA

|c38
|p1  HotR^ijapaM japati, retas tat si~Ncaty
|p2  upAMshu japaty, upAMshv iva vai retasaH siktiH
|p3  purAhAvAj japati. yad vai kimcordhvam AhAvAc, chastrasyaiva tat
|p4  parA~NcaM catuShpady AsInam abhyAhvayate,
     tasmAt parA~Nco bhUtvA catuShpAdo retaH si~Ncanti
|p5  samya.N dvipAd bhavati, tasmAt samya~Nco bhUtvA dvipAdo retaH si~Ncanti
|p6  pitA #mAtarishvety Aha.
     prANo vai pitA prANo #mAtarishvA prANo reto, retas tat si~Ncaty
|p7  achidrA padA dhA iti. reto vA achidram, Ato hy achidraH sambhavaty
|p8  achidrokthA kavayaH shaMsann iti. ye vA anUcAnAs te kavayas,
     ta idam achidraM retaH prajanayann ity eva tad Aha
|p9  somo vishvavin nIthAni neShad bR^ihaspatir ukthAmadAni shaMsiShad iti.
     brahma vai #bR^ihaspatiH, kShatraM #somaH,
     stutashastrANi nIthAni cokthamadAni ca.
     daivena caivaitad brahmaNA prasUto daivena ca kShatreNokthAni shaMsaty
|p10  etau ha vA asya sarvasya prasavasyeshAte yad idaM kiMca
|p11  tad yad etAbhyAm aprasUtaH karoty, akR^itaM tad.
     akR^itam akar iti vai nindanti
|p12  kR^itam asya kR^itam bhavati, nAsyAkR^itaM kR^itam bhavati ya evaM veda
|p13  vAg Ayur vishvAyur vishvam Ayur ity Aha.
     prANo vA AyuH, prANo reto, vAg yonir; yoniM tad upasaMdhAya retaH si~Ncati
|p14  ka idaM shaMsiShyati saidaM shaMsiShyatIty Aha.
     #prajApatir vai kaH, #prajApatiH prajanayiShyatIty eva tad Aha

|c39
|p1  AhUya tUShNIMshaMsaM shaMsati, retas tat siktam vikaroti.
     siktir vA  agre 'tha vikR^itir
|p2  upAMshu tUShNIMshaMsaM shaMsaty, upAMshv iva vai retasaH siktis
|p3  tira iva tUShNIMshaMsaM shaMsati, tira iva vai retAMsi vikriyante
|p4  ShaTpadaM tUShNIMshaMsaM shaMsati. ShaDvidho vai puruShaH Sha.la.Nga,
     AtmAnam eva tat ShaDvidhaM Sha.la.NgaM vikaroti
|p5  tuShNIMshaMsaM shastvA purorucaM shaMsati, retas tad vikR^itam prajanayati.
     vikR^itir vA agre 'tha jAtir
|p6  uccaiH purorucaM shaMsaty, uccair evainaM tat prajanayati
|p7  dvAdashapadAm purorucAM shaMsati.
     dvAdasha vai mAsAH saMvatsaraH, saMvatsaraH #prajApatiH,
     so 'sya sarvasya prajanayitA.
     sa yo 'sya sarvasya prajanayitA,
     sa evainaM tat prajayA pashubhiH prajanayati prajAtyai
|p8  prajAyate prajayA pashubhir ya evaM veda
|p9  jAtavedasyAm purorucaM shaMsati jAtavedonya.NgAM
|p10  tad Ahur: yat tR^itIyasavanam eva jAtavedasa Ayatanam,
     atha kasmAt prAtaHsavane jAtavedasyAm purorucaM shaMsatIti
|p11  prANo vai jAtavedAH, sa hi jAtAnAM veda.
     yAvatAM vai sa jAtAnAM veda te bhavanthi,
     yeShAm u na veda kim u te syur.
     yo vA Ajya AtmasaMskR^itiM veda, tat suviditam

|c40
|p1  pra vo devAyAgnaya iti shaMsati. prANo vai pra,
     prANaM hImAni sarvANi bhUtAny anuprayanti.
     prANam eva tat sambhAvayati, praNaM saMskurute
|p2  dIdivaMsam apUrvyam iti shaMsati.
     mano vai dIdAya, manAso hi na kiM cana pUrvam asti.
     mana eva tat sambhAvayati, manaH saMskurute
|p3  sa naH sharmANi vItaya iti shaMsati.
     vAg vai sharma, tasmAd vAcAnuvadantam Aha:
     sharmavad AsmA ayAMsIti.
     vAcam eva tat sambhAvayati, vAcaM saMskuruta
|p4  uta no brahmann aviSha iti shaMsati.
     shrotraM vai brahma, shrotreNo hi brahma shR^iNoti,
     shrotre brahma pratiShThitaM.
     shrotram eva tat sambhAvayati,
     shrotraM saMskurute
|p5  sa yantA vipra eShAm iti shaMsaty.
     apAno vai yantApAnena hy ayaM yataH prANo na parA.N bhavaty.
     apAnam eva tat sambhAvayaty, apAnaM saMskuruta
|p6  R^itAvA yasya rodasI iti shaMsati.
     cakShur vA R^itaM.
     tasmAd yataro vivadamAnayor AhAham anusThyA cakShuShAdarsham iti,
     tasya shrad dadhati.
     cakShur eva tat sambhAvayati, cakShuH saMskurute
|p7  nU no rAsva sahasravat tokavat puShTimad vasv ity uttamayA paridadhAty.
     AtmA vai samastaH sahasravAMs tokavAn puShTimAn.
     AtmAnam eva tat samastaM sambhAvayaty, AtmAnaM samastaM saMskurute
|p8  yAjyayA yajati. prattir vai yAjyA, puNyaiva lakShmIH.
     puNyAm eva tal lakShmIM sambhAvayati, puNyAM lakShmIM saMskurute
|p9  sa evaM vidvAMsh chandomayo devatAmayo brahmamayo 'mR^itamayaH
     sambhUya devatA apyeti ya evaM veda
|p10  yo vai tad veda yathA chandomayo devatAmayo brahmamayo 'mR^itamayaH
     sambhUyo devatA apyeti, tat suviditam
|p11  ity adhyAtmam, athAdhidaivatam

|c41
|p1  ShaTpadaM tUShNIMshaMsaM shaMsati. ShaD vA R^itava.
     R^itUn eva tat kalpayaty, R^itUn apyeti
|p2  dvAdashapadAm purorucaM shaMsAti. dvAdasha vai mAsA.
     mAsAn eva tAt kalpayati, mAsAn apyeti
|p3  pra vo devAyAgnaya iti shaMsaty.
     antarikShaM vai prAntarikShaM hImAni sarvANi bhUtAny anuprayanty.
     antarikSham eva tat kalpayaty, antarikSham apyeti
|p4  dIdivAMsam apUrvyam iti shaMsaty.
     asau vai dIdaya yo 'sau tapaty, etasmAd dhi na kiM cana pUrvam asty.
     etam eva tat kalpayaty, etam apyeti
|p5  sa naH sharmANi vItaya iti shaMsaty.
     #agnir vai sharmAny annAdyAni yachaty.
     #agnim eva tat kalpayaty, #agnim apyety
|p6  u ta no brahmann aviSha iti shaMsati. candramA vai brahma.
     candramasam eva tat kalpayati, candramasam apyeti
|p7  sa yantA vipra eShAm iti shaMsati.
     #vAyur vai yantA, #vAyunA hIdaM yatam antarikShaM na samR^ichati.
     #vAyum eva tat kalpayati, #vAyum apyety
|p8  R^itAvA yasya rodasI iti shaMsati. dyAvApR^ithivI vai rodasI.
     dyAvApR^ithivI eva tat kalpayati, dyAvApR^ithivI apyeti
|p9  nU no rAsvo sahasravat tokavat puShTimad vasv ity uttamayA paridadhAti.
     saMvatsaro vai samastaH sahasravAMs tokavAn puShTimAn.
     saMvatsaram eva tat samastaM kalpayati, saMvatsaraM samastam apyeti
|p10  yAjyayA yajati. vR^iShTir vai yAjyA vidyud eva,
     vidyud dhIdaM vR^iShTim annAdyaM samprayachati.
     vidyutam eva tat kalpayati, vidyutam apyeti
|p11  sa evaM vidvAn etanmayo devatAmayo bhavati bhavati

|bAB3 {pa~NcikA 3}

|c1 {adhyAya 11, khaNDaH 1-11}
|p1  grahokthaM vA etad yat pra:ugaM.
     nava prAtar grahA gR^ihyante, navabhir bahiShpavamAne stuvate.
     stute stome dashamaM gR^ihNAti, hiMkAra itarAsAM dashamaH. so sA sammA
|p2  vAyavyaM shaMsati, tena vAyavya ukthavAn
|p3  aindravAyavaM shaMsati, tenaindravAyava ukthavAn
|p4  maitrAvaruNaM shaMsati, tena maitrAvaruNa ukthavAn
|p5  AshvinaM shaMsati, tenAshvina ukthavAn
|p6  aindraM shaMsAti, tena shukrAmanthinA ukthavantau
|p7  vaishvadevaM shaMsati, tenAgrayaNa ukthavAn
|p8  sArasvataM shaMsati
|p9  na sArasvato graho 'sti
|p10  vAk tu #sarasvatI. ye tu keca vAcA grahA gR^ihyante, te 'sya sarve shastokthA
|p11  ukthino bhavanti ya evaM veda

|c2
|p1  annAdyaM vA etenAvarunddhe yat pra:ugAm.
     anyAnyA devatA pra:uge shasyate, 'nyad-anyad uktham pra:uge kriyate
|p2  'nyad-anyad asyAnnAdyaM graheShu dhriyate ya evaM vedai/tad
|p3  dha vai yajamAnasyAdhyAtmatamam ivokthaM yat pra:ugaM.
     tasmAd enainaitad upekShyatamam ivety Ahur,
     etena hy enaM hotA saMskarotIti
|p4  vAyavyaM shaMsAti. tasmAd Ahur.
     #vAyuH prANaH prANo reto,
     retaH puruShasya prathamaM sambhavataH sambhavatIti.
     yad vAyavyaM shaMsati, prANam evAsya tat saMskaroty
|p5  aindravAyavaM shaMsati. yatra vAva prANas tad apAno.
     yad aindravAyavaM shaMsAti, prANApAnAv evAsya tat saMskaroti
|p6  maitrAvaruNaM shaMsAti. tasmAd Ahush:
     cakShuH puruShasya prathamaM sambhavataH sambhavatIti.
     yan maitrAvaruNaM shaMsati, cakShur evAsya tat saMskaroty
|p7  AshvinaM shaMsati. tasmAt kumAraM jAtaM saMvadanta:
     upa vai shushrUShate, ni vai dhyAyatIti.
     yad AshvinaM shaMsati, shrotrAm evAsya tat saMskaroty
|p8  aindraM shaMsati. tasmAt kumAraM jAtaM saMvadante:
     pratidhArayati vai grIvA atho shira iti.
     yad aindraM shaMsati, vIryam evAsya tat saMskaroti
|p9  vaishvadevaM shaMsati.
     tasmAt kumAro jAtaH pashceva pracarati, vaishvadevAni hy a.NgAni.
     yad vaishvadevaM shaMsaty, a.NgAny evAsya tat saMskaroti
|p10  sArasvataM shaMsati.
     tasmAt kumAraM jAtaM jaghanyA vAg Avishati, vAg ghi #sarasvatI.
     yat sArasvataM shaMsati, vAcam evAsya tat saMskaroty
|p11  eSha vai jAto jAyate sarvAbhya etAbhyo devatAbhyaH sarvebhya ukthebhyaH
     sarvebhyash chandobhyaH sarvebhyaH pra:ugebhyaH
     sarvebhyaH savanebhyo ya evaM veda yasya caivaM viduSha etac chaMsanti

|c3
|p1  prANAnAM vA etad ukthaM yat pra:ugaM. sapta devatAH shaMsati.
     sapta vai shIrShau prANAH, shIrShann eva tat prANAn dadhAti
|p2  kiM sa yajamAnasya pApabhadram Adriyeteti ha smAha yo 'sya hotA syAd ity.
     atraivainaM yathA kAmayeta tathA kuryAd
|p3  yaM kAmayeta: prANenainaM vyardhayAnIti, vAyavyam asya lubdhaM shaMsed.
     R^icaM vA padaM vAtIyAt, tenaiva tal lubdham. praNenaivainaM tad vyardhayati
|p4  yam kAmayeta: prAnApAnAbhyAm enaM vyardhayAnIty,
     aindravAyavam asya lubdhaM shaMsed.
     R^icaM vA padaM vAtIyAt, tenaiva tal lubdham.
     prANApAnAbhyAm evainaM tad vyardhayati
|p5  yaM kAmayeta:
     cakShuShainaM vyardhAyanIti, maitrAvaruNam asya lubdhaM shaMsed.
     R^icam vA padaM vAtIyAt, tenaiva tal lubdhaM.
     cakShuShaivainam tad vyardhayati
|p6  yaM kAmayeta: shrotreNainaM vyardhayAnIty,
     Ashvinam asya lubdhaM shaMsed. R^icaM vA padaM vatIyAt, tenaiva tal lubdhaM.
     shrotreNaivainaM tad vyardhayati
|p7  yaM kAmayeta: vIryeNainaM vyardhayAnIty, aindram asya lubdhaM shaMsed.
     R^icaM vA padaM vAtIyAt, tenaiva tal lubdhaM.
     vIryenaivainAM tad vyardhayati
|p8  yaM kAmayetA.Ngair enaM vyardhayAnIti, vaishvadevam asya lubdhaM shaMsed.
     R^icaM vA padaM vAtIyAt, tenaiva tal lubdham.
     a.Ngair evainaM tad vyardhayati
|p9  yaM kAmayeta: vAcainaM vyardhayAnIti, sArasvatam asya lubdhaM shaMsed.
     R^icaM vA padaM vAtIyAt, tenaiva tal lubdhaM. vAcaivainaM tad vyardhayati
|p10  yam u kAmayeta: sarvair enam a.NgaiH sarveNAtmanA samardhayAnIty,
     etad evAsya yathApUrvam R^iju k.lptaM shaMset.
     sarvair evainaM tad a.NgaiH sarveNAtmanA samardhayati
|p11  sarvair a.NgaiH sarveNAtmanA samR^idhyate ya evaM veda

|c4
|p1  tad Ahur: yathA vAva stotram evaM shastram.
     AgneyIShu sAmagAH stuvate, vAyavyayA hotA pratipadyate:
     katham asya Agneyyo 'nushastA bhavantIty
|p2  #agner vA etAH sarvAs tanvo yad etA devatAH
|p3  sa yad #agniH pravAn iva dahati, tad asya vAyavyaM rUpaM.
     tad asya tenAnushaMsaty
|p4  atha yad dvaidham iva kR^itvA dahati, dvau vA #indravAyu,
     tad asyaindravAyavaM rupAM. tad asya tenAnushaMsaty
|p5  atha yad uc ca hR^iShyati ni ca hR^iShyati, tad asya maitrAvaruNaM rUpaM.
     tad asya tenAnushaMsati
|p6  sa yad #agnir ghorasaMsparshas tad asya vAruNaM rUpaM,
     taM yad ghorasaMsparshaM santam mitrakR^ityevopAsate tad asya maitraM rUpaM.
     tad asya tenAnushaMsaty
|p7  atha yad enaM dvAbhyAm bAhubhyAM dvAbhyAm araNIbhyAm manthanti,
     dvau vA #ashvinau, tad asyAshvinaM rUpaM. tad asya tenAnushaMsaty
|p8  atha yad uccairghoShaH stanayan bababAkurvann iva dahati
     yasmAd bhUtAni vijante, tad asyaindraM rUpaM. tad asya tenAnushaMsaty
|p9  atha yad enam ekaM santam bahudhA viharanti, tad asya vaishvadevaM rUpaM.
     tad asya tenAnushaMsaty
|p10  atha yat sphUrjayan vAcam iva vadan dahati, tad asya sArasvataM rUpaM.
     tad asya tenAnushaMsaty
|p11  evam u hAsya vAyavyayaiva pratipadyamAnasya tR^icena-tR^icenaivaitAbhir
     devatAbhiH stotriyo 'nushasto bhavati
|p12  vishvebhiH somyam madhv agna indreNa vAyunA \
     pibA mitrasya dhAmabhir iti vaishvadevam ukthaM shastvA vaishvadevyA,
     yajati, yathAbhAgaM tad devatAH prINAti

|c5
|p1  devapAtraM vA etad yad vaShaTkAro. vaShaTkaroti,
     devapAtreNaiva tad devatAs tarpayaty
|p2  anuvaShaTkaroti. tad yathAdo 'shvAn vA gA vA punarabhyAkAraM tarpayanty,
     evam evaitad devatAH punarabhyAkAraM tarpayanti yad anuvaShaTkarotI/mAn
|p3  evAgnIn upAsata ity Ahur dhiShNyAn,
     atha kasmAt pUrvasminn eva juhvati pUrvasmin vaShaTkurvantIti
|p4  yad eva somasyAgne vIhIty anuvaShaTkaroti, tena dhiShNyAn prINAty
|p5  asaMsthitAn somAn bhakShayantIty Ahur yeShAM nAnuvaShaTkaroti,
     ko nu somasya sviShTakR^idbhAga iti
|p6  yad vAva somasyAgne vIhIty anuvaShaTkaroti,
     tena iva saMsthitAn somAn bhakShayanti;
     sa u eva somasya sviShTakR^idbhAgo. vaShaTkaroti

|c6
|p1  vajro vA eSha yad vaShaTkAro.
     yaM dviShyAt taM dhyAyed vaShaTkariShyaMs,
     tasminn eva taM vajram AsthApayati
|p2  Sha.l iti vaShaTkaroti. ShaD vA R^itava.
     R^itUn eva tat kalpayaty, R^itUn pratiShThApayaty.
     R^itUn vai pratitiShThata idaM sarvam anupratitiShThati yad idaM kiMca
|p3  pratitiShThati ya evaM veda
|p4  tad u ha smAha #hiraNyadan #baida:
     etAni vA etena ShaT pratiShThApayati.
     dyaur antarikShe pratiShThitAntarikSham pR^ithivyAm pR^ithivy apsv ApaH
     satye satyam brahmaNi brahma tapasIty.
     etA eva tat pratiShThAH pratitiShThantIr
     idaM sarvam anupratitiShThati yad idaM kiMca.
     pratitiShThati ya evaM veda
|p5  vauSha.l iti vaShaTkaroty. asau vAva vAv, R^itavaH Sha.l.
     etam eva tad R^ituShv AdadhAty, R^ituShu pratiShThApayati.
     yAdR^ig iva vai devebhyaH karoti, tAdR^ig ivAsmai devAH kurvanti

|c7
|p1  trayo vai vaShaTkArA: vajro dhAmachad riktah
|p2  sa yam evoccair bali vaShaTkaroti sa vajras
|p3  taM-tam praharati dviShate bhrAtR^ivyAya vadhaM,
     yo 'sya stR^ityas tasmai startavai.
     tasmAt sa bhrAtR^ivyavatA vaShaTkR^ityo
|p4  'tha yaH samaH saMtato &6 'nirhANarcaH sa dhAmachat

     tasmAt sa prajAkAmena pashukAmena vaShaTkR^ityo
|p6  'tha yenaiva Sha.l avarAdhnoti sa rikto

     pApIyAn vaShaTkartA bhavati pApIyAn yasmai vaShaTkaroti.
     tasmAt tasyAshAM neyAt
|p8  kiM sa yajamAnasya pApabhadram Adriyeteti ha smAha yo 'sya hotA syAd ity.
     atraivainaM yathA kAmayeta tathA kuryAd
|p9  yaM kAmayeta: yathaivAnIjAno 'bhUt tathaivejAnaH syAd iti,
     yathaivAsya R^icam brUyAt tathaivAsya vaShaTkuryAt.
     sadR^isham evainaM tat karoti
|p10  yaM kAmayeta: pApIyAn syAd ity,
     uccaistarAm asya R^icam uktvA shanaistarAM vaShaTkuryAt.
     pApIyAMsam evainaM tat karoti
|p11  yaM kAmayeta:
     shreyAn syAd iti, shanaistarAm asya R^icam uktvoccaistarAM vaShaTkuryAc.
     chriya evainaM tac chriyAm AdadhAti
|p12  saMtatam R^icA vaShaTkR^ityaM, saMtatyai
|p13  saMdhIyate prajayA pashubhir ya evaM veda

|c8
|p1  yasyai devatAyai havir gR^ihItaM syAt, tAM dhyAyed vaShaTkariShyan.
     sAkShAd eva tad devatAm prINAti, pratyakShAd devAtAM yajati
|p2  vajro vai vaShaTkAraH, sa eSha prahR^ito 'shAnto dIdAya.
     tasya haitasya na sarva iva shAntiM veda na pratiShThAM.
     tasmAd dhApy etarhi bhUyAn iva mR^ityus.
     tasya haiShaiva shAntir eShA pratiShThA vAg ity eva.
     tasmAd vaShaTkR^itya-vaShaTkR^itya vAg ity anumantrayeta,
     sa enaM shAnto na hinasti
|p3  vaShaTkAra mA &2 mA<m> pramR^ikSho mAhaM tvAm pramR^ikSham,
     bR^ihatA mana upahvaye vyAnena sharIram,
     pratiShThAsi pratiShThAM gacha
     pratiShThAm mA gamayeti vaShaTkAram anumantrayeta
|p4  tad u ha smAha: dIrgham etat sad aprabhv, ojaH saha oja
|p5  ity eva vaShaTkAram anumantrayetau/jash
|p6  ca ha vai sahash ca vaShaTkArasya priyatame tanvau
|p7  priyeNaivainaM tad dhAmnA samardhayati
|p8  priyeNa dhAmnA samR^idhyate ya evaM veda
|p9  vAk ca vai prANApAnau ca vaShaTkAras,
     ta ete vaShaTkR^ite-vaShaTkR^ite vyutkrAmanti. tAn anumantrayeta:
     vAg ojaH saha ojo mAyi prANApAnAv ity,
     Atmany eva tad dhotA vAcaM ca prANApAnau ca pratiShThApayati
     sarvAyuH sarvAyutvAya
|p10  sarvam Ayur eti ya evaM veda

|c9
|p1  yaj~No vai devebhya udakrAmat, tam praiShaiH praiSham aichan.
     yat praiShaiH praiSham aichaMs, tat praiShANAm praiShatvaM
|p2  tam purorugbhiH prArocayan.
     yat purorugbhiH prArocayaMs, tat purorucAm puroruktvaM
|p3  taM vedyAm anvavindan. yad vedyAm anvavindaMs, tad veder veditvaM

     yad vittaM grahair vyagR^ihNata, tad grahANAM grahatvaM

     tan nividAM nivittvam

|c10
|p1  garbhA vA eta ukthAnAM yan nividas.
     tad yat purastAd ukthAnAm prAtaHsavane dhIyante,
     tasmAt parA~Nco garbhA dhIyante parA~NcaH sambhavanti
|p2  yan madhyato madhyaMdine dhIyante, tasmAn madhye garbhA dhR^itA
|p3  yad antatas tR^itIyasavane dhIyante,
     tasmAd amuto 'rvA~Nco garbhAH prajAyante prajAtyai
|p4  prajAyate prajayA pashubhir ya evaM veda
|p5  peshA vA eta ukthAnAM yan nividas.
     tad yat purastAd ukthAnAm prAtaHsavane dhIyante,
     yathaiva pravayaNataH peshaH kuryAt tAdR^ik tad.
     yan madhyato madhyaMdine dhIyante,
     yathaiva madhyataH peshaH kuryAt tAdR^ik tad.
     yad antatas tR^itIyasavane dhIyante,
     yathaivAvaprajjanataH peshaH kuryAt tAdR^ik tat

|c11
|p  1 sauryA vA etA devatA yan nividas.
     tad yat purastAd ukthAnAm prAtaHsavane dhIyante
     madhyato madhyaMdine 'ntatas tR^itIyasavana,
     Adityasyaiva tad vratam anuparyAvartante
|p2  paccho vai devA yaj~NaM samabharaMs, tasmAt paccho nividaH shasyante
|p3  yad vai tad devA yaj~NaM samabharaMs, tasmAd ashvaH samabhavat.
     tasmAd Ahur: ashvaM nividAM shaMstre dadyAd iti,
     tad u khalu varam eva dadati
|p4  na nividaH padam atIyAd
|p5  yan nividaH padam atIyAd, yaj~Nasya tac chidraM kuryAd,
     yaj~Nasya vai chidraM sravad yajamAno 'nu pApIyAn bhavati.
     tasmAn na nividaH padam atIyAn
|p6  na nividaH pade viparihared.
     yan nividaH pade vipariharen, mohayed yaj~Nam, mugdho yajamAnaH syAt.
     tasmAn na nividaH pade vipariharen
|p7  na nividaH pade samasyed.
     yan nividaH pade samasyed, yaj~Nasya tad AyuH sAMhAret,

     tasmAn na nividaH pade samasyet
|p8  predam brahma predaM kShatram ity ete eva samasyed,
     brahmakShatrayoH saMshrityai.
     tasmAd brahma ca kShatraM ca saMshrite
|p9  na tR^icaM na caturR^icam ati manyeta nividdhAnam,
     ekaikaM vai nividaH pAdam R^icaM sUktam prati.
     tasmAn na tR^icaM na caturR^icam ati manyeta nividdhAnaM,
     nividA hy eva stotram atshastam bhavaty
|p10  ekAm parishiShya tR^itIyasavane nividaM dadhyAd
|p11  yad dve parishiShya dadhyAt, prajananaM tad upahanyAd,
     garbhais tat prajA vyardhayet.
     tasmAd ekAm eva parishiShya tR^itIyasavane nividaM dadhyAn
|p12  na sUktena nividam atipadyeta
|p13  yena sUktena nividam atipadyeta,
     na tat punar upanivarteta, vAstuham eva tad
|p14  anyat taddaivataM tacchandasaM sUktam AhR^itya tasmin nividaM dadhyAn
|p15  mA pra gAma patho vayam iti purastAt sUktasya shaMsati
|p16  patho vA eSha praiti yo yaj~Ne muhyati.
     mA yaj~NAd indra somina iti, yaj~NAd eva tan na pracyavate
|p17  mAnta sthur no arAtaya ity, arAtIyata eva tad apahanti

|c12 {adhyAya 12, khaNDaH 1-13}
|p1  devavishaH kalpayitavyA, ity Ahush, chandash chandasi pratiShThApyam iti.
     shoMsAvom ity Ahvayate prAtaHsavane tryakShareNa,
     shaMsAmodaivom ity adhvaryuH pratigR^iNAti pa~NcAkShareNa.
     tad aShTAkSharaM sampadyate. 'ShTAkSharA vai gAyatrI,
     gAyatrIm eva tat purastAt prAtaHsavane 'cIk.lpatAm
|p2  ukthaM vAcIty Aha shastvA caturakSharam,
     om ukthashA ity adhvaryush caturakSharaM.
     tad aShThAkSharaM sampadyate. 'ShTAkSharA vai gAyatrI,
     gAyatrIm eva tad ubhayataH prAtaHsavane 'cIk.lpatAm
|p3  adhvaryo shoMsAvom ity Ahvayate madhyaMdine Sha.lakShareNa,
     shaMsAmodaivom ity adhvaryuH pratigR^iNAti pa~NcAkShareNa.
     tad ekAdashAkSharaM sampadyata.
     ekAdashAkSharA vai triShTup,
     triShTubham eva tat purastAn madhyaMdine 'cIk.lpatAm.
     ukthaM vAcIndrAyety Aha shastvA saptAkSharam,
     om ukthashA ity adhvaryush caturakSharaM.
     tad ekAdashAkSharaM sampadyata.
     ekAdashAkSharA vai triShTup,
     triShTubham eva tad ubhayato madhyaMdine 'cIk.lpatAm
|p4  adhvaryo shoshoMsAvom ity Ahvayate tR^itIyasavane saptAkShareNa,
     shaMsAmodaivom ity adhvaryuH pratigR^iNAti pa~NcAkShareNa.
     tad dvAdashAkSharaM sampadyate.
     dvAdashAkShAra vai jagatI,
     jagatim eva tat purastAt tR^itIyasavane 'cIk.lpatAm.
     ukthaM vAcIndrAya devebhya ity Aha shastvaikAdashAkSharam,
     om ity adhvaryur ekAkSharaM.
     tad dvAdashAkSharaM sampadyate.
     dvAdashAkShara vai jagatI,
     jagatIm eva tad ubhayatas tR^itIyasavane 'cIk.lpatAM
|p5  tad etad R^iShiH pashyann abhyanUvAca
|p6  yad gAyatre adhi gAyatram AhitaM traiShTubhAd vA traiShTubhaM niratakShata
     \ yad vA jagaj jagaty Ahitam padaM ya it tad vidus te amR^itatvam Anashur ity
|p7  etad vai tac chandash chandasi pratiShThApayati
|p8  kalpayati devavisho ya evaM veda

|c13
|p1  #prajApatir vai yaj~NaM chandAMsi devebhyo bhAgadheyAni vyabhajat.
     sa gAyatrIm evAgnaye #vasubhyaH prAtaHsavane 'bhajat,
     triShTubham #indrAya #rudrebhyo madhyaMdine,
     jagatIM #vishvebhyo devebhya Adityebhyas tR^itIyasavane
|p2  'thAsya yat svaM chanda AsId anuShTup,

     yAm modantam abhy udauhIr achAvAkIyAm abhiti.
     tad ajAnAt, sa svaM somam Aharat,
     sa sve some 'gram mukham abhi paryAharad anuShTubhaM.

|c14
|p1  #agnir vai devAnAM hotAsIt, tam mR^ityur bahiShpavamAne 'sIdat.
     so 'nuShTubhAjyam pratyapadyata, mR^ityum eva tat paryakrAmat.
     tam Ajye 'sIdat. sa pra:ugeNa pratyapadyata, mR^ityum eva tat paryakrAmat
|p2  tam mAdhyaMdine pavamAne 'sIdat.
     so 'nuShTubhA marutvatIyam pratyapadyata, mR^ityum eva tat paryakrAmat.
     tam mAdhyaMdine bR^ihatIShu nAshaknot sattum.
     prANA vai bR^ihatyaH, prANAn eva tan nAshaknod vyavaituM.
     tasmAn mAdhyaMdine hotA bR^ihatIShu stotriyeNaiva pratipadyate.
     prANA vai bR^ihatyaH, prANAn eva tad abhi pratipadyate
|p3  taM tR^itIyapavamAne 'sIdat.
     so 'nuShTubhA vaishvadevam pratyapadyata, mR^ityum eva tat paryakrAmat.
     taM yaj~NAyaj~NIye 'sIdat.
     sa vaishvAnarIyeNAgnimArutam pratyapadyata, mR^ityum eva tat paryakrAmad.
     vajro vai vaishvAnarIyam pratiShThA yaj~NAyaj~NIyaM,
     vajreNaiva tat pratiShThAyA mR^ityuM nudate.
     sa sarvAn pAshAn sarvAn sthANUn mR^ityor atimucya svasty evodamucyata,
     svasty eva hotonmucyate sarvAyuH sarvAyutvAya
|p4  sarvam Ayur eti ya evaM veda

|c15
|p1  #indro vai #vR^itraM hatvA nAstR^iShIti manyamAnaH parAH parAvato 'gachat,
     sa paramAm eva parAvatam agachad.
     anuShTub vai paramA parAvad, vAg vA anuShTup.

|c15

|c17
|p1  brAhmaNaspatyam pragAthaM shaMsati
|p2  bR^ihaspatipurohitA vai devA ajayan svargaM lokaM, vy asmi~Ml loke 'jayanta.
     tathaivaitad yajamAno bR^ihaspatipurohita eva jayati svargaM lokaM,
     vy asmi~Ml loke jayate
|p3  tau vA etau pragAthAv astutau santau punarAdAyaM shasyete. tad Ahur:
     yan na kiM canAstutaM sat punarAdAyaM shasyate,
     'tha kasmAd etau pragAthAv astutau santau punarAdAyaM shasyete iti
|p4  pavamAnokthaM vA etad yan marutvatIyaM.
     ShaTsu vA atra gAyatrIShu stuvate ShaTsu bR^ibatIShu tisR^iShu triShTupsu,
     sa vA eSha trichandAH pa~Ncadasho mAdhyaMdinaH pavamAnas.
     tad AhuH: kathaM ta eSha trichandAH pa~Ncadasho
     mAdhyaMdinaH pavamAno 'nushAsto bhavatIti
|p5  ye eva gAyatryA uttare pratipado yo gAyatro 'nucaras,

     etAbhyAm evAsya pragAthAbhyAm bR^ihatyo 'nushastA bhavanti

|p7  ye eva triShTubhau dhAyye yat traiShTubhaM nividdhAnam,

|c18
|p1  dhAyyAH shaMsati
|p2  dhAyyAbhir vai #prajApatir imA~Ml lokAn adhayad yaM-yaM kAmam akAmayata

     kAmayate ya evaM veda yad eva dhAyyA+H \
|p4  yatra-yatra vai devA yaj~Nasya chidraM nirajAnaMs,
     tad dhAyyAbhir apidadhus, tad dhAyyAnAM dhAyyAtvam
|p5  achidreNa hAsya yaj~NeneShTam bhavati ya evaM veda yad v eva dhAyyA+H \
|p6  syUma haitad yaj~Nasya yad dhAyyAs.
     tad yathA sUcyA vAsaH saMdadhad iyAd,
     evam evaitAbhir yaj~Nasya chidraM saMdadhad
     eti ya evaM veda yad v eva dhAyyA+H \
|p7  tAny u vA etAny upasadAm evokthAni yad dhAyyA.
     agnir netety AgneyI prathamopasat, tasyA etad ukthaM.
     tvaM soma kratubhir iti saumyA dvitIyopasat, tasyA etad uktham.
     pinvanty apa iti vaiShNavI tR^itIyopasat, tasyA etad ukthaM
|p8  yAvantaM ha vai saumyenAdhvareNeShTvA lokaM jayati,
     tam ata ekaikayopasadA jayati
     ya evaM veda yash caivaM vidvAn dhAyyAH shaMsati
|p9  tad dhaika Ahus: tAn vo maha iti shaMsed, etAM vAva vayam #bharateShu
     shasyamAnAm abhivyajAnIma iti vadantas
|p10  tat-tan nAdR^ityaM
|p11  yad etAM shaMsed, IshvaraH parjanyo 'varShToH=(W)
|p12  pinvanty apa ity eva shaMsed
|p13  vR^iShTivani padam, #maruta iti mArutam,
     atyaM na mihe vi nayantIti vinItavad.
     yad vinItavat tad vikrAntavad, yad vikrAntavat tad vaiShNavaM.
     vAjinam itIndro vai vAjI. tasyAM vA etasyAM catvAri padAni:
     vR^iShTivani mArutaM vaiShNavam aindraM
|p14  sA vA eShA tR^itIyasavanabhAjanA satI madhyaMdine shasyate.
     tasmAd dhedam #bharatAnAm pashavaH
     sAyaMgoShThAH santo madhyaMdine saMgavinIm Ayanti.
     so jagatI, jAgatA hi pashava, AtmA yajamAnasya madhyaMdinas,
     tad yajamAne pashUn dadhAti

|c19
|p1  #marutvatIyam pragAthaM shansati. pasavo vai #marutaH,
     pashavaH pragAthaH, pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p2  janiShThA ugraH sahase turAyeti sUktam shaMsati.
     tad vA etad yajamAnajananam eva sUktaM,
     yajamAnaM ha vA etena yaj~NAd devayonyai prajanayati
|p3  tat saMjayam bhavati. saM ca jayati vi ca jayata
|p4  etad gaurivItaM.
     #gaurivItir ha vai #shAktyo nediShThaM svargasya lokasyAgachat,
     sa etat sUktam apashyat, tena svargaM lokam ajayat.
     tathaivaitad yajamAna etena sUktena svargaM lokaM jayati
|p5  tasyArdhAH shastvArdhAH parishiShya madhye nividaM dadhAti
|p6  svargasya haiSha lokasya roho yan nivit
|p7  svargasya haital lokasyAkramaNaM yan nivit.
     tAm AkramamANa iva shaMsed,
     upaiva yajamAnaM nigR^ihNIta yo 'sya priyaH syAd.
     iti nu svargakAmasyA/thAbhicarato.
|p8  yaH kAmayeta:
     kShatreNa vishaM hanyAm iti, tris tarhi nividA sUktaM vishaMset.
     kShatraM vai nivid viT sUktaM, kShatreNaiva tad vishaM hanti
|p9  yaH kAmayeta:
     vishA kShatraM hanyAm iti, tris tarhi sUkteua nividaM vishaMset.
     kShatraM vai nivid viT sUktAM, vishaiva tat kShatraM hanti
|p10  ya u kAmayetobhayata enaM vishaH paryavachinadAnIty,
     ubhayatas tarhi nividaM vyAhvayItobhayata
     evainaM tad vishaH paryavachinattI/ti
|p11  nv abhicarata, itarathA tv eva svargakAmasya
|p12  vayaH sinparNA upa sedur indram ity uttamayA paridadhAti
|p13  priyamedhA R^iShayo nAdhamAnAH \
|p14  apa dhvAntam UrNuhIti.
     yena tamasA prAvR^ito manyeta tan manasA gached, apa haivAsmAt tal lupyate
|p15  pUrdhi cakShur iti cakShuShI marImR^ijyetA/jarasaM
|p16  ha cakShuShmAn bhavati ya evAM veda
|p17  mumugdhy asmAn nidhayeva baddhAn iti.
     pAshA vai nidhA, mumugdhy asmAn pAshAd iva baddhAn ity eva tad Aha

|c20
|p1  #indro vai #vR^itraM haniShyan sarvA devatA abravId:
     anu mopatiShThadhvam, upa mA hvayadhvam iti. tatheti.
     taM haniShyanta Adravan. so 'ven:
     mAM vai haniShyanta Adravanti, hantemAn bhIShayA iti.
     tAn abhi prAshvasIt, tasya shvasathAd IShamANA vishve devA adravan.
     #maruto hainaM nAjahuH:
     prahara bhagavo jahi vIrayasvety evainam etAM vAcaM vadanta upAtiShThanta.
     tad etad R^iShiH pashyann abhyanUvAca:
     vR^itrasya tvA shvasathAd IShamANA vishve devA Ajahur ye sakhAyaH \
     marudbhir indra sakhyaM te astv athemA vishvAH pR^itanA jayAsIti.
     so 'ved: ime vai kila me sacivA, ime mAkAmayanta,
     hantemAn asminn uktha AbhajA iti.
     tAn etasminn uktha Abhajad,
     atha haite tarhy ubhe eva niShkevalye ukthe Asatur
|p2  marutvatIyaM grahaM gR^ihNAti, marutvatIyam pragAthaM shaMsati,
     marutvatIyaM sUktaM shaMsati, marutvatIyAm nividaM dadhAti:
     #marutAM sA bhaktir
|p3  marutvatIyam ukthaM shastvA marutvatIyayA yajati,
     yathAbhAgaM tad devatAH prINAti
|p4  ye tvAhihatye maghavann avardhan ye shAmbare harivo ye gaviShTau \
     ye tvA nUnam anumadanti viprAH pibendra somaM sagaNo marudbhir iti
|p5  yatra-yatraivaibhir vyajayata yatra-yatra vIryam akarot,
     tad evaitat samanuvedyendreNainAn sasomapIthAn karoti

|c21
|p1  #indro vai #vR^itraM hatvA sarvA vijitIr vijityAbravIt #prajApatim:
     aham etad asAni yat tvam, aham mahAn asAnIti.
     sa #prajApatir abravId: atha ko 'ham iti.
     yad evaitad avoca, ity abravIt. tato vai #ko nAma #prajApatir abhavat;
     #ko vai nAma #prajApatir.
     yan mahAn #indro 'bhavat, tan #mahendrasya mahendratvaM
|p2  sa mahAn bhUtvA devatA abravId:
     uddhAram ma uddharateti. yathApy etarhIchati,
     yo vai bhavati yaH shreShThatAm ashnute (sa mahAn bhavati).
     taM devA abruvan: svayam eva brUShva yat te bhaviShyatIti.
     sa etam mAhendraM graham abrUta, mAdhyaMdinaM savanAnAM,
     niShkevalyam ukthAnAM, triShTubhaM chandasAm, pR^iShThaM sAmnAM.
     tam asmA uddhAram udaharanu.
|p3  ud asmA uddhAraM haranti ya evaM veda
|p4  tAM devA abruvan:
     sarvaM vA avocathA, api no 'trAstv iti.
     sa nety abravIt, kathaM vo 'pisyAd iti.
     tam abruvann: apy eva no 'stu maghavann iti. tAn IkShataiva

|c22
|p1  te devA abruvann:
     iyaM vA #indrasya priyA jAvA vAvAtA #prAsahA nAmAsyAm evechAmahA iti.
     tatheti. tasyAm aichanta. sainAn abravIt:
     prAtar vaH prativaktAsmIti.
     tasmAt striyaH patyAv ichante, tasmAd u stry anurAtram patyAv ichate.
     tAm prAtar upAyan, saitad eva pratyapadyata:
|p2  yad vAvAna purutamam purAShA.l A vR^itrahendro nAmAny aprAH \
     aceti prAsahas patis tuviShmAn itI/ndro
|p3  vai prAsahas patis tuviShmAn
|p4  yadIm ushmAsi kartave karat tad iti.
     yad evaitad avocAmAkarat tad ity evainAMs tad abravIt

     apy asyA ihAstu, yA no 'smin na vai kam avidad iti. tatheti.
     tasyA apy atrAkurvaMs
|p6  tasmAd eShAtrApi shasyate: yad vAvAna purutamam purAShA.l iti
|p7  senA vA #indrasya priyA jAyA vAvAtA #prAsahA nAma,
     #ko nAma #prajApatiH shvashuras.
     tad yAsya kAme senA jayet,
     tasyA ardhAt tiShThaMs tR^iNam ubhayataH parichidyetarAM senAm abhy asyet:
     #prAsahe #kas tvA pashyatIti.
     tad yathaivAdaH snuShA shvashurA.l lajjamAnA nilIyamAnaity,
     evam eva sA senA bhajyamAnA nilIyamAnaiti yatraivaM vidvAMs
     tR^iNam ubhayataH parichidyetarAM senaM abhy asyati:
     #prAsahe #kas tvA pashyatIti
|p8  tAn #indra uvAcApi vo 'trAstv iti. te devA abruvan:
     virAD yAjyAstu niShkevalyasya yA trayastriMshadakSharA
|p9  trayastriMshad vai devA:
     aShTau #vasava, ekAdasha #rudrA, dvAdashAdityAH, #prajApatish ca #vaShaTkArash ca.
     devatA akSharabhAjaH karoty,
     akSharam-akSharam eva tad devatA anuprapibanti,
     devapAtreNaiva tad devatAs tR^ipyanti
|p10  yaM kAmayetAnAyatanavAn syAd ity,
     avirAjAsya yajed gAyatryA vA tR^iShTubhA vAnyena vA chandasA, vaShaTkuryAd:
     anAyatanavantam evainaM tat karoti
|p11  yaM kAmayetAyatanavAn syAd iti, virAjAsya yajet:
     pibA somam indra mandatu tvety etayAyatanavantam evainaM tat karoti

|c23
|p1  R^ik ca vA idam agre sAma cAstAM saiva nAma R^ig AsId amo nAma sAma.
     sA vA R^ik sAmopAvadan: mithunaM saMbhavAva prajAtyA iti.
     nety abravIt sAma, jyAyAn vA ato mama mahimeti.
     te dve bhUtvopAvadatAM, te na prati cana samavadata.
     tAs tisro bhUtvopAvadaMs, tat tisR^ibhiH samabhavad.
     yat tisR^ibhiH samabhavat tasmAt tisR^ibhiH stuvanti, tisR^ibhir udgAyanti;
     tisR^ibhir hi sAma sammitaM.
     tasmAd ekasya bahvyo jAyA bhavanti, naikasyai bahavaH patayo.
     yad vai tat sA cAmash ca samabhavatAM, tat sAmAbhavat, tat sAmnaH sAmatvaM
|p2  sAman bhavati ya evaM veda

     asAmanya iti hi nindanti
|p4  te vai pa~NcAnyad bhUtvA pa~NcAnyad bhUtvAkalpetAm:
     AhAvAsh ca hiMkArash ca prastAvash ca prathamA ca R^ig udgIthash ca,
     madhyamA ca pratihArash cottamA ca nidhanaM ca vaShaTkArash ca

|p6  yad u virAjaM dashinIm abhisamapadyetAM, tasmAd Ahur:
     virAji yaj~No dashinyAm pratiShThita ity

|c24
|p1  stotriyaM shaMsaty, AtmA vai stotriyas

|c25 {adhyAya 13, khaNDaH 1-14}
|p1  somo vai rAjAmuShmi~Ml loka AsIt, taM devAsh ca R^iShayash cAbhyAdhyAyan:
     katham ayam asmAn somo rAjAgached iti.
     te 'bruvaMsh chandAMsi: yUyaM na imaM somaM rAjAnam Aharateti. tatheti.
     te suparNA bhUtvodapataMs.
     te yat suparNA bhUtvodapataMs,
     tad etat #sauparNam ity AkhyAnavida AcakShate
|p2  chandAMsi vai tat somaM rAjAnam achAcaraMs.
     tAni ha tarhi caturakSharANi-caturakSharANy eva chandAMsy Asan.
     sA jagatI caturakSharA prathamodapatat.
     sA patitvArdham adhvano gatvAshrAmyat,
     sA parAsya trINy akSharANy ekAkSharA bhUtvA
     dIkShAM ca tapash ca harantI punar abhyavApatat.
     tasmAt tasya vittA dIkShA vittaM tapo yasya pashavaH santi.
     jAgatA hi pashavo, jagatI hi tAn Aharad
|p3  atha triShTub udapatat.
     sA patitvA bhUyo 'rdhAd adhvano gatvAshrAmyat,
=   sA parAsyaikam akSharaM tryakSharA bhUtvA dakShinA harantI punar abhyavApatat.
     tasmAn madhyaMdine dakShiNA nIyante triShTubho loke, triShTub bhi tA Aharat

|c26
|p1  te devA abruvan gAyatrIM.
     tvaM na imaM somaM rAjAnam Ahareti.
     sA tathety abravIt, tAM vai mA sarveNa svastyayanenAnumantrayadhvam iti.
     tatheti. sodapatat, tAM devAH sarveNa svastyayanenAnvamantrayanta:
     preti ceti cety. etad vai sarvaM svastyayanaM yat preti ceti ceti.
     tad yo 'sya priyaH syAt tam etenAnumantrayeta:
     preti ceti ceti, svasty eva gachati, svasti punar Agachati
|p2  sA patitvA somapAlAn bhIShayitvA padbhyAM ca mukhena ca somaM rAjAnaM
     samagR^ibhNAd, yAni cetare chandasI akSharANy ajahitAM tAni copasamagR^ibhNAt
|p3  tasyA anuvisR^ijya #kR^ishAnuH somapAlaH savyasya pado nakham achidat,
     tac chalyako 'bhavat, tasmAt sa nakham iva.
     yad vasham asravat sA vashAbhavat,
     tasmAt sA havir ivAtha yaH shalyo yad anIkam Asit sa sarpo nirdaMshy abhavat,

     so sA tatheShur abhavat

|c27
|p1  sA yad dakShiNena padA samagR^ibhNAt, tat prAtaHsavanam abhavat.

     tasmAt tat samR^iddhatamam manyante sarveShAM savanAnAm.

|c28
|p1  te vA ime itare chandasI gAyatrIm abhyavadetAM:
     vittaM nAv akSharANy anuparyAgur iti.
     nety abravId gAyatrI, yathAvittam eva na iti.
     te deveShu prashnam aitAM, te devA abruvan: yathAvittam eva va iti.
     tasmAd dhApy etarhi vittyAM vyAhur:
     yathAvittam eva na iti.
     tato vA aShTAkSharA gAyatry abhavat, tryakSharA triShTub,

|p2  sAShTAkSharA gAyatrI prAtaHsavanam udayachan,

|c29
|p1  te devA abruvann #AdityAn:
     yuShmAbhir idaM savanam udyachAmeti. tatheti.
     tasmAd AdityArambhaNaM tR^itIyasavanam, AdityagrahaH purastAt tasya

|p3  nAnuvAShaTkaroti, na bhakShayati.

     tvayedaM saha savanam udyachAmeti. tatheti.
     tasmAt sAvitrI pratipad bhavati vaishvadevasya,
     sAvitragrahaH purastAt tasya.
     yajati: damUnA devaH savitA vareNya iti madvatyA rUpasamR^iddhayA.
     madvad vai tR^itIyasavanasya rUpaM.
     nAnunvaShaTkaroti, na bhakShayati.
     saMsthA vA eShA yad anunvaShaTkAraH, saMsthA bhakShaH, prANaH #savitA:
     net prANaM saMsthApayAnIty
|p5  ubhe vA eSha ete savane vipibati yat #savitA:

     tad yat pibavat sAvitryai nividaH padam purastAd bhavati madvad upariShTAd,

|p6  bahvyaH prAtar vAyavyAH shasyanta, ekA tR^itIyasavane.

|c30
|p1  ArbhavaM shaMsaty
|p2  #R^ibhavo vai deveShu tapasA somapItham abhyajayaMs.
     tebhyaH prAtaHsavane &0,1 'vAcikalpayiShaMs,
     tAn #agnir #vasubhiH prAtaHsavanAd anudata.

     tAn #indro #rudrair mAdhyaMdinAt savanAd anudata.

     tava vA ime 'ntevAsAs, tvam evaibhiH sampibasveti.

|c31
|p1  vaishvadevaM shaMsati
|p2  yathA vai prAja evaM vaishvadevaM.
     tad yathAntaraM janatA evaM sUktAni, yathAraNyAny evaM dhAyyAs.
     tad ubhayato dhAyyAm paryAhvayate.
     tasmAt tAny araNyAni santy anaraNyAni mR^igaish ca vayobhish ceti ha smAha
|p3  yathA vai puruSha evaM vaishvadevaM.
     tasya yathAvantaram a.NgAny evaM sUktAni, yathA parvANy evaM dhAyyAs.
     tad ubhayato dhAyyAm paryAhvayate.
     tasmAt puruShasya parvANi shithirANi santi dR^i.lhAni,
     brahmaNA hi tAni dhR^itAni
|p4  mUlaM vA etad yaj~Nasya yad dhAyyAsh ca yAjyAsh ca.
     tad yad anyA-anyA dhAyyAsh ca yAjyAsh ca kuryur,
     unmUlam eva tad yaj~NaM kuryus.
     tasmAt tAH samAnya eva syuH
|p5  pA~NcajanyaM vA etad ukthaM yad vaishvadevaM.
     sarveShAM vA etat pa~NcajanAnAm uktham:
     devamanuShyANAM gandharvApsarasAM sarpANAM ca pitRNAM caiteShAM
     vA etat pa~Ncaja~NAnAm ukthaM
|p6  sarva enam pa~NcajanA vidur,
     ainam pa~Ncinyai janatAyai havino gachanti ya evaM veda
|p7  sarvadevatyo vA eSha hotA yo vaishvadevaM shaMsati.
     sarvA disho dhyAyec chaMsiShyan, sarvAsv eva tad dikShu rasaM dadhAti
|p  8 yasyAm asya dishi dveShyaH syAn na tAM dhyAyed,
     anuhAyaivAsya tad vIryam Adatte
|p9  'ditir dyaur aditir antarikSham ity
     uttamayA paridadhAtIyaM vA #aditir iyaM dyaur iyaM antarikSham
|p10  aditir mAtA sa pitA sa putra itIyaM vai mAteyam piteyam putro
|p11  vishve devA aditiH pa~Nca janA ity, asyAM vai #vishve devA asyAm pa~NcajanA
|p12  aditir jAtam aditir janitvam itIyaM vai jAtam iyaM janitvaM
|p13  dviH pacchaH paridadhAti. catuShpAdA vai pashavaH, pashUnAm avaruddhyai.
     sakR^id ardharcashaH, pratiShThAyA eva.
     dvipratiShTho vai puruShash catuShpAdAH pashavo,
     yajamAnam eva tad dvipratiShThaM catuShpAtsu pashuShu pratiShThApayati
|p14  sadaiva pa~NcajanIyayA paridadhyAt.
     tad upaspR^isan bhUmim paridadhyat.
     tad yasyAm eva yaj~NaM sambharati,
     tasyAm evainaM tad antataH pratiShThApayati
|p15  vishve devAH shR^iNutemaM havam ma iti

     yathAbhAgaM tad devatAH prINAti

|c32
|p1  AgneyI prathamA ghR^itayAjyA, saumI saumyayAjyA, vaiShNavI ghR^itayAjyA.

     pitR^ibhyo vA anustaraNI, tasmAt saumyasya pitR^imatyA yajaty

|c33
|p1  #prajApatir vai svAM duhitaram abhyadhyAyad,

     tan mAduShasya mAduShatvam.

     parokShapriyA iva hi devAH

|c34
|p1  tad agninA paryAdadhus, tan #maruto 'dhUnvaMs, tad agnir na prAcyAvayat.

|c39 {adhyAya 14, khaNDaH 1-6}
|p1  devA vA asurair yuddham upaprAyan vijayAya, tAn #agnir nAnvakAmayataituM.

     gAyatrI vai tan.
     na ha vai gAyatrI kShamA ramata,

|c44
|p1  yo vA eSha tapaty eSho 'gniShToma, eSha sAhnas.

|p2  tena saMtvaramAnAs careyur, yathaiva prAtaHsavana evam,
     mAdhyaMdina evaM tR^itIyasavana.
     evam u ha yajamAno 'pramAyuko bhavati
|p3  yad dha vA idam pUrvayoH savanayor asaMtvaramANAsh caranti,
     tasmAd dhedam prAcyo grAmatA bahulAviShTA.
     atha yad dhedaM tR^itIyasavane saMtvaramANash caranti,
     tasmAd dhedam pratya~Nci dIrghAraNyAni bhavanti.
     tathA ha yajamAnaH pramAyuko bhavati
|p4  tenAsaMtvaramANAsh careyur,
     yathaiva prAtaHsavana evam mAdhyaMdina evaM tR^itIyasavana.
     evam u ha yajamAno 'pramAyuko bhavati
|p5  sa etam eva shastreNAnuparyAvarteta.
     yadA vA eSha prAtar udety, atha mandraM tapati:
     tasmAn mandrayA vAcA prAtaHsavane shAMsed.
     atha yadAbhyety, atha balIyas tapati:
     tasmAd balIyasyA vAcA madhyaMdine shaMsed.
     atha yadAbhitarAm ety, atha baliShThatamaM tapati:
     tasmAd baliShThatamayA vAcA tR^itIyasavane shaMsed.
     evaM shaMsed yadi vAca IshIta, vAg ghi shastraM.
     yayA tu vAcottarottariNyotsaheta samApanAya,
     tayA pratipadyetaitat sushastatamam iva bhavati
|p6  sa vA eSha na kadA canAstam eti nodeti
|p7  taM yad astam etIti manyante,
     'hna eva tad antam itvAthAtmAnaM viparyasyate,
     rAtrIm evAvastAt kurute 'haH parastAd
|p8  atha yad enam prAtar udetIti manyante,
     rAtrer eva tad antam itvAthAtmAnaM viparyasyate,
     'har evAvastAt kurute rAtrIm parastAt
|p9  sa vA eSha na kadA cana nimrocati
|p10  na ha vai kadA cana nimrocaty,
     etasya ha sAyujyaM sarUpatAm salokatAm ashnute ya evaM veda ya evaM veda

|c45 {adhyAya 15, khaNDaH 1-6}
|p1  yaj~No vai devebhyo 'nnAdyam udakrAmat.
     te devA abruvan:
     yaj~No vai no 'nnAdyam udakramId, anv imaM yaj~Nam anna anvichAmeti.
     te 'bruvan:
     katham anvichAmeti, brAhmaNena ca chandobhish cety abruvaMs.
     te brAhmaNaM chandobhir adIkShayaMs,
     tasyAntaM yaj~Nam atanvatApi patnIH samayAjayaMs.
     tasmAd dhApy etarhi dIkShaNIyAyAm iShTAv Antam eva yaj~NaM tanvate,
     'pi patnIH saMyAjayanti.
     tam anu nyAyam anvavAyaMs
|p2  te prAyaNIyam atanvata.
     tam prAyaNIyena nedIyo 'nvAgachaMs, te karmabhiH samatvaranta.
     tac chaMyvantam akurvaMs,
     tasmAd dhApy etarhi prAyaNIyaM shaMyvantam eva bhavati.
     tam anu nyAyam anvavAyaMs
|p3  ta Atithyam atanvata.
     tam Atithyena nedIyo 'nvAgachaMs, te karmabhiH samatvaranta.
     tad i.lAntam akurvaMs, tasmAd dhApy etarhy Atithyam i.lAntam eva bhavati.
     tam anu nyAyam anvavAyaMs
|p4  ta upasado 'tanvata.
     tam upasadbhir nedIyo 'nvAgachaMs, te karmabhiH samatvaranta.
     te tisraH sAmidhenIr anUcya tisro devatA ayajaMs,
     tasmAd dhApy etarhy upasatsu tisra eva
     sAmidhenIr anUcya tisro devatA yajanti.
     tam anu nyAyam anvavAyaMs
|p5  ta upavasatham atanvata.
     tam upavasathye 'hany ApnuvaMs,
     tam AptvAntaM yaj~Nam atanvatApi patnIH samayAjayaMs.
     tasmAd dhApy etarhy upavasatha Antam eva yaj~NaM tanvate,
     'pi patnIH saMyAjayanti
|p6  tasmAd eteShu pUrveShu karmasu shanaistarAM-shanaistarAm ivAnubrUyAd
|p7  anUtsaram iva hi te tam AyAMs.
     tasmAd upavasathe yAvatyA vAcA kAmayIta,
     tAvatyAnubrUyAd, Apto hi sa tarhi bhavatItI
|p8  tam AptvAbruvaMs:
     tiShThasva no 'nnAdyAyeti.
     sa nety abravIt, kathaM vas tiShTheyeti. tAn IkShataiva.
     tam abruvan:
     brAhmaNena ca nash chandobhish ca sayug bhUtvAnnAdyAya tiShThasveti. tatheti.
     tasmAd dhApy etarhi yaj~NaH sayug bhUtvA devebhyo
     havyaM vahati brAhmaNena ca chandobhish ca

|c1 {adhyAya 16, khaNDaH 1-6}

|c3
|p1  athAtash chandAMsy eva vyatiShajaty.
     A tvA vahantu haraya, upo Shu shR^iNuhI gira iti
     gAyatrIsh ca pa.NktIsh ca vyatiShajati.
     gAyatro vai puruShaH, pA.NktAH pashavaH.
     puruSham eva tat pashubhir vyatiShajati, pashuShu pratiShThApayati.

     'yaM te astu haryata ity uShNihash ca bR^ihatIsh ca vyatiShajaty.
     auShNiho vai puruSho, bArhatAH pashavaH.
     puruSham eva tat pashubhir vyatiShajati, pashuShu pratiShThApayati.
     yad uShNik ca bR^ihatI ca, te dve anuShTubhau;
     teno vAco rUpAd anuShTubho rUpAd vajrarUpAn naity
|p3  A dhUrShu asmai, brahman vIra brahmakR^itiM juShANa iti
     dvipadAM ca triShTubhaM ca vyatiShajati.
     dvipAd vai puruSho, vIryaM triShTup.
     puruSham eva tad vIryeNa vyatiShajati, vIrye pratiShThApayati.
     tasmAt puruSho vIrye pratiShThitaH sarveShAm pashunAM vIryavattamo.
     yad u dvipadA ca viMshatyakSharA triShTup ca, te dve anuShTubhau;
     teno vAco rUpAd anuShTubho rUpAd vajrarUpan naity
|p4  eSha brahmA, pra te mahe vidathe shaMsiShaM harI iti
     dvipadAsh ca jagatIsh ca vyatiShajati.
     dvipAd vai puruSho, jAgatAH pashavaH.
     puruSham eva tat pashubhir vyatiShajati, pashuShu pratiShThApayati.

|c5
|p1  ahar vai devA ashrayanta rAtrIm asurAs,
     te samAvadvIryA evAsan, na vyAvartanta.
     so 'bravId #indraH:
     kash cAhaM cemAn ito 'surAn rAtrIm anv aveShyAva iti.
     sa deveShu na pratyavindad, abibhayU rAtres tamaso mR^ityos.
     tasmAd dhApy etarhi naktaM yAvanmatram ivaivApakramya bibheti,
     tama iva hi rAtrir mR^ityur iva
|p2  taM vai chandAMsy evAnvavAyaMs.
     taM yac chandAMsy evAnvavAyaMs,
     tasmAd #indrash caiva chandAMsi ca rAtrIM vahanti.
     na nivic chasyate na puroru.N na dhAyyA nAnyA devatendrash ca
     hy eva chandAMsi ca rAtrIM vahanti
|p3  tAn vai paryAyair eva paryAyam anudanta.
     yat paryAyaiH paryAyam anudanta, tat paryAyANAm paryAyatvaM
|p4  tAn vai prathamenaiva paryAyeNA pUrvarAtrAd
     anudanta madhyamena madhyarAtrAd uttamenApararAtrAd
|p5  api sharvaryA anusmasIty abruvann,
     apisharvarANi khalu vA etAni chandAMsIti ha smAhaitAni hIndraM rAtres
     tamaso mR^ityor bibhyatam atyapArayaMs, tad apisharvarANAm apisharvaratvam

|c6
|p1  pAntam A vo andhasa ity andhasvatyAnuShTubhA rAtrIm pratipadyala
|p2  AnuShTubhI vai rAtrir, etad rAtrirUpam
|p3  andhasvatyaH pItavatyo madvatyas triShTubho yAjyA bhavanty abhirUpA.
     yad yaj~Ne 'bhirUpaM tat samR^iddham
|p4  prathamena paryAyeNa stuvate, prathamAny eva padAni punar Adadate.
     yad evaiShAm ashvA gAva AsaMs, tad evaiShAM tenAdadate
|p5  madhyamena paryAyeNa stuvate, madhyamAny eva padAni punar Adadate.
     yad evaiShAm &2 anorathA AsaMs, tad evaiShAM tenAdadata
|p6  uttameua paryAyeNa stuvata, uttamAny eva padAni punar Adadate.
     yad evaiShAM vAso hiraNyam maNir adhyAtmam AsIt, tad evaiShAM tenAdadata
|p7  A dviShato vasu datte, nir enam ebhyaH sarvebhyo lokebhyo nudate,
     ya evaM veda
|p8  pavamAnavad ahar, ity Ahur, na rAtriH pavamAnavatI:
     katham ubhe pavamAnavatI bhavataH, kena te samAvadbhAjau bhavata iti
|p9  yad evendrAya madvane sutam, idaM vaso sutam andha,
     idaM hy anv ojasA sutam iti stuvanti ca shaMsanti ca:
     tena rAtriH pavamAnavatI, tenobhe pavamAnavatI bhavatas,
     tena te samAvadbhAjau bhavataH
|p10  pa~Ncadashastotram ahar, ity Ahur, na rAtriH pa~NcadashastotrA:
     katham ubhe pa~Ncadashastotre bhavataH, kena te samAvadbhAjau bhavata iti
|p11  dvAdasha stotrANy apisharvarANi,
     tisR^ibhir devatAbhiH saMdhinA rAthaMtareNa stuvate:
     tena rAtriH  pa~NcadashastotrA tenobhe pa~Ncadashastotre bhavatas,
     tena te samAvadbhAjau bhavataH
|p12  parimitaM stuvanty aparimitam anushaMsati,
     parimitaM vai bhUtam aparimitam bhavyam, aparimitasyAvaruddhyA ity
|p13  atishaMsati stotram.
     ati vai prajAtmAnam, ati pashavas.
     tad yat stotram atishaMsati,
     yad evAsyAty AtmAnaM tad evAsyAitenAvarunddhe 'varunddhe

|c7 {adhyAya 17, khaNDaH 1-8}
|p1  #prajApatir vai #somAyA rAj~Ne duhitaram prAyachat #sUryAM #sAvitrIM.
     tasyai sarve devA varA AgachaMs,
     tasyA etat sahasraM vahatum anvAkarod yad etad Ashvinam ity AcakShate.
     'nAshvinaM haiva tad yad arvAksahasraM,
     tasmAt tat sahasraM vaiva shaMsed bhUyo vA
|p2  prAshya ghR^itaM shaMsed.
     yathA ha vA idam ano vA ratho vAkto vartata, evaM haivAkto vartate
|p3  shakunir ivotpatiShyann AhvayIta
|p4  tasmin devA na samajAnata:
     mamedam astu mamedam astv iti.
     te saMjAnAnA abruvann:
     Ajim asyAyAmahai.
     sa yo na ujjeShyati, tasyedam bhaviShyatIti.
     te 'gner evAdhi gR^ihapater #AdityaM kAShThAm akurvata,
     tasmAd AgneyI pratipad bhavaty AshvinasyAgnir hotA gR^ihapatiH sa rAjeti
|p5  tad dhaika Ahur:
     agnim manye pitaram agnim Apim ity etayA pratipadyeta
|p6  divi shukraM yajataM sUryasyeti prathamayaiva R^icA kAShThAm ApnotIti
|p7  tattan nAdR^ityaM ya enaM tatra brUyAd:
     agnim-agnim iti vai pratyapAdy, agnim ApatsyatIti, shashvat tathA syAt
|p8  tasmAd:
     agnir hotA gR^ihapatiH sa rAjety etayaiva pratipadyeta.
     gR^ihapativatI prajAtimatI shAntA, sarvAyuH sarvAyutvAya
|p9  sarvam Ayur eti ya evaM veda

|c8
|p1  tAsAM vai devatAnAm AjiM dhAvantInAm abhisR^iShTAnAm
     #agnir mukham prathamaH pratyapadyata.
     tam #ashvinAv anvAgachatAM, tam abrUtAm:
     apodihy, AvAM vA idaM jeShyAva iti.
     sa tathety abravIt, tasya vai mamehApyastv iti. tatheti.
     tasmA apy atrAkurutAM, tasmAd Agneyam Ashvine shasyate
|p2  tA #uShasam anvAgachatAM, tAm abrUtAm:
     apodihy, AvAM vA idaM jeShyAva iti.
     sA tathety abravIt, tasyai vai mamehApyastv iti. tatheti.
     tasyA apy atrAkurutAM, tasmAd uShasyam Ashvine shasyate
|p3  tAv #indram anvAgachatAM, tam abrUtAm:
     AvAM vA idam maghava~N jeShyAva iti.
     na ha taM dadhR^iShatur apodihIti vaktuM.
     sa tathety abravIt, tasya vai mamehApyastv iti. tatheti.
     tasmA apy atrAkurutAM, tasmAd aindram Ashvine shasyate
|p4  tad #ashvinA udajayatAm, #ashvinAv AshnuvAtAM.
     yad #ashvinA udajayatAm #ashvinAv AshnuvAtAM,
     tasmAd etad Ashvinam ity AcakShate
|p5  'shnute yad-yat kAmayate ya evaM veda

     yac chasyata AgneyaM shasyata uShasyam shasyata aindram:
     atha kasmAd etad Ashvinam ity AcakShata ity.
     #ashvinau hi tad udajayatAm, #ashvinAv AshnuvAtAM.
     yad #ashvinA udajayatAm #ashvinAv AshnuvAtAM,
     tasmAd etad Ashvinam ity AcakShate

|c9
|p1  ashvatarIrathenAgnir Ajim adhAvat, tAsAm prAjamAno yonim akU.layat,
     tasmAt tA na vijAyante

     ud u tyaM jAtavedasam iti sauryANi pratipadyeteti

     yathaiva gatvA kAShThAm aparAdhnuyAt, tAdR^ik tat
|p9  sUryo no divas pAtv ity etenaiva pratipadyeta.
     yathaiva gatvA kAShThAm abhipadyeta, tAdR^ik tad
|p10  ud u tyaM jAtavedasam iti dvitIyaM shaMsati

|c10
|p1  tad Ahuh:
     #sUryo nAtishasyo, bR^ihatI nAtisasyA.
     yat #sUryam atishaMsed brahmavarcasam atipadyeta,
     yad bR^ihatIm atishaMset prANAn atipadyetetI/ndra
|p2  kratuM na A bharety aindram pragAthaM shaMsati
|p3  shikShA No asmin puruhUta yAmani jIvA jyotir ashImahIty

     asau vAva svardR^ik, tena #sUryaM nAtishaMsati

     ahar vai #mitro, rAtrir #varuNa.
     ubhe vA eSho 'horAtre Arabhate, yo 'tirAtram upaiti.
     tad yan maitrAvaruNam pragAthaM shaMsaty,
     ahorAtrayor evainaM tat pratiShThApayati
|p10  sUracakShasa iti, tena #sUryaM nAtishaMsati.
     yad u bArhataH pragAthas, tena bR^ihatIM nAtishaMsati
|p11  mahI dyauH pR^ithivI ca nas,
     te hi dyAvApR^ithivi vishvashambhuveti dyAvApR^ithivIye shaMsati.
     dyAvApR^ithivI vai pratiShThe:
     iyam eveha pratiShThAsAv amutra.
     tad yad dyAvApR^ithivIye shaMsati, pratiShThayor evainaM tat pratiShthApayati
|p12  devo devI dharmaNA sUryaH shucir iti, tena #sUryaM nAtishaMsati
|p13  yad u gAyatrI ca jagatI ca te dve bR^ihatyau, tena bR^ihatIM nAtishaMsati
|p14  vishvasya devI mR^icayasya janmano na yA roShAti na grabhad iti
     dvipadAm shaMsati
|p15  citaidham uktham iti ha sma vA etad AcakShate yad etad AshvinaM.
     #nirR^itir ha sma pAshiny upAste:
     yadaiva hotA paridhAsyaty, atha pAshAn pratimokShyAmIti.
     tato vA etAm #bR^ihaspatir dvipadAm apashyan:
     nA ya roShAti na grabhad iti,
     tayA #nirR^ityAH pAshinyA adharAcaH pAshAn apAsyat.
     tad yad etaM dvipadAM hotA shaMsati,
     #nirR^ityA eva tat pAshinyA adharAcaH pAsAn apAsyati,
     svasty eva hotonmucyate sarvAyuH sarvAyutvAya
|p16  sarvam Ayur eti ya evaM veda
|p17  mR^icayasya janmana ity.
     asau vAva marcayatIva, tena #sUryaM nAtishaMsati
|p18  yad u dvipadA puruShachandasaM, sA sarvANi chandAMsy abhyAptA:
     tena bR^ihatIM nAtishaMsati

|c11
|p1  brAhmaNaspatyayA paridadhAti.
     brahma vai #bR^ihaspatir, brahmaNy evainaM tad antataH pratiShThApayaty
|p2  evA pitre vishvadevAya vR^iShNa ity etayA paridadhyAt prajAkAmaH pashukAmo
|p3  bR^ihaspate suprajA vIravanta iti.
     prajayA vai suprajA vIravAn
|p4  vayaM syAma patayo rayINAm iti
|p5  prajAvAn pashumAn rayimAn vIravAn bhavati
     yatraivaM vidvAn etayA paridadhAti
|p6  bR^ihaspate ati yad aryo arhAd ity

     'tIva vAnyAn brahmavarcasam arhati
|p7  dyumad iti.
     dyumad iva vai brahmavarcasaM vibhAtIti, vIva vai brahmavarcasam bhAti

     dIdAyeva vai brahmavarcasaM

     citram iva vai brahmavarcasam
|p10  brahmavarcasI brahmayashasI bhavati yatraivaM vidvAn etayA paridadhAti

|p12  brAhmaNaspatyA, tena #sUryaM nAtisaMsati

     tena bR^ihatIM nAtishaMsati
|p14  gAyatryA ca triShTubhA ca vaShaTkuryAd

|p16  brahmavarcasI brahmayashasI vIryavAn bhavati
     yatraivaM vidvAn gAyatryA ca triShTubhA ca vaShaTkaroty
|p17  ashvinA vAyunA yuvaM sudakSho,bhA pibatam ashvineti

     brahma vai gAyatry annaM virAd, brahmaNaiva tad annAdyaM saMdadhAti
|p19  brahmavarcasI brahmayashasI bhavati,
     brahmAdyam annam atti yatraivaM vidvAn gAyatryA ca virAjA ca vaShaTkaroti

     pra vAm andhAMsi madyAny asthur, ubhA pibatam ashvinety etAbhyAm

|c12
|p1  caturviMsham etad ahar upayanty ArambhaNIyam
|p2  etena vai saMvatsaram Arabhanta,

     anArabdhaM vai tac chando, 'nArabdhA sA devatA,
     yad etasminn ahani nArabhante.

|p5  ukthyo bhavati.
     pashavo vA ukthAni, pashUnAm avaruddhyai

     sa mAso.
     mAsasha eva tat saMvatsaram Arabhante
|p7  tasya ShaShTish ca trINi ca shatAni stotriyAs.
     tAvanti saMvatsarasyAhAny, ahashsha eva tat saMvatsaram Arabhante

     na vA etad anyo 'gniShTomAd ahar dAdhArA na vivyAceti
|p9  sa yady agniShTomaH syAd,
     aShTAcatvAriMshAs trayaH pavamAnAH syush caturviMshAnItarANi stotrANi.
     tad u ShaShTish caiva trINi ca shatAni stotriyAs.
     tAvanti saMvatsarasyAhAny, ahashsha eva tat saMvatsaram Arabhanta

     sarvANi caturviMshAni stotrANi, pratyakShAd dhy etad ahash caturviMshaM.
     tasmAd ukthya eva syAt

|c13
|p1  bR^ihadrathaMtare sAmanI bhavata.
     ete vai yaj~Nasya nAvau sampAriNyau yad bR^ihadrathaMtare,

|c14

|c15 {adhyAya 18, khaNDaH 1-8}
|p1  jyotir gaur Ayur iti stomebhir yanty.
     ayaM vai loko jyotir, antarikShaM gaur, asau loka AyuH
|p2  sa evaiSha uttaras tryaho
|p3  jyotir gaur Ayur iti trINy ahAni, gaur Ayur jyotir iti trINy
|p4  ayaM vai loko jyotir asau loko jyotis,
     te ete jyotiShI ubhayataH saMlokete

|c16
|p1  prathamaM Sha.laham upayanti, Sha.l ahAni bhavanti.
     ShaD vA R^itava, R^itusha eva tat saMvatsaram Apnuvanty,
     R^itushAN saMvatsare pratitiShThanto yanti
|p2  dvitIyaM Sha.laham upayanti, dvAdashAhAni bhavanti.

|p3  tR^itIyaM Sha.laham upayanty, aShTAdashAhAni bhavanti.

|c17
|p1  gavAm ayanena yanti.
     gAvo vA #AdityA, #AdityAnAm eva tad ayanena yanti
|p2  gAvo vai satram Asata shaphA~N chR^i.NgANi &1 siShAsantyas,
     tAsAM dashame mAsi shaphAH shR^i.NgANy ajAyanta.
     tA abruvan:
     yasmai kAmAyAdIkShAmahy ApAma tam, uttiShThAmeti.
     tA yA udatiShThaMs, tA etAH shR^i.NgiNyo
|p3  'tha yAH samApayiShyAmaH saMvatsaram ity Asata,
     tAsAm ashraddhayA shR^i.NgANi prAvartanta, tA etAs tUparA.
     UrjaM tv asunvaMs, tasmAd u tAH sarvAn R^itUn prAptvottaram uttiShThanty,
     UrjaM hy asunvan.
     sarvasya vai gAvaH premANaM sarvasya cArutAM gatAH
|p4  sarvasya premANaM sarvasya cArutAM gachati ya evaM vedA/dityAsh
|p5  ca ha vA #a.Ngirasash ca svarge loke 'spardhanta:
     vayam pUrva eShyAmo vayam iti.
     te hAdityAH pUrve svargaM lokaM jagmuH,
     pashcevA.NgirasaH ShaShTyAM vA varSheShu
|p6  yathA vA prAyaNIyo 'tirAtrash caturviMsha ukthyaH sarve
     'bhiplavAH Sha.lahA AkShyanty anyAny ahAni, tad #AdityAnAm ayanam
|p7  prAyaNIyo 'tirAtrash caturviMsha ukthyaH sarve
     pR^iShThyAH Sha.lahA AkShyanty anyAny ahAni, tad #a.NgirasAm ayanaM
|p8  sA yathA srutir a~NjasAyany evam abhiplavaH Sha.lahaH svargasya
     lokasyAtha yathA mahApathaH paryANa evam
     pR^iShThyaH Sha.lahaH svargasya lokasya.
     tad yad ubhAbhyAM yanty, ubhAbhyAM vai yan na riShyaty,
     ubhayoH kAmayor upAptyai yash cAbhiplave Sha.lahe yash ca pR^iShThye

|c18
|p1  ekaviMsham etad ahar upayanti viShuvantam madhye saMvatsarasyai/tena
|p2  vai devA ekaviMshenAdityaM svArgaya lokAyodayachan
|p3  sa eSha ita ekaviMshas
|p4  tasya dashAvastAd ahAni divAkIrtyasya bhavanti dasha parastAn,
     madhya eSha ekaviMsha ubhayato virAji pratiShThita,
     ubhayato hi vA eSha virAji pratiShThitas.
     tasmAd eSho 'ntaremA~Ml lokAn yan na vyathate
|p5  tasya vai devA #Adityasya svargAl lokAd avapAtAd abibhayus,
     taM tribhiH svargair lokair avastAt pratyuttabhnuvan.
     stomA vai trayaH svargA lokAs.
     tasya parAco 'tipAtAd abibhayus,
     taM tribhiH svargair lokaiH parastAt pratyastabhnuvan.
     stomA vai trayaH svargA lokAs.
     tat trayo 'vastAt saptadashA bhavanti trayAH parastAn,
     madhya eSha ekaviMsha ubhayataH svarasAmabhir dhR^ita,
     ubhayato hi vA eSha svarasAmabhir dhR^itas.
     tasmAd eSho 'ntaremA~Ml lokAn yan na vyathate
|p6  tasya vai devA #Adityasya svargAl lokAd avapAtAd abibhayus,
     tam paramaiH svargair lokair avastAt pratyuttabhnuvan.
     stomA vai paramAH svargA lokAs.
     tasya parAco 'tipAtAd abibhayus,
     tam paramaiH svargair lokaiH parastAt pratyastabhnuvan.
     stomA vai paramAH svargA lokAs.
     tat trayo 'vastAt saptadashA bhavanti trayaH parastAt,
     te dvau-dvau sampadya trayash catustriNshA bhavanti.
     catustriMsho vai stomAnAm uttamas.
     teShu vA eSha etad adhyAhitas tapati,
     teShu hi vA eSha etad adhyAhitas tapati

     sarvam evedam atirocate yad idaM kiMcottaro bhavati

|c19
|p1  svarasAmna upayantIme vai lokAH svarasAmAna.

     tad yat svarasAmna upayanty, eShv evainaM tal lokeShv Abhajanti
|p2  teShAM vai devAH saptadashAnAm pravlayAd abibhayuH:

     AyuShy evainaM tad vIrya indriye dadhAti

|c22
|p1  yathA vai puruSha evaM viShuvAMs.

|c23 {adhyAya 19, khaNDaH 1-6}
|p1  #prajApatir akAmayata:
     prajAyeya bhUyAn syAm iti.
     sa tapo 'tapyata,
     sa tapas taptvemaM dvAdashAham apshyad Atmana evA.NgeShu ca prANeShu ca.
     tam Atmana evA.Ngebhyash ca prANebhyash ca dvAdashadhA niramimIta,

|p2  bhavaty AtmanA, pra prajayA pashubhir jAyate ya evaM veda
|p3  so 'kAmayata:
     kathaM nu gAyatryA sarvato dvAdashAham paribhUya sarvAm R^iddhim R^idhnuyAm iti.
     taM vai tejasaiva purastAt paryabhavac
     chandobhir madhyato 'kSharair upariShTAd.
     gAyatryA sarvato dvAdashAham paribhUya sarvAm R^iddhim Ardhnot
|p4  sarvAm R^iddhim R^idhnoti ya evaM veda

     eShA vai gAyatrI pakShiNI cakShuShmatI jyotiShmatI bhAsvatI yad dvAdashAhas.

     ye 'ShTau madhya ukthyAH sa AtmA
