|c25
|p1  #prAjApatiyaj~No vA eSha yad dvAdashAhaH,
     #prajApatir vA etenAgre 'yajata dvAdashAhena.
     so 'bravId R^itUMsh ca mAsAMsh ca:
     yAjayata mA dvAdashAheneti.
     taM dIkShayitvAnapakramaM gamayitvAbruvan:
     dehi nu no 'tha tvA yAjayiShyAma iti.
     tebhya iSham Urjam prAyachat, saiShorg R^ituShu ca mAseShu ca nihitA.
     dadataM vai te tam ayAjayaMs, tasmAd dadad yAjyaH.
     pratigR^ihNanto vai te tam ayAjayaMs, tasmAt pratigR^ihNatA yAjyam
|p2  ubhaye rAdhnuvanti ya evaM vidvAMso yajante ca yAjayanti ca
|p3  te vA ima R^itavash ca mAsAsh ca gurava ivAmanyanta dvAdashAhe pratigR^ihya,
     te 'bruvan #prajApatiM:
     yAjaya no dvAdashAheneti.
     sa tathety abravIt, te vai dIkShadhvam iti te pUrvapakShAH pUrve dIkShanta,
     te pApmAnam apAhata.
     tasmAt te diveva, diveva hy apahatapApmAno.
     'parapakShA apare 'dIkShanta, te natarAm pApmAnam apAhata.
     tasmAt te tama iva, tama iva hy anapahatapApmAnas.
     tasmAd evaM vidvAn dIkShamANeShu pUrvaH-pUrva eva didIkShiShetA
|p4  =pa pApmAnaM hate ya evaM veda
|p5  sa vA ayam #prajApatiH saMvatsara R^ituShu ca mAseShu ca pratyatiShThat,
     te vA ima R^itavash ca mAsAsh ca #prajApatAv eva saMvatsare pratyatiShThaMs,
     ta ete 'nyonyasmin pratiShThitA.
     evaM ha vAva sa R^itviji pratitiShThati yo dvAdashAhena yajate.
     tasmAd Ahur:
     na pApaH puruSho yAjyo dvAdashAhena, ned ayam mayi pratitiShThAd iti
|p6  jyeShvhayaj~No vA eSha yad dvAdashAhaH,
     sa vai devAnAM jyeShTho ya etenAgre 'yajata.
     shreShThayaj~No vA eSha yad dvAdashAhaH,
     sa vai devAnAM shreShTho ya etenAgre 'yajata
|p7  jyeShThaH shreShTho yajeta, kalyANIha samA bhavati.
     na pApaH puruSho yAjyo dvAdashAhena, ned ayam mayi pratitiShThad itI/ndrAya
|p8  vai deva jyaiShThyAya shraiShThyAya nAtiShThanta,
     so 'bravId #bR^ihaspatiM:
     yAjaya mA dvAdashAheneti.
     tam ayAjayat, talo vai tasmai devA jyaiShThyAya shraiShThyAyAtiShThanta
|p9  tiShThante 'smai svA jyaiShThyAya shraiShThyAya,
     sam asmin svAH shreShThatAyAM jAnate ya evaM vedo/rdhvo
|p10  vai prathamas tryahas, tirya.N madhyamo, 'rvA.N uttamaH.
     sa yad UrdhvaH prathamas tryahas, tasmAd ayam agnir Urdhva uddIpyata,
     UrdhvA hy etasya dig.
     yat tirya.N madhyamas, tasmAd ayaM vAyus tirya.N pavate,
     tirashcIr Apo vahanti;
     tirashcI hy etasya dig.
     yad arvA.N uttamas, tasmAd asAv arvA.N tapaty, arvA.N varShaty,
     arvA~Nci nakShatrANy;
     ArvAci hy etasya dik.
     samya~Nco vA ime lokAH, samya~Nca ete tryahAH
|p11  samya~Nco 'smA ime lokAH shriyai dIdyati ya evaM veda

|c26
|p1  dIkShA vai devebhyo 'pAkrAmat.

     Urg vai vasanta, iSham eva tad Urjam abhyudavasyati

|c27
|p1  chandAMsi vA anyonyasyAyatanam abhyadhyAyan.
     gAyatrI triShTubhash ca jagatyai cAyatanam abhyadhyAyat,
     triShTub gAyatryai ca jagatyai ca, jagatI gAyatryai ca triShTubhash ca.
     tato vA etam #prajApatir vyU.lhachandasaM dvAdashAham apashyat, tam Aharat,
     tenAyajata, tena sa sarvAn kAmAMsh chandAMsy agamayat
|p2  sarvAn kAmAn gachati ya evaM veda
|p3  chandAMsi vyUhaty ayAtayAmatAyai
|p4  chandAMsy eva vyUhati.
     tad yathAdo 'shvair vAna.ludbhir
     vAnyair-anyair ashrAntatarair-ashrAntatarair upavimokaM yAnty,
     evam evaitac chandobhir
     anyair-anyair ashrAntatarair-ashrAntatarair upavimokaM svargaM lokam yanti
     yac chandAMsi vyUhatI/mau
|p5  vai lokau sahAstAM, tau vyaitAM.
     nAvarShan, na samatapat, te pa~NcajanA na samajAnata.
     tau devAH samanayaMs, tau saMyantAv etaM devavivAhaM vyavahetAM.
     rathaMtareNaiveyam amUM jinvati, bR^ihatAsAv imAM
|p6  naudhasenaiveyam amUM jinvati, shyaitenAsAv imAM.
     dhUmenaiveyam amUM jinvati, vR^iShTyAsAv imAM.
     devayajanam eveyam amuShyAm adadhAt, pashUn asAv asyAm
|p7  etad vA iyam amuShyAM devayajanam adadhAd yad etac candramasi kR^iShNam iva
|p8  tasmAd ApUryamANapakSheShu yajanta etad evopepsanta
|p9  UShAn asAv asyAM.
     tad dhApi #turah #kAvaSheya uvAcoShaH poSho #janamejayaketi.
     tasmAd dhApy etarhi gavyam mImAMsamAnAH pR^ichanti:
     santi tatroShA+H iti \ USho hi poSho.
     'sau vai loka imaM lokam abhiparyAvartata
|p10  tato vai dyAvApR^ithivI abhavatAM, na dyAvAntarikShAn nAntarikShAd bhUmiH

|c28
|p1  bR^ihac ca vA idam agre rathaMtaraM cAstAM.

     vairAjaM cAtyamanyanta.

|c29 {adhyAya 20, khaNDaH 1-4}
|p1  #agnir vai devatA prathamam ahar vahati,

|p2  yathAdevatam enena yathAstomaM yathAsAma yathAchandasaM rAdhnoti
     ya evaM veda

     eti prathame 'hani prathamasyAhno rUpam

     marutvatIyasya pratipadanucarau.
     rathavac ca pibavac ca prathame 'hani prathamasyAhno rUpam

     preti prathame 'hani prathamasyAhno rUpam
|p10  agnir netA, tvaM soma kratubhiH, pinvanty apa iti dhAyyAH.
     prathameShu padeShu devatA nirucyante, prathame 'hani prathamasyAhno rUpam
|p11  pra vA indrAya bR^ihata iti marutvatIyaH pragAthaH.
     preti prathame 'hani prathamasyAhno rUpam
|p12  A yAtv indro 'vasa upa na iti sUktam.
     eti prathame 'hani prathamasyAhno rUpam

     rathaMtaram pR^iShTham bhavati.

     eti prathame 'hani prathamasyAhno rUpam

     svastyayanaM vai tArkShyaH, svastitAyai
|p17  svastyayanam eva tat kurute,
     svasti saMvatsarasya pAram ashnute ya evaM veda

|c1 {adhyAya 21, khaNDaH 1-5}
|p1  vishve vai devA devatAs tR^itIyam ahar vahanti,

     ya evaM veda

     yad ashvavad yad antavad yat punarAvR^ittaM yat punarnuuR^ittaM
     yad ratavad yat paryastavad yat trivad yad antarUpaM,
     yad uttame pade devatA nirucyate, yad asau loko 'bhyudito,

     etAni vai tR^itIyasyAhno rUpANi

     tad vairUpasya vairUpatvaM

     yad ashvA bhUtvA padbhir apAghnata, tad ashvAnAm ashvatvam

|c3
|p1  Apyante vai stomA Apyante chandAMsi tR^itIye 'hany,

     vAg ity ekam akSharam, akSharam iti tryakSharaM

|c4
|p1  vAg vai devatA caturtham ahar vahaty,
     ekaviMshaH stomo vairAjaM sAmAnuShTup chando.
     yathAdevatam enena yathAstomaM yathAsAma yathAchandasaM rAdnnoti
     ya evaM veda
|p2  yad vA eti ca preti ca tac caturthasyAhno rUpaM.
     yad dhy eva prathamam ahas tad etat punar yac caturthaM.
     yad yuktavad yad rathavad yad Ashumad yat pibavad,
     yat prathame pade devatA nirucyate,
     yad ayaM loko 'bhyudito,
     yaj jAtavad yad dhavavad yac chukravad
     yad vAco rUpaM yad vaimadaM yad viriphitaM yad vichandA
     yad UnAtiriktaM yad vairAjaM yad AnuShTubhaM yat kariShyad
     yat prathamasyAhno rUpam:
     etAni vai caturthasyAhno rUpANy
|p3  AgniM na svavR^iktibhir iti
     caturthasyAhna Ajyam bhavati vaimadaM viriphitaM viriphitasya
     R^iShesh caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpam
|p4  aShTarcam pA.Nktam.
     pA.Nkto yaj~NaH pA.NktAH pashavaH, pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p5  tA u dasha jagatyo.
     jagatprAtaHsavana eSha tryahas, tena caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p6  tA u pa~NcadashAnuShTubha.
     AnuShTubhaM hy etad ahas, tena caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p7  tA u viMshatir gAyatryaH.
     punaH prAyaNIyaM hy etad ahas, tena caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p8  tad etad astutam asastam ayAtayAma sUktaM yaj~Na eva sAkShAt.
     tad yad etac caturthasyAhna Ajyam bhavati, yaj~NAd eva tad yaj~NaM tanvate,
     vAcam eva tat punar upayanti saMtatyai
|p9  saMtatais tryahair avyavachinnair yanti ya evaM vidvAMso yanti
|p10  vAyo shukro ayAmi te, vihi hotrA avItA, vAyo shataM harINAm,
     indrash ca vAyav eShAM somAnAm, A cikitAna sukratU, A no vishvAbhir Utibhis,
     tyam u vo aprahaNam, apa tyaM vR^ijinaM ripum,
     ambitame nadItama ity AnuShTubham pra:ugam.
     eti ca preti ca shukravac caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p11  taM tvA yaj~Nebhir Imaha iti marutvatIyasya pratipad. Imaha ity:
     abhyAyAmyam ivaitad ahas, tena caturthasyAhno rUpam
|p12  idaM vaso sutam andha, indra nedIya ed ihi, praitu brahmaNas patir,
     agnir netA, tvaM soma kratubhiH, pinvanty apaH,
     pra va indraya bR^ihata iti prathamenAhnA samAna AtAnash,
     caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p13  shrudhI havam indra mA riShaNya iti
     sUktaM havavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpam
|p14  marutvA~M indra vR^iShabho raNayeti sUktam,
     ugraM sahodAm iha taM huvemeti havavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rupAM
|p15  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavata
|p16  imaM nu mAyinaM huva iti
     paryAso havavAMsh caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p17  tA u gAyatryo.
     gAyatryo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinaM vahanti
|p18  tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAd gAyatrIShu nividaM dadhAti
|p19  pibA somam indra mandatu tvA, shrudhI havaM vipipAnasyAdrer iti
     vairAjam pR^iShTham bhavati.
     bArhate 'hani caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p20  yad vAvAneti dhAyyAcyutA
|p21  tvAm id dhi havAmaha iti bR^ihato yonim anu nivartayati,
     bArhataM hy etad ahar Ayatanena
|p22  tvam indra pratUrtiShv iti sAmapragAtho,
     'shastihA janiteti jAtavAMsh caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p23  tyam U Shu vAjinaM devajUtam iti tArkShyo 'cyutaH

|c5
|p1  kuha shruta indraH kasminn adyeti sUktaM vaimadaM viriphitaM
     viriphitasya R^iShesh caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p2  yudhmasya te vR^iShabhasya svarAja iti sUktam,
     ugraM gabhIraM januShAbhy ugram iti
     jAtavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p3  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavate
|p4  tyam u vaH satrAsAham iti paryAso.
     vishvAsu gIrShv Ayatam ity:
     abhyAyAmyam ivaitad ahas, tena caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p5  tA u gAyatryo.
     gAyatryo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinam vahanti.
     tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAd gAyatrIShu nividaM dadhAti
|p6  vishvo devasya netus, tat savitur vareNyam, A vishvadevaM satpatim iti
     vaishvadevasya pratipadanucarau.
     bArhate 'hani caturthe 'hani caturhasyAhno rUpam
|p7  A devo yAtu savitA suratna iti sAvitram.
     eti caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpam
|p8  pra dyAvA yaj~NaiH pR^ithivI namobhir iti dyAvApR^ithivIyam.
     preti caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpam
|p9  pra R^ibhubyoo dUtam iva vAcam iShya ity Arbhavam.
     preti ca vAcam iShya iti ca caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpam
|p10  pra shukraitu devI manISheti vaishvadevam.
     preti ca shukravac ca caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p11  tA u vichandasaH.
     santi dvipadAH santi catuShpadAs, tena caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p12  vaishvAnarasya sumatau syAmety AgnimArutasya pratipad,
     ito jAta iti jAtavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p13  ka IM vyaktA naraH sanI.lA iti mArutaM,
     nakir hy eShAM janUMShi vedeti jAtavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p14  tA u vichandasaH.
     santi dvipadAH santi catuShpadAs, tena caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p15  jAtavedase sunavAma somam iti jAtavedasyAcyutA/gniM
|p16  naro dIdhitibhir araNyor iti jAtavedasyaM,
     hastacyutI janayanteti jAtavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyAhno rUpaM
|p17  tA u vichandasaH.
     santi virAjaH santi triShTubhas, tena caturthasyAhno rUpam ahno rUpam

|c6 {adhyAya 22, khaNDaH 1-10}
|p1  gaur vai devatA pa~Ncamam ahar vahati,
     triNavah stomaH shAkvaraM sAma pA.Nktish chando.
     yathAdevatam enena yathAstomaM yathAsAma yathAchandasaM rAdhnoti
     ya evaM veda
|p2  yad vai neti na preti yat sthitaM, tat pa~NcamasyAhno rUpaM
|p3  yad dhy eva dvitIyam ahas tad etat punar yat pa~NcamaM
|p4  yad Urdhvavad yat prativad yad antarvad yad vR^iShaNvad yad vR^idhanvad,
     yan madhyame pade devatA nirucyate, yad antarikSham abhyuditaM
|p5  yad dugdhavad yad Udhavad yad dhenumad yat pR^ishnimad
     yan madvad yat pashurUpaM yad adhyAsavad
     - vikShudrA iva hi pashavo - yaj jAgataM - jAgatA hi pashavo
     - yad bArhatam - bArhatA hi pashAvo - yat pA.Nktam
     - pA.NktA hi pashavo - yad vAmaM - vAmam hi pashavo
     - yad dhaviShmad - dhavir hi pashavo - yad vapuShmad - vapur hi pashavo
     - yac chAkvaraM yat pA.NktaM yat kurvad yad dvitIyasyAhno rUpam:
     etAni vai pa~NcamasyAhno rUpANI/mam
|p6  U Shu vo atithim uSharbudham iti pa~NcamasyAhna Ajyam bhavati
     jAgatam adhyAsavat pashurUpam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p7  A no yaj~NaM divispR^isham, A no vAyo mahe tane, rathena pR^ithupAjasA,
     bahavaH sUracakShasa, imA u vAM diviShTayaH, pibA sutasya rasino,
     devaM-devaM vo 'vase devaM-devam, bR^ihad u gAyiShe vaca iti
     bArhatam pra:ugam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p8  yat pA~NcajanyayA visheti marutvatIyasya pratipat,
     pA~Ncajanyayeti pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p9  indra it somapA eka, indra nedIya ed ihy, ut tiShTha brahmaNas pate,
     'gnir netA, tvaM soma kratubhiH, pinvanty apo,
     bR^ihad indrAya gAyateti dvitIyenAhnA samAna AtAnaH pa~Ncame
     'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p10  avitAsi sunvato vR^iktabarhiSha iti
     sUktam madvat pA.Nktam pa~Ncapadam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p11  ittha hi soma in mada iti
     sUktam madvat pA.Nktam pa~Ncapadam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p12  indra piba tubhyaM suto madAyeti sUktam madvat traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavate
|p13  marutvA~M indra mIDhva iti paryAso.
     neti na preti pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpaM
|p14  tA u gAyatryo.
     gAyatryo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinaM vahanti.
     tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAd gAyatrIShu nividaM dadhAti

|c7
|p1  mahAnAmnIShv atra stuvate shAkvareNa sAmnA rAthaMtare
     'hani pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p2  #indro vA etAbhir mahAn AtmAnaM niramimIta, tasmAn mahAnAmnyo.
     'tho ime vai lokA mahAnAmnya ime mahAnta
|p3  imAn vai lokAn #prajApatiH sR^iShTvedaM sarvam ashaknod yad idam kiMca.
     yad imA~Ml lokAn #prajApatiH sR^iShTvedaM sarvam ashaknod yad idaM kiMca
     tac chakvaryo 'bhavaMs, tac chakvarINAM shakvarItvaM
|p4  tA UrdhvAH sImno 'bhyasR^ijata.
     yad UrdhvAH sImno 'bhyasR^ijata tat simA abhavaMs,
     tat simAnAM simAtvaM
|p5  svAdor itthA viShUvata, upa no haribhiH sutam,
     indraM vishvA avIvR^idhann ity anurUpo vR^iShaNvAn pR^ishnimAn madvAn
     vR^idhanvAn pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpaM
|p6  yad vAvAneti dhAyyAcyutA/bhi
|p7  tvA shUra nonuma iti rathaMtarasya yonim anu nivartayati,
     rAthaMtaraM hy etad ahar Ayatanena
|p8  mo Shu tvA vAghatash caneti sAmapragAtho 'dhyAsavAn
     pashurUpam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpaM
|p9  tyam U Shu vAjinaM devajUtam iti tArkShyo 'cyutaH

|c8
|p1  predam brahma vR^itratUryeShv Avitheti sUktam pA.Nktam
     pa~Ncapadam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcanAsyAhno rUpam
|p2  indro madAya vAvR^idha iti sUktam madvat pA.Nktam
     pa~Ncapadam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpaM
|p3  satrA madAsas tava vishvajanyA iti sUktam madvat traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavate
|p4  tam indraM vAjayAmasIti paryAsaH, sa vR^iShA vR^iShabho bhuvad iti
     pashurUpam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpaM
|p5  tA u gAyatryo.
     gAyatryo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinaM vahanti.
     tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAd gAyatrIShu nividaM dadhAti
|p6  tat savitur vR^iNImahe, 'dyA no deva savitar iti
     vaishvadevasya pratipadanucarau.
     rAthaMtare 'hani pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p7  ud u Shya devaH savitA damUnA iti sAvitram,
     A dAshuShe suvati bhUri vAmam iti vAmam
     pashurUpam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p8  mahI dyAvApR^ithivI iha jyeShThe iti dyAvApR^ithivIyaM,
     ruvad dhokSheti pashurUpam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p9  R^ibhur vibhvA vAja indro no achety ArbhavaM.
     vAjo vai pashavaH, pashurUpam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam
|p10  stuShe janaM suvrataM navyasIbhir iti vaishvadevam adhyAsavat
     pashurUpam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpaM
|p11  hUvisH pAntam ajaraM svarvidIty AgnimArutasya pratipad.
     dhaviShmat pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpaM
|p12  vapur nu tac cikituShe cid astv iti mArutaM
     vapuShmat pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpaM
|p13  jAtavedase sunavAma somam iti jAtavedasyAcyutA/gnir
|p14  hotA gR^ihapatiH sa rAjeti jAtavedasyam adhyAsavat
     pashurUpam pa~Ncame 'hani pa~NcamasyAhno rUpam

|c9
|p1  devakShetraM vA etad yat ShaShTham ahar.
     devakShetraM vA eta Agachanti ye ShaShTham ahar Agachanti
|p2  na vai devA anyonyasya gR^ihe vasanti, nartur R^itor gR^ihe vasatIty Ahus.
     tad yathAyatham R^itvija R^ituyAjAn yajanty asampradAyaM.
     tad yathartv R^itUn kalpayanti, yathAyathaM janatAs
|p3  tad Ahur:
     nartupraiShaiH preShitavyaM nartupraiShair vaShaTkR^ityaM.
     vAg vA R^itupraiShA, Apyate vai vAk ShaShThe 'hanIti
|p4  yad R^itupraiShaiH preShyeyur yad R^itupraiShair vaShaTkuryur,
     vAcam eva tad AptAM shrAntAm &5 mR^ikNavahIM vaharAviNIm R^icheyur
|p5  yad v ebhir na preShyeyur yad v ebhir na vaShaTkuryur,
     acyutAd yaj~Nasya cyaveran, yaj~NAt prANAt #prajApateH pashubhyo jihmA Iyus
|p6  tasmAd R^igmebhya evAdhi preShitavyam, R^igmebhyo 'dhi vaShaTkR^ityaM.
     tan na vAcam AptAM shrAntAm &5 mR^ikNavahIM vaharAviNIm R^ichanti,
     nAcyutAd yaj~Nasya cyavante,
     na yaj~NAt prANAt #prajApateH pashubhyo jihmA yanti

|c10
|p1  pArucchepIr upadadhati pUrvayoH savanayoH purastAt prasthitayAjyAnAM.
     rohitaM vai nAmaitac chando yat pArucchepam.
     etena vA #indraH sapta svargA~Ml ]okAn arohad
|p2  rohati sapta svargA~Ml lokan ya evaM veda
|p3  tad Ahur:
     yat pa~NcapadA eva pa~NcamasyAhno rUpaM ShaTpadAH ShaShThasyAtha
     kasmAt saptapadAH ShaShThe 'ha~N chasyanta iti
|p4  ShaDbhir eva padaiH ShaShTham ahar Apnuvanty apachidyevaitad ahar
     yat saptamaM, tad eva saptamena padenAbhyArabhya vasanti.
     vAcam eva tat punar upayanti, saMtatyai
|p5  saMtatais tryahair avyavachinnair yanti ya evaM vidvAMso yanti

|c11
|p1  devAsurA vA eShu lokeShu samayatanta.
     te vai devAH ShaShThenaivAhnaibhyo lokebhyo 'surAn prANudanta.
     teShAM yAny antarhastInAni vasUny AsaMs, tAny AdAya samudram praupyanta.
     ta etenaiva chandasAnuhAyAntarhastInAni vasUny Adadata.
     tad yad etat padam punaHpadaM, sa evA.Nkusha Asa~NjanAyA/dviShato
|p2  vasu datte, nir enam ebhyaH sarvebhyo lokebhyo nudate,
     ya evaM veda

|c12
|p1  dyaur vai devatA ShaShTham ahar vahati,
     trayastriMshaH stomo raivataM sAmAtichandAsh chando.
     yathAdevatam enena yathAstomaM yathAsAma yathAchandasaM rAdhnoti
     ya evaM veda
|p2  yad vai samAnodarkaM, tat ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM.
     yad dhy eva tR^itIyam ahas tad etat punar yat ShaShThaM.
     yad ashvavad yad antavad yat punarAvR^ittaM yat punarninR^ittaM
     yad ratavad yat paryastavad yat trivad yad antarUpaM,
     yad uttame pade devatA nirucyate, yad asau loko 'bhyudito
|p3  yat pArucchepaM yat saptapadaM yan nArAshaMsaM
     yan nAbhAnediShThaM yad raivataM yad atichandA
     yat kR^itaM yat tR^itIyasyAhno rUpaM:
     etAni vai ShaShThasyAhno rUpANy
|p4  ayaM jAyata manuSho dharImaNIti ShaShThasyAhna Ayam bhavati
     pArucchepam atichandAH saptapadaM ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p5  stIrNam barhir upa no yAhI vitaya, A vAM ratho niyutvAn vakShad avase,
     suShumA yAtam adribhir, yuvAM stomebhir devayanto ashvinA,var maha indra,
     vR^iShann indrA,stu shrauSha.l, o ShU No agne shR^iNuhi tvam I.lito,
     ye devAso divy ekAdasha sthe,yam adadAd rabhasam R^iNacyutam iti
     pra:ugam pArucchepam atichandAH
     saptapadaM ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p6  sa pUrvyo mahAnAm iti marutvatIyasya pratipad.
     anto vai mahad, antaH ShaShTham ahaH
     ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p7  traya indrasya somA, indra nedIya ed ihi, pra nUnam brahmaNas patir,
     agnir netA, tvaM soma kratubhiH, pinvanty apo,
     nakiH sudAso ratham iti tR^itIyenAhnA samAna AtAnaH
     ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p8  yaM tvaM ratham indra medhasAtaya iti
     sUktam pArucchepam atichandAH saptapadaM
     ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p9  sa yo vR^iShA vR^iShNyebhiH samokA iti sUktaM samAnodarkaM
     ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpam
|p10  indra marutva iha pAhi somam iti sUktaM,
     tebhiH sAkam pibatu vR^itrakhAda ity:
     anto vai khAdo, 'ntaH ShaShTham ahaH
     ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p11  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavate
|p12  'yaM ha yena vA idam iti paryAsaH,
     svar marutvatA jitam ity:
     anto vai jitam, antaH ShaShTham ahaH
     ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p13  tA u gAyatryo.
     gAyatryo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinaM vahanti.
     tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAd gAyatrIShu nividaM dadhAti
|p14  revatIr naH sadhamAde, revA~M id revata stoteti raivatam pR^iShTham bhavati.
     bArhate 'hani ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p15  yad vAvAneti dhAyyAcyutA
|p16  tvAm id dhi havAmaha iti bR^ihato yonim anu nivartayati.
     bArhataM hy etad ahar Ayatanene/ndram
|p17  id devatAtaya iti sAmapragAtho ninR^ittavAn
     ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p18  tyam U Shu vAjinaM devajUtam iti tArkShyo 'cyutaH

|c13
|p1  endra yAhy upa naH parAvata iti sUktam pArucchepam atichandAH
     saptapadaM ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpam
|p2  pra ghA nv asya mabato mahAnIti sUktaM
     samAnodarkaM ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpam
|p3  abhUr eko rayipate rayINAm iti sUktaM,
     ratham A tiShTha tuvinR^imNa bhImam ity:
     anto vai sthitam, antaH ShaShTham ahaH ShaShThe 'hani ShasThasyAhno rUpaM
|p4  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyAvata
|p5  upa no haribhiH sutam iti paryAsaH
     samAnodarkaH ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p6  tA u gAyatryo.
     gAyAtryo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinam vahanti.
     tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAd gAyatrIShu nividaM dadhAty
|p7  abhi tyaM devaM savitAram oNyor iti vaishvadevasya pratipad
     atichandAH ShAShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p8  tat savitur vareNyaM, doSho AgAd ity anucaro.
     'nto vai gatam, antaH ShaShTham ahaH ShasThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpam
|p9  ud u Shya devaH savitA savAyeti sAvitraM,
     shashvattamaM tadapA vahnir asthAd ity:
     anto vai sthitam, antaH ShaShTham ahaH ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p10  katarA pUrvA katarAparAyor iti dyAvApR^ithivIyaM
     samAnodarkaM ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p11  kim u shreShThaH kiM yaviShTho na Ajagann,
     upa no vAjA adhvaram R^ibhukShA ity ArbhavaM nArAshaMsaM
     trivat ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpam
|p12  idam itthA raudraM gUrtavacA,
     ye yaj~Nena dakShiNayA samaktA iti vaishvadevam

|c14
|p1  #nAbhAnediShThaM shaMsati
|p2  #nAbhAnediShThaM vai #mAnavam brahmacaryaM vasantam bhrAtaro nirabhajan.
     so 'bravId etya:
     kim mahyam abhAktety. etam eva niShThAvam avavaditAram ity abruvaMs.
     tasmAd dhApy etarhi pitaram putrA:
     niShThAvo 'vavaditety evAcakShate
|p3  sa pitaram etyAbravIt:
     tvAM ha vAva mahyam tatAbhAkShur iti.
     tam pitAbravIn:
     mA putraka tad AdR^ithA.
     #a.Ngiraso vA ime svargAya lokAya satram Asate,
     te ShaShThaM-ShaShTham evAhar Agatya muhyanti.
     tAn ete sUkte ShaShThe 'hani shaMsaya,
     teShAM yat sahasraM satrapariveShaNaM tat te svar yanto dAsyantIti. tatheti
|p4  tAn upait:
     prati gR^ibhNIta mAnavaM sumedhasa iti.
     tam abruvan:
     kiMkAmo vadasItI,dam eva vaH ShaShTham ahaH praj~NApayAnIty abravId,
     atha yad va etat sahasraM satrapariveShaNaM tan me svar yanto dattehi.
     tatheti. tAn ete sUkte ShaShThe 'hani ashaMsayat,
     tato vai te pra yaj~Nam ajAnan pra svargaM lokaM
|p5  tad yad ete sUkte ShaShThe 'hani shaMsati,
     yaj~Nasya praj~NAtyai svargasya lokasyAnukhyAtyai
|p6  taM svar yanto 'bruvann:
     etat te brAhmaNa sahasram iti.
     tad enaM samAkurvANam puruShaH kR^iShNashavAsy uttarata upotthAyAbravIn:
     mama vA idam, mama vai vAstuham iti.
     so 'bravIn:
     mahyaM vA idam adur iti.
     tam abravIt:
     tad vai nau tavaiva pitari prashna iti.
     sa pitaram ait, tam pitAbravIn:
     nanu te putrakAdU+r ity.
     adur eva ma, ity abravIt,
     tat tu me puruShah kR^iShNashavAsy uttarata upodatiShThan:
     mama vA idam, mama vai vAstuham ity aditeti.
     tam pitAbravIt:
     tasyaiva putraka, tat-tat tu sa tubhyaM dAsyatIti.
     sa punar etyAbravIt:
     tava ha vAva kila bhagava idam iti me pitAheti.
     so 'bravIt:
     tad ahaM tubhyam eva dadAmi ya eva satyam avAdIr iti
|p7  tasmAd evaM viduShA satyam eva vaditavyaM
|p8  sa eSha sahasrasanir mantro yan nAbhAnediShTha
|p9  upainaM sahasraM namati,
     pra ShaShThenAhnA svargaM lokaM jAnAti ya evaM veda

|c15
|p1  tAny etAni sahacarANy ity AcakShate:
     nAbhAnediShThaM vAlakhilyA vR^iShAkapim evAyamarutaM, tAni sahaiva shaMsed
|p2  yad eShAm antariyAt, tad yajamAnasyAntariyAd
|p3  yadi nAbhAnediShThaM reto 'syAntariyAd,
     yadi vAlakhilyAH prANAn asyAntariyAd,
     yadi vR^iShAkapim AtmAnam asyAntariyAd,
     yady evayAmarutam prahShThAyA enaM cyAvayed daivyai ca mAnuShyai ca
|p4  nAbhAnediShThenaiva reto 'si~Ncat, tad vAlakhilyAbhir vyakarot,
     #sukIrtinA #kAkShIvatena yoniM vyahApayad:
     urau yathA tava sharman mademeti.
     tasmAj jyAyAn san garbhaH kanIyAMsaM santam yoniM na hinasti,
     brahmaNA hi sa k.lpta.
     evayAmarutaitavai karoti, tenedaM sarvam etavai kR^itam eti
     yad idaM kiMcA/hash
|p5  ca kR^iShNam ahar arjunaM cety AgnimArutAsya pratipad,
     ahash cAhash ceti punarAvR^ittam punarninR^ittaM
     ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpam
|p6  madhvo vo nAma mArutaM yajatrA iti mArutam bahvabhivyAhR^ityam.
     anto vai bahv, antaH ShaShTham ahaH ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p7  jAtavedase sunavAma somam iti jAtavedasyAcyutA
|p8  sa pratnathA sahasA jAyamAna iti jAtavedasyaM
     samAnodarkaM ShaShThe 'hani ShaShThasyAhno rUpaM
|p9  dhArayan-dhArayann iti shaMsati, prasraMsAd vA antasya bibhAya.
     tad yathA punarAgrantham punarnigrantham
     antam badhnIyAn mayUkhaM vAntato dhAraNAya nihanyAt,
     tAdR^ik tad yad dhArayan-dhArayann iti shaMsati saMtatyai
|p10  saMtatais tryahair avyavachinnair yanti ya evaM vidvAMso yanti yanti

|c16 {adhyAya 23, khaNDaH 1-4}
|p1  yad vA eti ca preti ca tat saptamasyAhno rUpaM
|p2  yad dhy eva prathamam ahas tad evaitat punar yat saptamaM
|p3  yad yuktavad yad rathavad yad Ashumad yai pibavad,
     yat prathame pade devatA nirucyate, yad ayaM loko 'bhyudito
|p4  yaj jAtavad yad aniruktaM
|p5  yat kariShyad ya prathamasyAhno rUpaM:
     etAni vai saptamasyAhno rUpANi
|p6  samudrAd Urmir madhumA~M ud Arad iti
     saptamasyAhna Ajyam bhavaty aniruktam saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpaM
|p7  vAg vai samudro.
     na vai vAk kShIyate, na samudraH kShIyate.
     tad yad etat saptamasyAhna Ajyam bhavati,
     yaj~NAd eva tad yaj~NaM tanvate, vAcam eva tat punar upayanti saMtatyai
|p8  saMtatais tryahair avyavachinnair yanti ya evaM vidvAMso yanty
|p9  Apyante vai stomA, Apyante chandAMsi ShaShThe 'hani.
     tad yathaivAda AjyenAvadAnAni punaH pratyabhighArayanty ayAtayAmatAyA,
     evam evaitat stomAMsh ca chandAMsi ca punaH pratyupayanty ayAtayAmatAyai
     yad etat saptamasyAhna Ajyam bhavati
|p10  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     triShTupprAtaHsavana eSha tryaha
|p11  A vAyo bhUSha shucipA upa naH, pra yAbhir yAsi dAshvAMsam ach,A
     no niyudbhiH shatinIbhir adhvaram, pra sotA jIro adhvareShv asthAd,
     ya vAyava indramAdanAso, yA vAM shataM niyuto yAH sahasram,
     pra yad vAm mitrAvaruNA spUrdhann, A gomatA nAsatyA rathen,A
     no deva shavasA yAhi shuShmin, pra vo yaj~NeShu devayanto arcan,
     pra kShodasa dhAyasA sasra eSheti pra:ugam.
     eti ca preti ca saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpaM.
     tad u traiShTubhaM. triShTupprAtaHsavana eSha tryaha
|p12  A tvA rathaM yathotaya, idaM vaso sutam andha, indra nedIya ed ihi,
     praitu brahmaNas patir, agnir netA, tvaM soma kratubhiH,
     pinvanty apaH, pra va indrAya bR^ibata iti
     prathamenAhnA samAna AtAnaH saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpaM
|p13  kayA shubhA savayasaH sanI.lA iti sUktaM,
     na jAyamAno nashate na jAta iti jAtavat
     saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpaM
|p14  tad u kayAshubhIyam.
     etad vai saMj~NAnaM saMtani sUktaM yat kayAshubhIyam.
     etena ha vA #indro 'gastyo #marutas te samajAnata.
     tad yat kayAshubhIyaM shaMsati, saMj~NAtyA eva
|p15  tad v AyuShyaM.
     tad yo 'sya priyaH syAt, kuryAd evAsya kayAshubhIyaM
|p16  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavate
|p17  tyaM su meSham mahayA svarvidam iti sUktam,
     atyaM na vAjaM havanasyadaM ratham iti rathavat
     saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpaM
|p18  tad u jAgataM.
     jagatyo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinaM vahanti.
     tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAj jagatIShu nividaM dadhAti
|p19  mithunAni sUktAni shasyante traiShTubhAni ca jAgatAnI ca.
     mithunaM vai pashavaH pashavash chandomAH, pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p20  tvAm id dhi havAmahe,
     tvaM hy ehi cerava iti bR^ihatpR^iShTham bhavati saptame 'hani
|p21  yad eva ShaShThasyAhnas tad
|p22  yad vai rathaMtaraM tad vairUpaM yad bR^ihat tad vairAjaM,
     yad rathaMtaraM tac chAkvaraM yad bR^ihat tad raivataM
|p23  tad yad bR^ihatpR^iShTham bhavati,
     bR^ihataiva tad bR^ihat pratyuttabhnuvanty astomakR^intatrAya
|p24  yad rathaMtaraM syAt, kR^intatraM syAt
|p25  tasmAd bR^ihad eva kartavyaM
|p26  yad vAvAneti dhAyyAcyutA/bhi
|p27  tvA shUra nonuma iti rathaMtarasya yonim anu nivartayati.
     rAthaMtaraM hy etad ahar Ayatanena
|p28  pibA sutasya rasina iti sAmapragAthaH
     pibavAn saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpam
|p29  tyam U Shu vAjinaM devajUtam iti tArkShyo 'cyutaH

|c17
|p1  #indrasya nu vIryANi pra vocam iti sUktam.
     preti saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpaM
|p2  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavate
|p3  'bhi tyam meSham puruhUtam R^igmiyam iti suktaM.
     yad vAva preti tad abhIti saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpaM
|p4  tad u jAgataM.
     jagatyo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinaM vahanti.
     tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAj jagatIShu nividaM dadhAti
|p5  mithunAni sUktAni shasyante traiShTubhAni ca jAgatAni ca.
     mithunaM vai pashavaH pashavash chandomAH pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p6  tat savitur vR^iNImahe,
     'dyA no deva savitar iti vaishvadevasya pratipadanucarau.
     rAthaMtare 'hani saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpam
|p7  abhi tvA deva savitar iti sAvitraM.
     yad vAva preti tad abhIti saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpam
|p8  pretAM yaj~Nasya shambhuveti dyAvApR^ithivIyam.
     preti saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpam
|p9  ayaM devAya janmana ity ArbhavaM jAtavat
     saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpam
|p10  A yAhI vanasA saheti dvipadAH shaMsati.
     dvipAd vai puruShash catuShpAdAH pashavaH pashavash chandomAH,
     pashUnAm avaruddhyai.
     tad yad dvipadAH shaMsati,
     yajamAnam eva tad dvipratiShThaM catuShpAtsu pashuShu pratiShThApayaty
|p11  aibhir agne duvo gira iti vaishvadevam.
     eti saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpaM
|p12  tAny u gAyatrANi.
     gAyatratR^itIyasavana eSha tryaho
|p13  vaishvAnaro AjIjanad ity AgnimArutasya pratipaj.
     jAtavat saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpam
|p14  pra yat vas triShTubham iSham iti mArutam.
     preti saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpaM
|p15  jAtavedase sunavAma somam iti jAtavedasyAcyutA
|p16  dUtaM vo vishvavedasam iti jAtavedasyam
     aniruktaM saptame 'hani saptamasyAhno rUpaM
|p17  tAny u gAyatrAni.
     gAyatratR^itIyasavana eSha tryahaH

|c18
|p1  yad vai neti na preti yat sthitaM,
     tad aShTamasyAhno rUpaM
|p2  yad dhy eva dvitIyam ahas tad evaitat punar yad aShTamaM
|p3  yad Urdhvavad yat prativad yad antarvad yad vR^iShaNvad yad vR^idhanvad,
     yan madhyame pade devatA nirucyate, yad antarikSham abhyuditaM
|p4  yad dvyagni yan mahadvad yad dvihUtavad yat punarvad yat kurvad
|p5  yad dvitIyasyAhno rUpaM:
     etAni vA aShTamasyAhno rUpANy
|p6  agniM vo devam agnibhiH sajoShA ity aShTamasyAhna Ajyam bhavati
     dvyagny aShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpam
|p7  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     triShTupprAtaHsavana eSha tryahaH
|p8  kuvid a.Nga namasA ye vR^idhAsaH,
   =pIvoannA~M rayivR^idhaH sumedhA, uchann uShasaH sudinA ariprA,
     ushantA dUtA na dabhAya gopA, yAvat taras tanvo yAvad ojaH,
     prati vAM sUra udite sUktair, dhenuH pratnasya kAmyaM duhAnA,
     brahmA NA indropa yAhi vidvAn, Urdhvo agniH sumatiM vasvo ashred,
     uta syA naH sarasvatI juShANeti pra:ugam prativad antarvad dvihUtavad
     Urdhvavad aShTame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpaM
|p9  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     triShTupprAtaHsavana eSha tryaho
|p10  vishvAnarasya vas patim, indra it somapA eka, indra nedIya ed ihy,
     ut tiShTha brahmaNas pate, 'gnir netA, tvaM soma kratubhiH,
     pinvanty apo, bR^ihad indrAya gAyateti dvitIyenAhnA samAna
     AtAno 'ShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpam
|p11  shaMsA mahAm indraM yasmin vishvA iti sUktam
     mahadvad aShTame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpam
|p12  mahash cit tvam indra yata etAn iti sUktam
     mahadvad aShTame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpam
|p13  pibA somam abhi yam ugra tarda iti sUktam,
     UrvaM gavyam mahi gR^iNAna indreti
     mahadvad aShTame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpam
|p14  mahA~M indro nR^ivad A carShaNiprA iti sUktam
     mahadvad aShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpaM
|p15  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavate
|p16  tam asya dyAvApR^ithivI sacetaseti sUktaM,
     yad ait kR^iNvAno mahimAnam indriyam iti
     mahadvad aShTame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpam
|p17  tad u jAgataM.
     jagatyo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinaM vahanti.
     tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAj jagatIShu nividaM dadhAti
|p18  mithunAni sUktAni shasyante traiShTubhAni ca jAgatAni ca.
     mithunaM vai pashavaH pashavash chandomAH, pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p19  mahadvanti sUktAni shasyante.
     mahad vA antarikSham, antarikShasyAptyai
|p20  pa~Nca sUktAni shasyante.
     pa~NcapadA pa.NktiH pA.Nkto yaj~NaH pA.NktAH pashavaH pashavash chandomAH,
     pashUnAm avaruddhyA
|p21  abhi tvA shUra nonumo, 'bhi tvA pUrvapItaya iti
     rathaMtaram pR^iShTham bhavaty aShTame 'hani
|p22  yad vAvAneti dhAyyAcyutA
|p23  tvAm id dhi havAmaha iti bR^ihato yonim anu nivartayati.
     bArhataM hy etad ahar Ayataneno/bhayaM
|p24  shR^iNavac ca na iti sAmapragAtho.
     yac cedam adya yad u ca hya AsId iti bArhate 'hany
     aShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpaM
|p25  tyam UShu vAjinaM devajUtam iti tArkShyo 'cyutaH

|c19
|p1  apUrvyA purutamAny asmA iti sUktam, mahe vIrAya tavase turAyeti
     mahadvad aShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpaM.
     tAM su te kIrtim maghavan mahitveti sUktam
     mahadvad aShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpaM.
     tvam mahA~M indra yo ha shuShmair iti sUktam
     mahadvad aShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpaM.
     tvam mahA~M indra tubhyaM ha kShA iti sUktam
     mahadvad aShTame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpam
|p2  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavate
|p3  divash cid asya varimA vi papratha iti sUktam, indraM na mahneti
     mahadvad aShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpam
|p4  tad u jAgatAM.
     jagatyo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinaM vahanti.
     tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAj jagatIShu nividaM dadhAti
|p5  mithunAni sUktAni shasyante traiShTubhAni ca jAgatAni ca.
     mithunaM vai pashavaH pashavash chandomAH, pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p6  mahadvanti sUktAni shasyante.
     mahad vA antarikSham, antarikShasyAptyai.
     pa~Nca-pa~Nca sUktAni shasyante.
     pa~NcapadA pa.NktiH pA.Nkto yaj~NaH pA.NktAH pashavaH pashavash chandomAH,
     pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p7  tAni dvedhA, pa~NcAnyAni pa~NcAnyAni, dasha sampadyante:
     sA dashinI virA.l.
     annam virA.l annam pashavah pashavash chandomAH, pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p8  vishvo devasya netus, tat savitur vareNyam,
     A vishvadevaM satpatim iti vaishvadevasya pratipadanucarau.
     bArhate 'hani aShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpaM
|p9  hiraNyapANim Utaya iti sAvitram
     Urdhvavad aShTame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpam
|p10  mahI dyauH pR^ithivI ca na iti dyAvApR^ithivIyam
     mahadvad aShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpaM
|p11  yuvAnA pitarA punar ity Arbhavam
     punarvad aShTame 'hani aShTamasyAhno rUpam
|p12  imA nu kam bhuvanA sIShadhAmeti dvipadAH shaMsati.
     dvipAd vai puruShash catuShpAdAH pashavaH pashavash chandomAH,
     pashUnAm avaruddhyai.
     tad yad dvipadAH shaMsati,
     yajamAnam eva tad dvipratiShThaM catuShpAtsu pashuShu pratiShThApayati
|p13  devAnAm id avo mahad iti vaishvadevam
     mahadvad aShTame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpaM
|p14  tAny u gAyatrANi.
     gAyatratR^itIyasavana eSha tryaha
|p15  R^itAvAnaM vaishvAnaram ity AgnimArutasya pratipad,
     agnir vaishvAnaro mahAn iti
     mahadvad aShTame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpaM
|p16  krI.laM vaH shardho mArutam iti mArutaM,
     jambhe rasasya vAvR^idha iti
     vR^idhanvad aShTame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpaM
|p17  jAtavedase sunavAma somam iti jAtavedasyAcyutA/gne
|p18  mR^i.la mahA~M asIti jAtavedasyam
     mahadvad aShtame 'hany aShTamasyAhno rUpaM
|p19  tAny u gAyatrANi.
     gAyatratR^itIyasavana eSha tryaha eSha tryahaH

|c20 {adhyAya 24, khaNDaH 1-6}
|p1  yad vai samAnodarkaM, tan navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p2  yad dhy eva tR^itIhyam ahas tad evaitat punar yau navamaM
|p3  yad ashvavad yad antavad yat punarAvR^ittaM yat punarninR^ittaM
     yad ratavad yat paryastavad yat trivad yad antarUpaM,
     yad uttame pade devatA nirucyate, yad asau loko 'bhyudito
|p4  yac chucivad yat satyavad yat kShetivad yad gatavad yad okavad
|p5  yat kR^itaM yat tR^itIyasyAhno rUpam:
     etAni vai navamasyAhno rUpANy
|p6  aganma mahA namasA yaviShTham iti navamasyAhna Ajyam bhavati
     gatavan navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p7  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     triShTupprAtaHsavana eSha tryahaH
|p8  pra vIrayA shucayo dadrire te, te satyena manasA dIdhyAnA,
     divi kShayantA rajasaH pR^ithivyAm, A vishvavArAshvinA gataM no,
     'yaM soma indra tubhyaM sunva A tu, pra brahmANo a.Ngiraso nakShanta,
     sarasvatIM devayanto havanta, A no divo bR^ihataH parvatAd A,
     sarasvaty abhi no neShi vasya iti
     pra:ugaM shucivat satyavat kShetivad gatavad
     okavan navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p9  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     triShTupprAtaHsavana eSha tryahas
|p10  taM-tam id rAdhase mahe, traya indrasya somA, indra nedIya ed ihi,
     pra nUnam brahmaNas patir, agnir netA, tvaM somA kratubhiH, pinvanty apo,
     nakiH sudAso ratham iti tR^itIyenAhnA samAna
     AtAno navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpam
|p11  indraH svAhA pibatu yasya soma iti sUktam.
     anto vai svAhAkAro, 'nto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p12  gAyat sAma nabhanyaM yathA ver iti sUktam,
     arcAma tad vAvR^idhAnaM svarvad ity:
     anto vai svar, anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p13  tiShThA harI ratha A yujyamAneti sUktam.
     anto vai sthitam, anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpam
|p14  imA u tvA purutamasya kAror iti sUktaM, dhiyo ratheShThAm ity:
     anto vai sthitam, anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p15  tad u traiShTubhaM.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavate
|p16  pra mandine pitumad arcatA vaca iti sUktam
     samAnodarkaM navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p17  tad u jAgataM.
     jagatyo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinaM vahanti.
     tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivld dhIyate.
     tasmAj jagatIShu nividaM dadhAti
|p18  mithunAni sUktAni sasyante traiShTubhAni ca jAgatAni ca.
     mithunaM vai pashavaH pashavash chandomAH, pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p19  pa~NcA sUktAni shasyante.
     pa~NcapadA pa.NktiH pA.Nkto yaj~NaH pA.NktAH pashavaH pashavash chandomAH,
     pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p20  tvAm id dhi havAmahe,
     tvaM hy ehi cerava iti bR^ihatpR^iShTham bhavati navame 'hani
|p21  yad vAvAneti dhAyyAcyutAbhi tvA shUra nonuma iti
     rathaMtarasya yonim anu nivartayati.
     rAthaMtaraM hy etad ahar Ayatanenendra tridhAtu sharaNam iti
     sAmapragAthas trivAn navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM.
     tyam U Shu vAjinaM devajUtam iti tArkShyo 'cyutaH

|c21
|p1  saM ca tve jagmur gira indra pUrvIr iti sUktaM
     gatavan navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p2  kadA bhuvan rathakShayANi brahmeTi sUktaM kShetivad antarUpaM.
     kShetIva vA antaM gatvA, navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpam
|p3  A satyo yAtu maghavA~M R^ijIShIti sUktaM
     satyavan navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpam
|p4  tat ta indriyam paramam parAcair iti sUktam.
     anto vai paramam, anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p5  tad u traiShTubham.
     tena pratiShThitapadena savanaM dAdhArAyatanAd evaitena na pracyavate
|p6  'ham bhuvaM vasunaH pUrvyas patir iti sUktam,
     ahaM dhanAni saM jayAmi shashvata ity:
     anto vai jitam, anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p7  tad u jAgataM.
     jagatyo vA etasya tryahasya madhyaMdinaM vahanti.
     tad vai vac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhIyate.
     tasmAj jagatIShu nividaM dadhAti
|p8  mithunAni sUktAni shasyante traiShTubhAni ca jAgatAni ca.
     mithunaM vai pashavaH pashavash chandomAH, pashUnAm avaruddhyai.
     pa~Nca-pa~Nca sUktAni shasyante.
     pa~NcapadA pa.NktiH pA.Nkto yaj~NaH pA.NktAH pashavaH pashavash chandomAH,
     pashUnAm avaruddhyai.
     tAni dvedhA, pa~NcAnyAni pa~NcAnyAni, dasha sampadyante:
     sA dashinI virA.l.
     annam virA.l annam pashavaH pashavash chandomAH, pashUnAm avaruddhyai
|p9  tat savitur vR^iNImahe,
     'dyA no deva savitar iti vaishvadevasya pratipadanucarau.
     rAthaMtare 'hani navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p10  doSho AgAd iti sAvitraM anto vai gatam,
     anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpam
|p11  pra vAm mahidyavI abhIti dyAvApR^ithivIyaM,
     shucI upa prashastaya iti shucivan navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpam
|p12  indra iShe dadAtu nas, te no ratnAni dhattanety ArbhavaM,
     trir A sAptAni sunvata iti trivan navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpAm
|p13  babhrur eko viShuNaH sUnaro yuveti dvipadAH shaMsati.
     dvipAd vai puruShash catuShpAdAH pashavaH pashavash chandomAh,
     pashUnAm avaruddhyai.
     tad yad dvipadAH shaMsati,
     yajamAnam eva tad dvipratiShThaM catuShpAtsu pashuShu pratiShThApayati
|p14  ye triMshati trayas para iti vaishvadevaM
     trivan navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p15  tAny u gAyatrANi.
     gAyatratR^itIyasavana eSha tryaho
|p16  vaishvAnaro na Utaya ity AgnimArutasya pratipad,
     A pra yatu parAvata ity:
     anto vai parAvato, 'nto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpam
|p17  maruto yasya hi kShaya iti mArutaM kShetivad antarUpaM.
     kShetIva vA antaM gatvA, navame 'hani navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p18  jatavedase sunavAma somam iti jAtavedasyAcyutA
|p19  prAgnaye vAcam Irayeti jAtavedasyaM
     samAnodarkaM navame 'navamasyAhno rUpaM
|p20  sa naH parShad ati dviShaH sa naH parShad ati dviSha iti saMsah.
     bahu vA etasmin navarAtre kiMca-kiMca vAraNaM kriyate, shAntyA eva.
     tad yat:
     sa naH parShad ati dviShaH sa naH parShad ati dviSha iti shaMsati,
     sarvasmAd evainAMs tad enasaH pramu~Ncati
|p21  tAny u gAyatrANi.
     gAyatratR^itIyasavana eSha tryahaH

|c22
|p1  pR^iShThyaM Sha.laham upayanti.
     yathA vai mukham evam pR^iShThyaH Sha.lahas.
     tad yathAntaram mukhasya jihvA tAlu dantA, evaM chandomA.
     atha yenaiva vAcaM vyAkaroti yena svAdu cAsvAdu ca vijAnAti,
     tad dashamam ahar
|p2  yathA vai nAsike evam pR^iShThyaH Sha.lahas.
     tad yathAntaram nAsikayor, evaM chandomA.
     atha yenaiva gandhAn vijAnAti, tad dashamam ahar
|p3  yathA vA akShy evam pR^iShThyaH Sha.lahas.
     tad yathAntaram akShNaH kR^iShNam, evaM chandomA.
     atha yaiva kanInikA yena pashyati, tad dashamam ahar
|p4  yathA vai karNa evam pR^iShThyaH Sha.lahas.
     tad yathAntaraM karNasyaivaM chandomA.
     atha yenaiva shR^iNoti, tad dashamam ahaH
|p5  shrIr vai dashamam ahaH, shriyaM vA eta Agachanti ye dashamam ahar Agachanti.
     tasmAd dashamam ahar avivAkyam bhavati:
     mA shriyo 'vavAdiShmeti, duravavadaM hi shreyasas
|p6  te tataH sarpanti
|p7  te mArjayante
|p8  te patnIshAlAM samprapadyante
|p9  teShAM ya etAm AhutiM vidyAt, sa brUyAt:
     samanvArabhadhvam iti.
     sa juhuyAd
|p10  iha rameha ramadhvam, iha dhR^itir iha svadhR^itir,
     #agne vAT, svAhA vA.l iti
|p11  sa yad iha ramety AhAsminn evainAMs tal loke ramayatIha ramadhvam iti
     yad Aha, prajAm evaiShu tad ramayatIha dhR^itir iha svadhR^itir iti
     yad Aha, prajAM caiva tad vAcaM ca yajamAneShu dadhAty.
     #agne vA.l iti rathaMtaram, svAhA vA.l iti bR^ihad
|p12  devAnAM vA etan mithunaM yad bR^ihadrathaMtare,
     devAnAm eva tan mithunena mithunam avarundhate,
     devAnAm mithunena mithunam prajAyante prajAtyai
|p13  prajAyate prajayA pashubhir ya evaM veda
|p14  te tataH sarpanti, te mArjayante, ta AgnIdhraM samprapadyante.
     teShAM ya etAm AhutiM vidyAt, sa brUyat:
     samanvArabhadhvam iti.
     sa juhuyAd
|p15  upasR^ijan dharuNam mAtaraM dharuNo dhayan \
     rAyas poSham iSham Urjam asmAsu dIdharat svAheti
|p16  rAyas poSham iSham Urjam avarunddha Atmane ca yajamAnebhyash ca
     yatraivaM vidvAn etAm AhutiM juhoti

|c23
|p1  te tataH sarpanti, te sadaH samprapadyante.
     yathAyatham anya R^itvijo vyutsarpanti, saMsarpanty udgAtAras,
     te #sarparAj~NyA R^ikShu stuvata
|p2  iyaM vai #sarparAj~NIyaM hi sarpato rAj~NIyaM vA alomikevAgra AsIt.
     saitam mantram apashyad:
     AyaM gauH pR^ishnir akramId iti.
     tAm ayam pR^ishnir varNa Avishan nAnArUpo,
     yaM-yaM kAmam akAmayata
     yad idaM kiMcauShadhayo vanaspatayaH sarvANi rUpANi
|p3  prishnir enaM varNa Avishati nAnArUpo, yaM-yaM kAmaM kAmayate ya evaM veda
|p4  manasA prastauti manasodgAyati manasA pratiharati, vAcA shaMsati
|p5  vAk ca vai manash ca devAnAm mithunaM.
     devAnAm eva tan mithunena mithunam avarundhate,
     devAnAm mithunena mithunam prajAyante prajAtyai.
     prajAyate prajayA pashubhir ya evaM vedA/tha
|p6  caturhotRn hotA vyAcaShTe, tad eva tat stutam anushaMsati
|p7  devAnAM vA etad yaj~NiyaM guhyaM nAma yac caturhotAras.
     tad yac caturhotRn hotA vyAcaShTe,
     devAnAm eva tad yaj~NiyaM guhyaM nAma prakAshaM gamayati,
     tad enam prakAshaM gatam prakAsham gamayati.
|p8  gachati prakAshaM ya evaM veda
|p9  yam brAhmaNam anUcAnaM yasho narched,
     iti ha smAhAraNyam paretya darbhastambAn udgrathya
     dakShiNato brahmANam upaveshya caturhotRn vyAcakShIta
|p10  devAnAM vA etad yaj~NiyaM guhyaM nAma yac caturhotAras.
     tad yac caturhotRn vyAcakShIta,
     devAnAm eva tad yaj~NiyaM guhyaM nAma prakAshaM gamayati,
     tad enam prakAshaM gatam prakAshaM gamayati.
     gachati prakAshaM ya evaM veda

|c24
|p1  athaudumbarIM samanvArabhanta
|p2  iSham Urjam anvArabha ity

     tasmAt sa triH saMvatsarasya pacyate

     iSham eva tad Urjam annAdyaM samanvArabhante

     vAg vai yaj~No, yaj~Nam eva tad yachanty

     ahar vai svargo lokaH, svargam eva tal lokaM niyachanti

     yad divA vAcaM visR^ijerann, ahar bhrAtR^ivyAya parishiMShyur

     yaj~Nenaiva tat svargeNa lokena svargaM lokaM yanti
|p13  yad ihonam akarma yad atyarIricAma \
     #prajApatiM tat pitaram apyetv iti vAcaM visR^ijante
|p14  #prAjapatiM vai prajA anuprajAyante,
     #prajApatir UnAtiriktayoH pratiShThA, nainAn UnAM nAtiriktaM hinasti

|c25
|p1  adhvaryo ity Ahvayate caturhotR^iShu vadiShyamANas, tad AhAvasya rUpam
|p2  oM hotas tathA hotar ity
     adhvaryuH pratigR^iNAty avasite-'vasite dashasu padeShu
|p3  teShAM cittiH srug AsI+t \

     yAM devAH prajApatigR^ihapataya R^iddhim arAdhnuvaMs tAm R^iddhiM rAtsyAmo
|p14  'tha #prajApates tanUr anudravati brahmodyaM cA/nnAdA
|p15  cAnnapatnI cAnnAdA tad #agnir, annapatnI tad #Adityo
|p16  bhadrA ca kalyANI cA.
     bhadrA tat #somaH, kalyANI tat pashAvo
|p17  'nilayA cApabhayA cAnilayA tad #vAyur, na hy eSha kadA canelayaty.
     apabhayA tan mR^ityuH, sarvaM hy etasmAd bIbhAyA/nAptA
|p18  cAnApyA cAnAptA tat pR^ithivy, anApyA tad dyaur
|p19  anAdhR^iShyA cApratidhR^iShyA cAnAdhR^iShyA tad #agnir, apratidhR^iShyA tad #Adityo
|p20  'pUrvA cAbhrAtR^ivyA cApUrvA tan mAno, 'bhrAtR^ivyA tat saMvatsara
|p21  etA vAva dvAdasha #prajApates tanva, eSha kR^itsnaH #prajApatis.
     tat kR^itsnam #prajApatim Apnoti dashamam ahar
|p22  atha brahmodyam vadanty.
     #agnir gR^ihapatir iti haika AhuH, so 'sya lokasya gR^ihapatir.
     #vAyur gR^ihapatir iti haika AhuH, so 'ntarikShalokasya gR^ihapatir.
     asau vai gR^ihapatir yo 'sau tapaty.
     eSha patir, R^itavo gR^ihA.
     yeShAM vai gR^ihapatiM devaM vidvAn gR^ihapatir bhavati,
     rAdhnoti sa gR^ihapatiM, rAdhnuvanti te yajamAnA.
     yeShAM vA apahatapApmAnaM devaM vidvAn gR^ihapatir bhavaty,
     apa sa gR^ihapatiH pApmAnaM hate, 'pa te yajamAnAH pApmAnaM ghnate.
     'dhvaryo arAtsmArAtsma

|c26 {adhyAya 25, khaNDaH 1-9}
|p1  uddharAhavanIyam ity aparAhNa Aha.
     yad evAhnA sAdhu karoti, tad eva tat prA.N uddhR^itya tadabhaye nidhatta

   yad eva rAtryA sAdhu karoti, tad eva tat prA.N uddhR^itya tadabhaye nidhatte
|p3  yaj~No vA AhavanIyaH, svargo loka AhavanIyo
|p4  yaj~Na eva tat svarge loke svargaM lokaM nidhatte ya evaM veda

     vaishvadevenAgnihotreNa Sho.lashakalena pashuShu pratiShThitena rAdhnoti

|c28
|p1  asau vA asyAdityo yUpaH, pR^ithivI vedir, oShadhayo barhir,

|c29
|p1  #vR^iShashuShmo ha #vAtAvata uvAca #jAtUkarNyo:

   yad vai tad agnihotram ubhayedyur ahUyatAnyedur vAva tad etarhi hUyata ity

|c30
|p1  ete ha vai saMvatsarasya cakre yad ahorAtre,
     tAbhyAm eva tat saMvatsaram eti sa yo 'nudite juhoti,
     yathaikatashcakreNa yAyAt tAdR^ik tad.
     atha ya udite juhoti,
     yathobhayatashcakreNa yAn kShipram adhvAnaM samashnvIta tAdR^ik tat
|p2  tad eShAbhi yaj~NagAthA gIyate
|p3      bR^ihadrathaMtarAbhyAm idam eti yuktaM
         yad bhUtaM bhaviShyac cApi sarvam \
         tAbhyAm iyAd agnIn AdhAya dhIro
         divaivAnyaj juhuyAn naktam anyad
     iti
|p4  rAthamtarI vai rAtry, ahar bArhatam.
     #agnir kai rathaMtaram #Adityo bR^ihad,
     ete ha vA enaM devate bradhnasya viShTapaM svargaM lokaM gamayato
     ya evaM vidvAn udite juhoti.
     tasmAd udite hotavyaM
|p5  tad eShAbhi yaj~NagAthA gIyate
|p6
          yathA ha vA sthUriNaikena yAyAd
         akR^itvAnyad upayojanAya \
         evaM yanti te bahavo janAsaH
         purodayAj juhvati ye 'gnihotram
     iti
|p7  tAM vA etAM devatAm prayatIM sarvam idam anupraiti
     yad idaM kiMcaitasyai hIdaM devatAyA anucaraM sarvaM
     yad idaM kiMca, saiShAnucaravatI devatA
|p8  vindate ha vA anucaram, bhavaty asyAnucaro ya evaM veda
|p9  sa vA eSha ekAtithiH, sa eSha juhvatsu vasati
|p10  tad yad ado gAthA bhavaty
|p11
          anenasam enasA so 'bhishastAd
         enasvato vApaharAd enaH
         ekAtithim apa sAyaM ruNaddhi
         bisAni steno apa so jahArety
|p12  eSha ha vai sa ekAtithiH, sa eSha juhvatsu vasaty.
     etaM vAva sa devatAm aparuNaddhi,
     yo 'lam agnihotrAya san nAgnihotraM juhoti.
     tam eShA devatAparoddhAparuNaddhy asmAc ca lokAd amuShmAc cobhAbhyAM,
     yo 'lam agnihotrAya san nAgnihotraM juhoti
|p13  tasmAd yo 'lam agnihotrAya syAj juhuyAt
|p14  tasmAd Ahur:
     na sAyam atithir aparudhya ity
|p15  etad dha sma vai tad vidvAn #nagarI #jAnashruteya
     uditahominam #aikAdashAkSham #mAnutantavyam uvAca:
     prajAyAm enaM vij~NAtA smo yadi vidvAn vA juhoty avidvAn veti.
     tasyo haikAdashAkShe rAShTram iva prajA babhUva.
     rAShTram iva ha vA asya prajA bhavati ya evaM vidvAn udite juhoti.
     tasmAd udite hotavyam

|c31
|p1  udyann u khalu vA #Aditya AhavanIyena rashmIn saMdadhAti.
     sa yo 'nudite juhoti,
     yathA kumArAya vA vatsAya vAjAtAya stanam pratidadhyAt tAdR^ik tad.
     atha ya udite juhoti,
     yathA kumArAya vA vatsAya vA jAtAya stanam pratidadhyAt tAdR^ik tat.
     tam asmai pratidhIyamAnam ubhayor lokayor annAdyam anu pratidhIyate
     'smAc ca lokAd amuShmac cobhAbhyAM
|p2  sa yo 'nudite juhoti,
     yathA puruShAya vA hastine vAprayate hasta AdadhyAt tAdrik tad.
     atha ya udite juhoti,
     yathA puruShAya vA hastine vA prayate hasta AdadhyAt tAdR^ik tat.
     tam eSha etenaiva hastenordhvaM hR^itvA svarge loka AdadhAti
     ya evaM vidvAn udite juhoti.
     tasmAd udite hotavyam
|p3  udyann u khalu vA #AdityaH sarvANi bhUtAni praNayati,
     tasmAd enam prANa ity AcakShate.
     prANe hAsya samprati hutam bhavati ya evaM vidvAn udite juhoti.
     tasmAd udite hotavyam
|p4  eSha ha vai satyaM vadan satye juhoti,
     yo 'stamite sAyaM juhoty udite prAtar.
     bhUr bhuvaH svar o+m #agnir jyotir jyotir #agnir iti sAyaM juhoti,
     bhUr bhuvaH svar o+M #sUryo jyotir jyotiH #sUrya iti prAtaH.
     satyaM hAsya vadataH satye hutam bhavati ya evaM vidvAn udite juhoti.
     tasmAd udite hotavyaM
|p5  tad eShAbhi yaj~NagAthA gIyate
|p6
          pratAH-prAtar anR^itaM te vadanti
         purodayAj juhvati ye 'gnihotram \
         divA kIrtyam adivA kIrtayantaH
         #sUryo jyotir na tadA jyotir eShAm
     iti

|c32
|p1  #prajApatir akAmayata:
     prajAyeya bhUyAn syAm iti.
     sa tApo 'tapyata, sa tapas taptvemA~Ml lokAn asR^ijata:
     pR^ithivIm antarikShaM divaM.
     tA~Ml lokAn abhyatapat,
     tebhyo 'bhitaptebhyas trINi jyotIMShy ajAyantAgnir eva pR^ithivyA ajAyata,
     #vAyur antarikShAd, #Adityo divas.
     tAni jyotIMShy abhyatapat, tebhyo 'bhitaptebhyas trayo vedA ajAyanta:
     R^igveda evAgner ajAyata, yajurvedo #vAyoH sAmaveda #AdityAt.
     tAn vedAn abhyatapat, tebhyo 'bhitaptebhyas trINi shukrANy ajAyanta:
     bhUr ity eva R^igvedAd ajAyata, bhuva iti yajurvedAt, svar iti sAmavedAt
|p2  tAni shukrANy abhyatapat,
     tebhyo 'bhitaptebhyas trayo varNA ajAyantAkAra ukAro makAra iti.
     tAn ekadhA samabharat, tad etad o+m iti.
     tasmAd om-om iti praNauty.
     om iti vai svargo loka, om ity asau yo 'sau tapati
|p3  sa #prajApatir yaj~Nam atanuta, tam Aharat, tenAyajata.
     sa R^icaiva hautram akarod, yajuShAdhvaryavaM sAmnodgIthaM.
     yad etat trayyai vidyAyai shukraM, tena brahmatvam akarot
|p4  sa #prajApatir yaj~NaM devebhyaH samprAyachat,
     te devA yaj~Nam atanvata, tam Aharanta, tenAyajanta.
     ta R^icaiva hautram akurvan, yajuShAdhvaryavaM, sAmnodgIthaM.
     yad evaitat trayyai vidyAyai shukraM, tena brahmatvam akurvaMs
|p5  te devA abruvan #prajApatiM:
     yadi no yaj~Na R^ikta ArtiH syAd yadi yajuShTo yadi sAmato yady
     avij~NAtA sarvavyApad vA, kA prAyashcittir iti.
     sa #prajApatir abravId devAn:
     yadi vo yaj~Na R^ikta Artir bhavati, bhUr iti gArhapatye juhavAtha;
     yadi yajuShTo, bhuva ity AgnIdhrIye 'nvAhAryapacane vA haviryaj~NeShu;
     yadi sAmataH, svar ity AhavanIye;
     yady avij~NAtA sarvavyApad vA,
     bhUr bhuvaH svar iti sarvA anudrutyAhavanIya eva juhavAthety
|p6  etAni ha vai vedAnAm antaHshleShaNAni yad etA vyAhR^itayas.
     tad yathAtmanAtmAnaM saMdadhyAd,
     yathA parvaNA parva yathA shleShmaNA carmaNyaM vAnyad
     vA vishliShTam saMshleShayed:
     evam evaitAbhir yaj~Nasya vishliShTaM saMdadhAti.
     saiShA sarvaprAyashcittir yad etA vyAhR^itayas,
     tasmAd eShaiva yaj~Ne prAyashcittiH kartavyA

|c33
|p1  tad Ahur mahAvadA+H \
     yad R^icaiva hautraM kriyate yajuShAdhvaryavaM sAmnodgIthaM,
     vyArabdhA trayI vidyA bhavaty:
     atha kena brahmatvaM kriyata iti.
     trayyA vidyayeti brUyAd
|p2  ayaM vai yaj~No yo 'yam pavate.
     tasya vAk ca manash ca vartanyau, vAcA ca hi manasA ca yaj~No vartata.
     iyaM vai vAg ado manas,
     tad vAcA trayyA vidyayaikam pakShaM saMskurvanti,
     manasaiva brahmA saMskaroti
|p3  te haike brahmANa upAkR^ite prAtaranuvAke
     stomabhAgA~N japitvA bhAShamANA upAsate.
     tad dhaitad uvAca brAhmaNa upAkR^ite prAtaranuvAke
     brahmANam bhAShamAnaM dR^iShTvArdham asya yaj~NasyAntaragur iti.
     tad yathaikapAt puruSho yann ekatashcakro vA ratho vartamAno bhreShaM nyety,
     evam eva sa yaj~No bhreShaM nyeti,
     yaj~Nasya bhreSham anu yajamAno bhreShaM nyeti
|p4  tasmAd brahmopAkR^ite prAtarauvAke vAcaMyamaH syAd opAMshvantaryAmayor homAd,
     upAkR^iteShu pavamAneShv odR^ico.
     'tha yAni stotrANi sashastrANy, A teShAM vaShaTkArAd vAcaMyama eva syAt.
     tad yathobhayataHpAt puroSho yann ubhayatashcakro
     vA ratho vartamAno na riShyaty, evam eva sa yaj~No na riShyati,
     yaj~NasyAriShTim anu yajamAno na riShyati

|c34
|p1  tad Ahur:
     yad grahAn me 'grahIt prAcArIn ma AhutIr me 'hauShId ity
     adhvaryave dakShiNA nIyanta, udagAsIn ma ity udgAtre,
     'nvavocan me 'shaMsIn me 'yAkShIn ma iti hotre:
     kiM svid eva cakruShe brahmaNe dakShiNA nIyante,
     'kR^itvAho svid eva harantA iti
|p2  yaj~Nasya haiSha bhiShag yad brahmA,
     yaj~NAyaiva tad bheShajaM kR^itvA haraty
|p3  atho yad bhUyiShThenaiva brahmaNA chandasAM rasenArtvijyaM karoti
     yad brahmA, tasmAd brahmA,rdhabhAg gha
     vA eSha itareShAm R^itvijAm agra Asa
     yad brahmA,rdham eva brahmaNa AsArdham itareShAm R^itvijAM
|p4  tasmAd yadi yaj~Na R^ikta ArtiH syAd yadi yajuShTo yadi sAmato
     yady avij~NAtA sarvavyApad vA, brahmaNa eva nivedayante.
     tasmAd yadi yaj~Na R^ikta Artir bhavati,
     bhUr iti brahmA gArhapatye juhuyAd;
     yadi yajuShTo, bhuva ity AgnIdhrIye 'nvAhAryapacane vA haviryaj~NeShu;
     yadi sAmataH, svar ity AhavanIye;
     yady avij~NAtA sarvavyApad vA,
     bhUr bhuvaH svar iti sarvA anudrutyAhavanIya eva juhuyat
|p5  sa prastotopAkR^ite stotra Aha:
     brahman stoShyAmaH prashAstar iti.
     sa bhUr iti brahmA prAtaHsavane brUyAd, indravantaH studhvam iti,
     bhuva iti mAdhyaMdine savane brUyAd, indravantaH studhvam iti;
     svar iti tR^itIyasavane brUyAd, indravantaH studhvam iti;
     bhUr bhuvaH svar ity ukthe vAtirAtre vA brUyAd, indravantaH studhvam iti
|p6  sa yad AhendravantaH studhvam ity, aindro vai yaj~Na,
     #indro yaj~Nasya devatA.
     sendram eva tad udgIthaM karotIndrAn mA gAd, indravantaH studhvam iti
     evainAMs tad Aha tad Aha

|bAB6 {pa~NcikA 6}

|c1 {adhyAya 26, khaNDaH 1-3}
|p1  devA ha vai sarvacarau satraM niShedus, te ha pApmAnaM nApajaghnire.
     tAn hovAcArbudaH #kAdraveyaH sarpaR^iShir mantrakR^id:
     ekA vai vo hotrAkR^itA, tAM vo 'haM karavANy,
     atha pApmAnam apahaniShyadhva iti.
     te ha tathety Ucus.
     teShAM ha sma sa madhyaMdine-madhyaMdina &2 evopodAsarpan,
     grAvNo 'bhiShTauti
|p2  tasmAn madhyaMdinemadhyaMdina eva grAvNo 'bhiShTuvanti tadanukR^iti
|p3  sa ha &2 <sma> yenopodAsarpat,
     tad dhApy etarhy #arbudodAsarpaNI nAma prapad asti
|p4  tAn ha rAjA madayAM cakAra, te hocur:
     AshIviSho vai no rAjAnam avekShate,
     hantAsyoShNISheNAkShyAv apinahyAmeti. tatheti.
     tasya hoShNISheNakShyAv &1 apinehus,
     tasmAd uShNISham eva paryasya grAvNo 'bhiShTuvanti tadanukR^iti
|p5  tAn ha rAjA madayAm eva cakAra, te hocuH:
     svena vai no mantreNa grAvNo 'bhiShTautIti,
     hantAsyAnyAbhir R^igbhir mantram ApR^inacAmeti. tatheti.
     tasya hAnyAbhir R^igbhir mantram ApapR^icus, tato hainAn na madayAM cakAra.
     tad yad asyAnyAbhir R^igbhir mantram ApR^i~Ncanti, shAntyA eva
|p6  te ha pApmAnam apajaghnire.
     teShAm anv apahatiM sarpAH pApmAnam apajaghnire,
     ta ete 'pahatapApmAno hitvA pUrvAM jIrNAM tvacaM navayaiva prayanty
|p7  apa pApmAnaM hate ya evaM veda

|c2
|p1  tad AhuH:
     kiyatIibhir abhiShTuyAd iti.
     shatenety AhuH.
     shatAyur vai puruShaH shatavIryaH shatendriya,
     AyuShy evainaM tad vIrya indriye dadhAti
|p2  &1 trayastriMshatA vety Ahus.
     trayastriMshato vai sa devAnAm pApmano 'pAhaMs,
     trayastriMshad vai tasya devA ity
|p3  aparimitAbhir abhiShTuyAd.
     aparimito vai #prajApatih.
     #prajApater vA eShA hotrA yad grAvastotrIyA,
     tasyAM sarve kAmA avarudhyante.
     sa yad aparimitAbhir abhiShTauti, sarveShAM kAmAnAm avaruddhyai
|p4  sarvAn kAmAn avarunddhe ya evaM veda
|p5  tasmAd aparimitAbhir evAbhiShTuyAt
|p6  tad AhuH:
     katham abhiShTuyAd ity.
     akSharashA+H \ caturakSharashA+H \ pacchA+H \ ardharcashA+H \ R^ikshA+H iti \
     tad yad R^iksho na tad avakalpate,
     'tha yat paccho no eva tad avakalpate,
     'tha yad akSharashash caturakSharasho vi tathA chandAMsi
     lupyeran bahUni tathAkSharANi hIyerann.
     ardharcasha evAbhiShTuyAt, pratiShThAyA eva
|p7  dvipratiShTho vai puruShash catuShpAdAH pashavo,
     yajAmanam eva tad dvipratiShThaM catuShpAtsu pashuShu pratiShThApayati.
     tasmAd ardharcasha evAbhiShTuyAt
|p8  tad Ahur:
     yan madhyaMdine-madhyaMdina eva grAvNo 'bhiShTauti,
     katham asyetarayoH savanayor abhiShTutam bhavatIti.
     yad eva gAyatrIbhir abhiShTauti, gAyatraM vai prAtaHsavanaM,
     tena prAtaHsavane;
     'tha yaj jagatIbhir abhiShTauti, jAgataM vai tR^itIyasavanaM,
     tena tR^itIyasavana
|p9  evam u hAsya madhyaMdine-madhyaMdina eva grAvNo 'bhiShTuvataH
     sarveShu savaneShv abhiShTutam bhavati ya evaM veda
|p10  tad Ahur:
     yad adhvaryur evAnyAn R^itvijaH sampreShyAty,
     atha kasmAd eSha etAm asampreShitaH pratipadyata iti.
     mano vai grAvastotrIyasampreShitaM vA idam manas,
     tasmAd eSha etAm asampreShitaH pratipadyate

|c3
|p1  vAg vai subrahmaNyA, tasyai somo rAjA vatsah.
     some rAjani krIte subrahmaNyAm Ahvayanti yathA dhenum upahvayet,
     tena vatsena yajamAnAya sarvAn kAmAn duhe
|p2  sarvAn hAsmai kAmAn vAg duhe ya evaM veda
|p3  tad AhuH:
     kiM subrahmaNyAyai subrahmaNyAtvam iti.
     vAg eveti brUyAd, vAg vai brahma ca subrahma ceti
|p4  tad Ahur:
     atha kasmAd enam pumAMsaM santaM strIm ivAcakShata iti.
     vAg ghi subrahmaNyeti brUyAt, teneti
|p5  tad Ahur:
     yad antarvedItara R^itvija ArtvijyaM kurvanti bahirvedi subrahmaNyA,
     katham asyAntarvedy ArtvijyaM kR^itam bhavatIti.
     veder vA utkaram utkiranti;
     yad evotkare tiShThann AhvayatIti brUyAt, teneti
|p6  tad Ahur:
     atha kasmAd utkare tiShThan subrahmaNyAm AhvayatIty.
     R^iShayo vai satram Asata.
     teShAM yo varShiShTha AsIt tam abruvan:
     subrahmaNyAm Ahvaya, tvaM no nediShThAd devAn hvayiShyasIti.
     varShiShTham evainaM tat kurvanty, atho vedim eva tat sarvAm prINAti
|p7  tad AhuH:
     kasmAd asmA R^iShabhaM dakShiNAm abhyAjantIti.
     vR^iShA vA R^iShabho yoShA subrahmaNyA tan mithunaM,
     tasya mithunasya prajAtyA ity
|p8  upAMshu pAtnIvatasyAgnidhro yajati.
     reto vai pAtnIvata, upAMshv iva vai retasaH siktir
|p9  nAnuvaShaTkaroti.
     saMsthA vA eShA yad anuvaShaTkAro:
     ned retaH saMsthApayAnIty.
     asaMsthitaM vai retasaH samR^iddhaM.
     tasmAn nAnuvaShaTkaroti
|p10  neShTur upastha AsIno bhakShayati.
     pantIbhAjanaM vai neShTAgniH patnIShu reto dadhAti prajAtyA,
     #agninaiva tat patnIShu reto dadhAti prajAtyai
|p11  prajAyate prajayA pashubhir ya evaM veda
|p12  dakShiNA anu subrahmaNyA saMtiShThate.
     vAg vai subrahmaNyAnnaM dakShiNAnnAdya eva
     tad vAci yaj~Nam antataH pratiShThApayanti pratiShThApayanti

|c4 {adhyAya 27, khaNDaH 1-5}
|p1  devA vai yaj~Nam atanvata, tAMs tanvAnAn asurA abhyAyan:
     yaj~Naveshasam eShAM kariShyAma iti.
     tAn dakShiNata upAyan, yata eShAM yaj~Nasya taniShTham amanyanta.
     te devAH pratibudhya #mitrAvaruNau dakShiNataH paryauhaMs,
     te #mitrAvaruNAbhyAm eva dakShiNataH prAtaHsavane 'surarakShAMsy apAghnata.
     tathaivaitad yajamAnA
     #mitrAvaruNAbhyAm eva dakShiNataH prAtaHsavane 'surarakShaMsy apaghnate.
     tasmAn maitrAvaruNam maitrAvaruNaH prAtaHsavane shaMsati,
     #mitrAvaruNAbhyAM hi devA dakShiNataH prAtaHsavane 'surarakShAMsy apAghnata
|p2  te vai dakShiNato 'pahatA asurA madhyato yaj~Nam prAvishaMs.
     te devAH pratibudhyendram madhyato 'dadhus,
     ta #indreNaiva madhyataH prAtaHsavane 'surarakShAMsy apAghnata.
     tathaivaitad yajamAnA
     #indreNaiva madhyataH prAtaHsavane 'surarakShAMsy apaghnate.
     tasmAd aindram brAhmaNAcchaMsI prAtaHsavane shaMsatIndreNa
     hi devA madhyataH prAtaHsavane 'surarakShAMsy apAghnata
|p3  te vai madhyato 'pahatA asurA uttarato yaj~Nam prAvishaMs.
     te devAH pratibudhyendrAgnI uttarataH paryauhaMs,
     ta #indrAgnibhyAM evottarataH prAtaHsavane 'surarAkShAMsy apAghnata.
     tathaivaitad yajamAnA
     #indrAgnibhyAm evottarataH prAtaHsavane 'surarakShAMsy apaghnate.
     tasmAd aindrAgnam achAvAkaH prAtaHsavane shaMsatIndrAgnibhyAM
     hi devA uttarataH prAtaHsavane 'surarakShAMsy apAghnata
|p4  te vA uttarato 'pahatA asurAH purastAt paryadravan samanIkatas.
     te devAH pratibudhyAgnim purastAt prAtaHsavane paryauhaMs,
     te 'gninaiva purastAt prAtaHsavane 'surarakShAMsy apAghnata.
     tathaivaitad yajamAnA
     #agninaiva purastAt prAtaHsavane 'surarakShAMsy apaghnate.
     tasmAd Agneyam prAtaHsavanam
|p5  apa pApmAnaM hate ya evaM veda
|p6  te vai purastAd apahatA asurAH pashcAt parItya prAvishaMs.
     te devAH pratibudhya #vishvAn devAn AtmAnaM pashcAt tR^itIyasavane paryauhaMs,
     te #vishvair eva devair AtmabhiH pashcAt tR^itIyasavane 'surarakShAMsy apAghnata.
     tathaivaitad yajamAnA
     #vishvair eva devair AtmabhiH pashcAt tR^itIyasavane 'surarakShAMsy apaghnate.
     tasmAd vaishvadevaM tR^itIyasavanam
|p7  apa pApmAnaM hate ya evaM veda
|p8  te vai devA asurAn evam apAghnata sarvasmAd eva yaj~NAt.
     tato vai devA abhavan, parAsurA
|p9  bhavaty AtmanA, parAsya dviShan pApmA bhrAtR^ivyo bhavati,
     ya evaM veda
|p10  te devA evaM k.lptena yaj~NenApAsurAn pApmAnam aghnatAjayan svargaM lokam
|p11  apa ha vai dviShantam pApmAnam bhrAtR^ivyaM hate,
     jayati svargaM lokaM ya evaM veda yash caivaM vidvAn savanAni kalpayati

|c5
|p1  stotriyaM stotriyasyAnurUpaM kurvanti prAtaHsavane,
     'har eva tad ahno 'nurUpaM kurvanty,
     avareNaiva tad ahnA param ahar abhyArabhante
|p2  'tha tathA na madhyaMdine.
     shrIr vai pR^iShThAni,
     tAni tasmai na &0 tasthAnAni yat stotriyaM stotriyasyAnurUpaM kuryus
|p3  tayaiva vibhaktyA tR^itIyasavane na stotriyaM stotriyasyAnurUpAM kurvanti

|c6
|p1  athAta ArambhaNIyA eva
|p2  R^ijunItI no varuNa iti maitrAvaruNasya, mitro nayatu vidvAn iti.
     praNetA vA eSha hotrakANAM yan maitrAvaruNas,
     tasmAd eShA praNetR^imatI bhavatI/ndraM
|p3  vo vishvatas parIti brAhmaNAcchaMsino,
     havAmahe janebhya itIndram evaitayAhar-ahAr nihvayante
|p4  na haiShAM vihave 'nya #indraM vR^i.Nkte yatraivaM vidvAn
     brAhmaNAcchaMsy etAm, ahar-ahaH shaMsati
|p5  yat soma A sute nara ity achAvAkasyendrAgnI ajohavur itIndrAgnI
     evaitayAhar-ahar nihvayante.
     na haiShAM vihave 'nya indrAgnI vR^i.Nkte yatraivaM vidvAn
     achAvAka etAm ahar-ahaH shaMsati
|p6  tA vA etAH svargasya lokasya nAvaH sampAriNyaH,
     svargam evaitAbhir lokam abhisaMtaranti

|c7
|p1  athAtaH paridhAnIyA eva
|p2  te syAma deva varuNeti maitrAvaruNasyeShaM svash ca dhImahIty.
     ayaM vai loka iSham ity asau lokaH svar ity,
     ubhAv evaitayA lokAv Arabhante
|p3  vy antarikSham atirad iti brAhmanAcchaMsino,
     vivattR^icaM svargam evaibhya etAya lokaM vivR^iNoti
|p4  made somasya rocanA \ indro yad abhinad valam iti
|p5  siShAsavo vA ete yad dIkShitAs, tasmAd eShA valavatI bhavaty
|p6  ud gA Ajad a.Ngirobhya AvisH kR^iNvan guhA satIH \
     arvA~NcaM nunude valam iti, sanim evaibhya etayAvarunddha
|p7  indreNa rocanA diva iti, svargo vai loka indreNa rocanA divo
|p8  dR^i.lhAni dR^iMhitAni ca \ sthirANi na parANuda iti
|p9  svarga evaitayA loke 'harahaH pratitiShThanto yanty
|p10  AhaM sarasvatIvator ity achAvAkasya.
     vAg vai #sarasvatI, vAgvator iti haitad AhendrAgnyor avo vR^iNa ity.
     etad dha vA #indrAgnyoH priyaM dhAma yad vAg iti,
     priyeNaivainau tad dhAmnA samardhayati
|p11  priyeNa dhAmnA samR^idhyate ya evaM veda

|c8
|p1  ubhayyaH paridhAnIyA bhavanti hotrakANAm prAtaHsavane
     ca mAdhyaMdine cAhInAsh caikAhikAsh ca
|p2  tata aikAhikAbhir eva maitrAvaruNo paridadhAti,
     tenAsmAl lokAn na pracyavate
|p3  'hInAbhir achAvAkaH, svargasya lokasyAptyA
|p4  ubhayIbhir brAhmaNAcchaMsI.
     teno sa ubhau vyanvArabhamANa etImaM cAmuM ca lokam,
     atho maitrAvaruNaM cAchAvAkaM cAtho ahInaM caikAham cAtho saMvatsaraM
     cAgniShTomaM caivam u sa ubhau vyanvArabhamANa ety
|p5  atha tata aikAhikA eva tR^itIyasavane hotrakANAm paridhAnIyA bhavanti.
     pratiShThA vA ekAhaH, pratiShThAyAm eva tad yaj~Nam antataH pratiShThApayanty
|p6  anavAnam prAtaHsavane yajed
|p7  ekAM dve na stomam atishaMset.
     tad yathAbhiheShate pipAsate kShipram prayachet, tAdR^ik tad.
     atho kShipraM devebhyo 'nnAdyaM somapItham prayachAnIti.
     kShipraM hAsmi~Ml loke pratitiShThaty
|p8  aparimitAbhir uttarayoH savanayor.
     aparimito vai svargo lokaH, svargasya lokasyAptyai
|p9  kAmaM tad dhotA shAMsed yad dhotrakAH purvedyuH shaMseyur,
     yad vA hotA tad dhotrakAH.
     prANo vai hotA.NgAni hotrakAH, samAno vA ayam prANo '.NgAny anusaMcarati.
     tasmAt tat kAmaM hotA shaMsed yad dhotrakAH pUrvedyuH shaMseyur,
     yad vA hotA tad dhotrakAH
|p10  sUktAntair hotA paridadhad ety,
     atha samAnya eva tR^itIyasavane hotrakANAm paridhAnIyA bhavanty.
     AtmA vai hotA.NgAni hotrakAH.
     samAnA vA ime '.NgAnAm antAs,
     tasmAt samAnya eva tR^itIyasavane hotrakANAm paridhAniyA bhavanti bhavanti

|c9 {adhyAya 28, khaNDaH 1-8}
|p1  A tvA vahantu haraya iti prAtaHsavana unnIyamAnebhyo 'nvAha
     vR^iShaNvatIH pItavatIH sutavatIr madvatI rUpasamR^iddhA
|p2  aindrIr anvAhaindro vai yaj~No
|p3  gAyatrIr anvAha, gAyatraM vai prAtaHsavanaM
|p4  nava nyUnAH prAtaHsavane 'nvAha, nyUne vai retaH sicyate
|p5  dasha madhyaMdine 'nvAha,
     nyUne vai retaH siktam madhyaM striyai prApya sthaviShTham bhavati
|p6  nava nyUnAs tR^itIyasavane 'nvAha, nyUnAd vai prajAH prajAyante
|p7  tad yad etAni kevalasUktAny anvAha,
     yajamAnam eva tad garbham bhUtam prajanayati yaj~NAd devayonyai
|p8  te haike sapta-saptAnvAhuH sapta prAtaHsavane sapta mAdhyaMdine
     sapta tR^itIyasavane:
     yAvatyo vai puronuvAkyAs tAvatyo yAjyAH,
     sapta vai prA~Nco yajanti sapta vaShaTkurvanti,
     tAsAm etAH puronnvAkyA iti vadantas
|p9  tat tathA na kuryAd.
     yajamAnasya ha te reto vilumpanty atho yajamAnam eva,
     yajamAno hi sUktaM
|p10  navabhir vA etam maitrAvaruNo 'smAl lokAd antarikShalokam abhi pravahati,
     dashabhir antarikShalokAd amuM lokam abhy -- antarikShaloko hi jyeShTho --
     navabhir amuShmAl lokAt svargaM lokam abhi
|p11  na ha vai te yajamAnAM svargaM lokam abhi vo.lhum arhanti
     ye sapta-saptAnvAhus
|p12  tasmAt kevalasha eva sUktAny anubrUyAt

|c10
|p1  athAha:

     ce,daM te somyam madhv iti hotA yajatI,ndra tvA vR^iShabhaM vayaM iti

     kathaM teShAm aindryo bhavantIti

     yad vai kiMca pItavat padaM
     tad aindraM rUpaM, tenendram prINAti

|c11
|p1  asAvi devaM goR^ijIkam andha iti madhyaMdina unnIyamAnebhyo
     'nvAha vR^iShaNvatIH pItavatIH sutavatIr madvatI rUpasamR^iddhA

     triShTubho 'nvAha, traiShTubham vai mAdhyaMdinaM savanaM

     atha kasmAn madhyaMdine madvatIr anu cAha yajanti cAbhir iti
|p4  mAdyantIva vai madhyaMdine devatAH, sam eva tR^itIyasavane mAdayante.

|p12  somAH pradivo vidAnA ity achAvAko yajaty
|p13  ApUrNo asya kalashaH svAhety AgnIdhro yajati

     sa etAbhir eva mAdhyaMdinaM savanam abhyatR^iNad.

|c12
|p1  ihopa yAta shavaso napAta iti tR^itIyasavana unnIyamAnebhyo
     'nvAha vR^iShaNvatIH pItavatIH sutavatIr madvatI rUpasamR^iddhAs.
     tA aindrArbhavyo bhavanti
|p2  tad Ahur:
     yan nArbhavIShu stuvate, 'tha kasmAd ArbhavaH pavamAna ity AcakShata iti
|p3  #prajApatir vai pita #R^ibhUn martyAn sato
     'martyAn kR^itvA tR^itIyasavana Abhajat, tasmAn nArbhavIShu stuvate,
     'thArbhavaH pavamAna ity AcakShate

     atho #indraM evaitat savane 'nvAbhajatIty

     nAnAdevatyAbhir itare, kathaM teShAm aindrArbhavyo bhavantItI/ndrAvaruNA
|p7  sutapAv imaM sutam iti maitrAvaruNo yajati,
     yuvo ratho adhvaraM devavItaya iti bahUni vaha.
     tad #R^ibhUNAm rUpam
|p8  indrash ca somam pibatam bR^ihaspata iti brAhmaNAcchaMsI yajaty,

     tad #R^ibhUNAM rUpam
|p10  ameva naH suhavA A hi gantaneti neShTA yajati,
     gantaneti bahUni vAha.
     tad #R^ibhUNAM rUpam
|p11  indrAviShNU pibatam madhvo asyety achAvAko yajaty,
     A vAm andhAMsi madirANy agmann iti bahUni vAha.
     tad #R^ibhUNAM rUpam
l2 imaM stomam arhate jAtavedasa ity AgnIdhro yajati,
     ratham iva sam mahemA manIShayeti bahUni vAha.
     tad #R^ibhUNAM rUpam
|p13  evam u haitA aindrArbhavyo bhavanti

     tR^itIyasavanasyaiva samR^iddhyai

|c13
|p1  athAha:

     katham asyaitA ukthinyaH sarvAH samAH samR^iddhA bhavantIti

|c14
|p1  athAha:
     yad etAs tisra ukthinyo hotrAH, katham itarA ukthinyo bhavantIty
|p2  Ajyam evAgnIdhrIyAyA uktham, marutvatIyam potrIyAyai,
     vaishvadevaM neShTrIyAyai.
     tA vA etA hotrA evAMnya.NgA eva bhavanty
|p3  athAha:
     yad ekapraiShA anye hotrakA,
     atha kasmAd dvipraiShaH potA dvipraiSho neShTeti
|p4  yatrAdo gAyatrI suparNo bhUtvA somam Aharat,
     tad etAsAM hotrANAm #indra ukthAni parilupya hotre pradadau:
     yUyam mAbhyahvayadhvaM yUyam asyAvediShTeti.
     te hocur devA:
     vAceme hotre prabhAvayAmeti, tasmAt te dvipraiShe bhavata.
     R^icAgnIdhrIyAm prabhAvayAM cakrus,
     tasmAt tasyaikayarcA bhUyasyo yAjyA bhavanty
|p5  athAha:
     yad dhotA yakShad dhotA yakShad iti maitrAvaruno hotre preShyaty,
     atha kasmAd ahotR^ibhyaH sadbhyo hotrashaMsibhyo
     hotA yakShad dhotA yakShad iti preShyatIti
|p6  prANo vai hotA prANaH sarva R^itvijaH,
     prANo yakShat prAno yakShad ity eva tad AhA/thAhAsty
|p7  udgAtRNAm praiShA+H \ nA+~M iti astITi brUyAd.
     yad evaitat prashAstA japaM japitvA studhvam ity Aha,
     sa eShAm praiSho
|p8  'thAhAsty achAvAkasya pravarA+H \ nA+~M iti \ astIti brUyAd.
     yad evainam adhvaryur AhAchAvAka vadasva yat te vAdyam ity,
     eSho 'sya pravaro
|p9  'thAha:
     yad aindrAvaruNam maitrAvaruNas tR^itIyasavane shaMsaty,
     atha kasmAd asyAgneyau stotriyAnurUpan bhavata ity.
     #agninA vai mukhena devA asurAn ukthebhyo nirjaghnus,
     tasmAd asyAgneyau stotriyAnurUpan bhavato
|p10  'thAha:
     yad aindrAbArhaspatyam brAhmaNAcchAMsI tR^itIyasavane shaMsaty
     aindrAvaiShNavam achAvAkaH,
     katham enayor aindrAH stotriyAnurUpA bhavantItI,ndro
     ha sma vA asurAn ukthebhyaH prajigAya, so 'bravIt:
     kash cAhaM cety.
     ahaM cAhaM ceti ha sma devatA anvavayanti.
     sa yad #indraH pUrvaH prajigAya,
     tasmAd enayor aindrAH stotriyAnurUpA bhavanti.
     yad v ahaM cAhaM ceti ha sma devatA anvavayus,
     tasmAn nAnAdevatyAni shaMsataH

|c15
|p1  athAha:
     yad vaishvadevaM vai tR^itIyasavanam,
     atha kasmAd etAny aindrANi jAgatAni sUktani tR^itIyasavana
     ArambhaNIyAni shasyanta itI,ndram evaitair Arabhya yantIti brUyAd.
     atho yaj jAgataM vai tR^itIyasavanaM, taj jagatkAmyaiva.

     sUktAni tR^itIyasavana ArambhaNIyAni shasyante

|p3  sam iShety.
     annaM vA iSho, 'nnAdyasyAvaruddhyA

     svastitAyA evaitad aharahaH shaMsaty

     atha kasmAd eShAM triShTubhaH paridhAnIyA bhavantIti.

     bR^ihaspatir naH pari pAtu pashcAd iti brAhmaNAcchAMsina,

|p7  bhau hi tau jigyatur

     sa imA~Ml lokAn vicakrame 'tho vedAn atho vAcaM.
     tad AhuH:
     kiM tat sahasram itI,me lokA ime vedA atho vAg iti brUyAd
|p12  airayethAm-airayethAm ity achAvAka ukthye 'bhyasyati,
     sa hi tatrAntyo bhavaty

     ity AhuH, katham anyeShv ahassv abhyasyati katham atra nAbhyasyed iti.

|c17 {adhyAya 29, khaNDaH 1-10}
|p1  yaH shvaHstotriyas, tam anurUpaM kurvanti prAtaHsavane 'hInasaMtatyai
|p2  yathA vA ekAhaH suta, evam ahInas.
     tad yathaikAhasya sutasya savanAni saMtiShThamAnAni yanty,
     evam evAhInasyAhAni saMtiShThamAnAni yanti.
     tad yac chvaHstotriyam anurUpaM kurvanti prAtaHsavane 'hInasaMtatyA,
     ahInam eva tat saMtanvanti
|p3  te vai devAsh ca R^iShayash cAdriyanta:
     samAnena yaj~NaM saMtanavAmeti, ta etat samAnaM yaj~NasyApashyau:
     samAnAn pragAthAn samAnIH pratipadaH samAnAni sUktAny
|p4  okaHsArI vA #indro.
     yatra vA #indraH pUrvaM gachaty, aiva tatrAparaM gachati,
     yaj~Nasyaiva sendratAyai

|c18
|p1  tAn vA etAn sampAtAn #vishvAmitraH prathamam apashyat,
     tAn #vishvAmitreNa dR^iShTAn #vAmadevo 'sR^ijatai,
     vA tvAm indra vajrinn atra, yan na indro jujuShe yac ca vaShTi,
     kathA mahAm avR^idhat kasya hotur iti,
     tAn kShipraM samapatad.
     yat kShipraM samapatat, tat sampAtAnAM sampAtatvaM
|p2  sa hekShAM cakre #vishvAmitro:
     yAn vA ahaM sampAtAn apashyaM tAn #vAmadevo 'sR^iShTa,
     kAni nv ahaM sUktAni sampAtAMs tatpratimAn sR^ijeyeti.
     sa etAni sUktAni sampAtAMs tatpratimAn asR^ijata:
     sadyo ha jAto vR^iShabhaH kanIna, indraH pUrbhid Atirad dAsam arkair,
     imAm U Shu prabhR^itiM sAtaye dhA, ichanti tvA somyAsaH sakhAyaH,
     shAsad vahnir duhitur naptyaM gAd, abhi taShTeva dIdhayA manIShAm iti
|p3  ya eka id dhavyash carShaNInAm iti #bharadvAjo;
     yas tigmashR^i.Ngo vR^iShabho na bhIma,
     ud u brahmANy airata shravasyeti #vasiShTho,
     'smA id u pra tavase turAyeti #nodhAs
|p4  ta ete prAtaHsavane Sha.lahastotriyA~N chastvA
     mAdhyaMdine 'hInasUktAni shaMsanti
|p5  tAny etAny ahInasUktAny:
     A satyo yAtu maghavA~M R^iijIShIti satyavan maitrAvaruno;
     'smA id u pra tavase turAye,ndrAya= brahmANi rAtatamA \
     indra brahmANi gotamAso akrann iti brahmaNvad brAhmaNAcchaMsI;
     shAsad vahnir -- janayanta vahnim iti vahnivad achAvAkas
|p6  tad Ahuh:
     kasmAd achAvAko vahnivad etat sUktam ubhayatra shaMsati
     parA~NciShu caivAhassv abhyAvartiShu ceti

     vahati ha vai vahnir dhuro yAsu yujyate.

     parA~NciShu caivAhassv abhyAvartiShu ca

     nAbhAnediShThaM vAlakhilyA vR^iShAkapim evayAmarutaM.
     tAni saha vA shaMset saha vA na shaMsed
|p6  yad enAni nAnA shaMsed, yathA puruShaM vA reto vA vichindyAt tAdR^ik tat.
     tasmAd enAni saha vA shaMset saha vA na shaMset
|p7  sa ha #bulila #Ashvatara #Ashvir vaishvajito hotA sann IkShAM cakra:
     eShAM vA eShAM shilpAnAM vishvajiti
     sAMvatsarike dve madhyaMdinam abhi pratyetor
     hantAham ittham evayAmarutaM shaMsayAnIti.
     tad dha tathA shaMsayAM cakAra
|p8  tad dha tathA shasyAmane #gaushla AjagAma, sa hovAca:
     hotaH kathA te shastraM vicakram plavata iti
|p9  kihy hy abhUd ity
|p10  evayAmarud ayam uttarataH shasyata iti sa hovAcaindro vai madhyaMdinaH,
     kathendram madhyaMdinAn ninIShasIti
|p11  nendram madhyaMdinAn ninIShAmIti hovAca
|p12  chandas tv idam amadhyaMdinasAcy.
     ayaM jAgato vAtijAgato vA.
     sarvaM vA idaM jAgataM vAtijAgataM vA.
     sa u mAruto.
     maiva shaMsiShTeti
|p13  sa hovAcAramAchAvakety.
     atha hAsminn anushAsanam IShe

|p15  tad dha tathA shaMsayAM cakAra.
     tad idam apy etarhi tathaiva shasyate

|c1 {adhyAya 31, khaNDaH 1}
|p1  athAtaH pashor vibhaktis, tasya vibhAgaM vakShyAmo
|p2  hanU sajihve prastotuH, shyenaM vakSha udgAtuH,
     kaNThaH kAkudraH pratihartur, dakShiNA shroNir hotuH,
