     savyam potur, dakShiNa Urur achAvAkasya,
     savya AgnIdhrasya, dakShiNo bAhur Atreyasya,
     savyaH sadasyasya, sadaM cAnUkaM ca gR^ihapater,
     dakShiNau pAdau gR^ihapater vratapradasya,
     savyau pAdau gR^ihapater bhAryAyai vratapradasyau,ShTha
     enayoH sAdhAraNo bhavati, taM gR^ihapatir eva prashiMShyAj.
     jAghanIm patnIbhyo haranti, tAm brAhmaNAya dadyuH.
     skandhyAsh ca manikAs tisrash ca kIkasA grAvastutas,
     tisrash caiva kIkasA ardhaM ca vaikartasyonnetur,
     ardhaM caiva vaikartasya klomA ca shamitus.
     tad brAhmaNAya dadyAd, yady abrAhmaNaH syAc.
     chiraH subrahmaNyAyai, yaH shvaHsutyAm prAha tasyAjinam,
     i.la sarveShAM hotur vA
|p3  tA vA etAH ShaTtriMshatam ekapA yaj~NaM vAhanti.
     ShaTtriMshadakSharA vai bR^ihatI, bArhatAH svargA lokAH.
     prAnAMsh caiva tat svargAMsh ca lokAn Apnuvanti,
     prANeShu caiva tat svargeShu ca lokeShu pratitiShThanto yanti

     tad yathA selagA vA pApakR^ito vA pashuM vimathnIraMs tAdR^ik tat

|c2 {adhyAya 32, khaNDaH 1-11}

|c3
|p1  #tad Ahur:

     kA tatra prAyashcittir iti.
     tAm abhimantrayeta
|p2  yasmAd bhIShA niShIdasi tato no abhayaM kR^idhi \
     pashUn naH sarvAn gopAya namo rudrAya mI.lhuSha iti.
     tAm utthApayed:
     ud asthAd devy aditir Ayur yaj~NapatAv adhAt \
     indrAya kR^iNvatI bhAgam mitrAya varuNaya cety.
     athAsyA udapAtram Udhasi ca mukhe copagR^ihNIyAd, athainAm brAhmaNAya dadyAt.
     sA tatra prAyashcittis
|p3  tad Ahur:
     yasyAgnihotry upAvasR^iShTA duhyamAnA vAshyeta,
     kA tatra prAyashcittir ity.
   ashanAyAM ha vA eShA yajamAnasya pratikhyAya vAshyate.
     tAm annam apy Adayec chAntyai, shAntir vA annaM.
     sUyavasAd bhagavatI hi bhUyA iti.
     sA tatra prAyashcittis
|p4  tad Ahur:
     yasyAgnihotry upAvasR^iShTA duhyamAnA &7 spandeta,
     kA tatra prAyashcittir iti.
     sA yat tatra skandayet, tad abhimR^ishya japed:
     yad adya dugdham pR^ithivIm asR^ipta yad oShadhIr atyasR^ipad yad ApaH \
     payo gR^iheShu payo aghnyAyAm payo vatseShu payo astu tan mayIti.
     tatra yat parishiShTaM syAt, tena juhuyAd yady alaM homAya syAD
     yady u vai sarvaM siktaM syAd, athAnyAm AhUya tAM dugdhvA tena juhuyAd,
     A tv eva shraddhAyai hotavyaM.
     sA tatra prAyashcittiH

|c4
|p1  tad Ahur:
     yasya sAyaMdugdhaM sAMnAyyaM duShyed vApahared vA,

     prAtardugdhaM dvaidhaM kR^itvA tasyAnyatarAm bhaktim Atacya tena yajeta:

|p2  tad Ahur:

|p3  tad Ahur:

     kA tatra prAyascittir ity.
     aindraM vA mAhendraM veti samAnaM.
     sA tatra prAyashcittis
|p4  tad Ahur:

|c5
|p1  tad Ahur:

     athottarata AhavanIyasyoShNam bhasma nirUhya juhuyAn
     manasA vA prAjApatyayA varcA.

     tac ced &1 vyapanetuM shaknuyAn,

|c6

|p1  #harishcandro ha #vaidhasa #aikShvAko rAjAputra Asa.

            yaM nv imam putram ichanti ye vijAnanti ye ca na \
           kiM svit putreNa vindate tan ma AcakShva #nAradeti

|p4        R^inam asmin saMnayaty amR^itatvaM ca gachati \
           pitA putrasya jAtasya pashyec cej jIvato mukham \\
|p5        yAvantaH pR^ithivyAm bhogA yAvanto jAtavedasi \
           yAvanto apsu prANinAm bhUyAn putre pitus tataH \\
|p6        shashvat putreNa pitaro 'tyAyan bahulaM tamaH \
           AtmA hi jaj~Na AtmanaH sa irAvaty atitAriNI \\
|p7        kiM nu malaM kim ajinaM kim u shmashrUNi kiM tapaH \
           putram brahmANa ichadhvaM sa vai loko 'vadAvadaH \\
|p8        annaM ha prANaH sharaNaM ha vAso
           rUpaM hiraNyam pashavo vivAhAH \
           sakhA ha jAyA kR^ipaNaM ha duhitA
           jyotir ha putraH parame vyoman \\
|p9        patir jAyAm pravishati garbho bhUtvA sa mAtaram \
           tasyAm punar navo bhUtvA dashame mAsi jAyate \\

           AbhUtir eShAbhUtir bIjam etan nidhIyate \\

|c14
|p1  athainam uvAca:
     #varuNaM rAjAnam upadhAva:
     putro me jAyatAM, tena tvA yajA iti
|p2  tatheti. sa #varuNaM rAjAnam upasasAra:
     putro me jAyatAM, tena tvA yajA iti. tatheti.
     tasya ha putro jaj~Ne #rohito nAma
|p3  taM hovAcAjani vai te putro, yajasva mAneneti.
     sa hovAca:
     yadA vai pashur nirdasho bhavaty, atha sa medhyo bhavati.
     nirdasho nv astv, atha tvA yajA iti. tatheti
|p4  sa ha nirdasha Asa.
     tam hovAca:
     nirdasho nv abhUd, yajasva mAneneti.
     sa hovAca:
     yadA vai pashor dantA jAyante, 'tha sa medhyo bhavati.
     dantA nv asya jAyantAm, atha tvA yajA iti. tatheti
|p5  tasya ha dantA jaj~Nire.
     taM hovAcAj~Nata vA asya dantA, yajasva mAneneti.
     sa hovAca:
     yadA vai pashor dantAH padyante, 'tha sa medhyo bhavati.
     dantA nv asya padyantAm, atha tvA yajA iti. tatheti
|p6  tasya ha dantAH pedire.
     taM hovAcApatsata vA asya dantA, yajasva mAneneti.
     sa hovAca:
     yadA vai pashor dantAH punar jAyante, 'tha sa medhyo bhavati.
     dantA nv asya punar jAyantAm, atha tvA yajA iti. tatheti
|p7  tasya ha dantAH punar jaj~Nire.
     taM hovAcAj~Nata vA asya punar dantA, yajasva mAneneti.
     sa hovAca:
     yadA vai kShatriyaH &1 saMnAhuko bhavaty, atha sa medhyo bhavati.
     saMnAhaM nu prApnotv, atha tvA yajA iti. tatheti
|p8  sa ha saMnAham &2 prApa, taM hovAca:
     saMnAhaM nu &2 prApad, yajasva mAneneti.
     sa tathety uktvA putram AmantrayAm Asa:
     tatAyaM vai mahyaM tvAm adadAd, dhanta tvayAham imaM yajA iti
|p9  sa ha nety uktvA dhanur AdAyAraNyam apAtasthau,
     sa saMvatsaram araNye cacAra

|c15
|p1  atha haikShvAkaM #varuNo jagrAha, tasya hodaraM jaj~Ne.
     tad u ha #rohitaH shushrAva, so 'raNyAd grAmam eyAya.
     tam #indraH puruSharUpeNa paryetyovAca:
           nAnA shrAntAya shrIr astIti #rohita shushruma \
           pApo nR^iShadvaro jana #indra ic carataH sakhA \\
     caraiveti
|p2  caraiveti vai mA brAhmaNo 'vocad,
     iti ha dvitIyaM saMvatsaram araNye cacAra.
     so 'raNyAd grAmam eyAya, tam #indraH puruSharUpeNa paryetyovAca:
           puShpiNyau carato ja.Nghe bhUShNur AtmA phalagrahiH \
           shere 'sya sarve pApmAnaH shrameNa prapathe hatAsh \\
     caraiveti
|p3  caraiveti vai mA brAhmaNo 'vocad,
     iti ha tR^itIyaM saMvatsaram araNye cacAra.
     so 'raNyAd grAmam eyAya, tam #indraH puruSharUpeNa paryetyovAca:
           Aste bhaga AsInasyordhvas tiShThati tiShThataH \
           shete nipadyamAnasya carAti carato bhagash \\
     caraiveti
|p4  caraiveti vai mA brAhmaNo 'vocad,
     iti ha caturthaM saMvatsaram araNye cacAra.
     so 'raNyAd grAman eyAya, tam #indraH puruSharUpeNa paryetyovAca:
           #kaliH shayAno bhavati saMjihAnas tu #dvAparaH \
           uttiShThaMs #tretA bhavati #kR^itaM sampadyate caraMsh \\
     caraiveti
|p5  caraiveti vai mA brAhmaNo 'vocad,
     iti ha pa~NcamaM saMvatsaram araNye cacAra.
     so 'raNyAd grAmam eyAya, tam #indraH puruSharUpeNa paryetyovAca:
           caran vai madhu vindati caran svAdum udumbaram \
           sUryasya pashya shremANaM yo na tandrayate caraMsh \\
     caraiveti
|p6  caraiveti vai mA brAhmaNo 'vocad,
     iti ha ShaShThaM saMvatsaram araNye cacAra.
     so 'jIgartaM #sauyavasim R^iShim &1 ashanAyAparItam araNya upeyAya
|p7  tasya ha trayaH putrA AsuH:
     #shunaHpuchaH #shunaHshepaH #shunolA.NgUla
     iti.
     taM hovAca:
     R^iShe 'haM te shataM dadAmy, aham eShAm ekenAtmAnaM niShkrINA iti.
     sa jyeShTham putraM nigR^ihNAna uvAca:
     na nv imam iti, no evemam iti kaniShTham mAtA.
     tau ha madhyame sampAdayAM cakratuH #shunaHshepe.
     tasya ha shataM dattvA sa tam AdAya so 'raNyAd grAmam eyAya
|p8  sa pitaram etyovAca:
     tata hantAham anenAtmAnaM niShkrINA iti.
     sa #varuNaM rAjAnam upasasArAnena tvA yajA iti.
     tatheti, bhUyan vai brAhmaNaH kShatriyAd iti #varuNa uvAca.
     tasmA etaM rAjasUyaM yaj~Nakratum provAca.
     tam etam abhiShecanIye puruSham pashum Alebhe

|c16
|p1  tasya ha #vishvAmitro hotAsIj, #jamadagnir adhvaryur,
     #vasiShTho brahmAyAsya udgAtA.
     tasmA upAkR^itAya niyoktAraM na vividuH.
     sa hovAcAjIgartaH #sauyavasir:
     mahyam aparaM shataM dattAham enaM niyokShyAmIti.
     tasmA aparaM shataM dadus, taM sa &0,1 niyuyoja
|p2  tasmA upAkR^itAya niyuktAyAprItAyA paryagnikR^itAya vishasitAraM na vividuH.
     sa hovAcAjIgartaH #sauyavasir:
     mahyam aparaM shataM dattAham enaM vishasiShyAmIti.
     tasmA aparaM shataM daduH,
     so 'siM &1 niHshyAna eyAyA+tha ha #shunaHshepa IkShAM cakre:
     'mAnuSham iva vai mA vishasiShyanti, hantAhaM devatA &1 upadhAvAnIti.
     sa #prajApatim eva prathamaM devatAnAm upasAsara:
     kasya nUnaM katamasyAmR^itAnAm ity etayarcA
|p4  tam #prajApatir uvAcAgnir vai devAnAM nediShThas, tam evopadhAveti.
     so 'gnim upasasArAgner vayam prathamasyAmR^itAnAm iti etayarcA
|p5  tam #agnir uvAca:
     #savitA vai prasavAnAm Ishe, tam evopadhAveti.
     sa #savitAram upasasArAbhi tvA deva savitar ity etena tR^icena
|p6  taM #savitovAca:
     #varuNAya vai rAj~Ne niyukto 'si, tam evopadhAveti.
     sa #varuNaM rAjAnam upasasArAta uttarAbhir ekatriMshatA
|p7  taM #varuNa uvAcAgnir vai devAnAm mukhaM suhR^idayatamas,
     taM nu stuhy atha tvotsrakShyAma iti.
     so 'gniM tuShTAvAta uttarAbhir dvAviMshatyA
|p8  tam #agnir uvAca:
     #vishvAn nu devAn stuhy, atha tvotsrakShyAma iti.
     sa #vishvAn devAMs tuShTAva:
     namo mahadbhyo namo arbhakebhya ity etayarcA
|p9  taM #vishve devA Ucur:
     #indro vai devAnAm ojiShTho baliShThaH sahiShThaH sattamaH pArayiShNutamas,
     taM nu stuhy, atha tvotsrakShyAma iti.
     sa #indraM tuShTAva.
     yac cid dhi satya somapA iti caitena sUktenottarasya ca pa~Ncadashabhis
|p10  tasmA #indraH stUyamAnaH prIto manasA hiraNyarathaM dadau.
     tam etayA pratIyAya:
     shashvad indra iti
|p11  tam #indra uvAcAshvinau no stuhy, atha tvotsrakShyAma iti.
     so 'shvinau tuShTAvAta uttareNa tR^icena
|p12  tam #ashvinA ucatur:
     #uShasaM nu stuhy, atha tvotsrakShyAma iti.
     sa #uShasaM tuShTAvAta uttarena tR^icena
|p13  tasya ha smarcy-R^icy uktAyAM vi pAsho mumuce,
     kanIya #aikShvAkasyodaram bhavaty;
     uttamasyAm evarcy uktAyAM vi pAsho mumuce, 'gada #aikShvAka Asa

|c17
|p1  tam R^itvija Ucus:
     tvam eva no 'syAhnaH saMsthAm adhigachety.
     atha haitaM #shunaHshepo '~NjaHsavaM dadarsha,
     tam etAbhish catasR^ibhir abhisuShAva:
     yac cid dhi tvaM gR^ihe-gR^iha ity.
     athainaM droNakalasham abhyavaninAyoc chiShTaM camvor bharety
     etayarcAtha hAsminn anvArabdhe pUrvAbhish catasR^ibhiH sasvAhAkArAbhir
     juhavAM cakArAthainam avabhR^itham abhyavaninAya:
     tvaM no agne varuNasya vidvAn ity etAbhyAm.
     athainam ata Urdhvam agnim AhavanIyam upasthApayAM cakAra:
     shunash cic chepaM niditaM sahasrAd ity
|p2  atha ha #shunaHshepo #vishvAmitrasyA.Nkam AsasAda.
     sa hovAcAjIgartaH #sauyavasir:
     R^iShe punar me putraM dehIti. neti hovAca #vishvAmitro,
     devA vA imam mahyam arAsateti.
     sa ha #devarAto #vaishvAmitra Asa.
     tasyaite #kApileyabAbhravAH
|p3  sa hovacAjIgartaH #sauyavasis:
     &1 tvamvehi vihvayAvahA iti.
     sa hovAcAjIgartaH #sauyavasir:
           #A.Ngiraso janmanAsy #AjIgartiH shrutaH kaviH \
           riShe paitAmahAt tantor mApagAH punar ehi mAm \\
     iti.
     sa hovAca #shunaHshepo:
           'darshus tvA shAsahastaM na yac chUdreShv alapsata \
           gavAM trINi shatAni tvam avR^iNIthA mad #a.Ngira
     iti 
|p4  sa hovAcAjIgartaH #sanyavasis:
           tad vai mA tAta tapati pApaM karma mayA kR^itam \
           tad ahaM nihnave tubhyam pratiyantu shatA gavAm \\
     iti.
     sa hovAca #shunaHshepo:
           yaH sakR^it pApakaM kuryAt kuryAd enat tato 'param \
           nApAgAH shaudrAn nyAyAd asaMdheyaM tvayA kR^itam \\
     ity
|p5  asaMdheyam iti ha #vishvAmitra upapapAda.
     sa hovAca #vishvAmitro.
           bhIma eva #sauyavasiH shAsena vishishAsiShuH \        
           asthAn, maitasya putro bhUr mamaivopehi putratAm \\
     iti
|p6  sa hovAca #shunaHshepaH:
           sa vai yathA no j~NapayA rAjaputra tathA vada \
           yathaivA.NgirasaH sann upeyAM tava putratAm \\
     iti.
     sa hovAca #vishvAmitro:
           jyeShTho me tvam putrANAM syAs tava shreShThA prajA syAt \
           upeyA daivam me dAyaM tena vai tvopamantraya
     iti
|p7  sa hovAca #shunaHshepaH:
           &0,1 saMjAnAneShu vai &0,1 brUyAH sauhardyAya me shriyai \
           yathAham bharataR^iShabhopeyAM= tava putratAm \\
     ity.
     atha ha #vishvAmitraH putrAn AmantrayAm Asa:
           #madhuchandAH shR^iNotana #R^iShabho #reNur #aShTakaH \
           ye keca bhrAtaraH sthanAsmai jyaiShThyAya kalpadhvam \\
     iti

|c18
|p1  tasya ha #vishvAmitrasyaikashatam putrA AsuH pa~NcAshad eva
     jyAyAMso #madhuchandasaH pa~NcAshat kanIyAMsas
|p2  tad ye jyAyAMso, na te kushalam menire.
     tAn anuvyAjahArAntAn vaH prajA bhakShIShTeti.
     ta ete 'ndhrAH #puNDrAH #shabarAH #pulindA #mUtibA ity
     udantyA bahavo bhavanti #vaishvAmitrA dasyUnAm bhUyiShThAH
|p3  sa hovAca #madhuchandAH pa~NcAshatA sArdhaM:
          yan naH pitA saMjAnIte tasmiMs tiShThAmahe vayam \
          puras tvA sarve kurmahe tvAm anva~Nco vayaM smasIty
|p4  atha ha #vishvAmitraH pratItaH putrAMs tuShTAva
|p5       te vai putrAH pashumanto vIravanto bhaviShyatha \
          ye mAnam me 'nugR^ihNanto vIravantam akarta mA \\
|p6       puraetrA vIravanto #devarAtena #gAthinAH \
          sarve rAdhyAH stha putrA, eSha vaH sadvivAcanam \\
|p7       eSha vaH #kushikA vIro #devarAtas, tam anvita \
          yuShmAMsh ca dAyam ma upetA vidyAM yAm u ca vidmasi \\
|p8       te samya~Nco #vaishvAmitrAH sarve sAkaM sarAtayaH \
          #devarAtAya tasthire dhR^ityai shraiShThyAya #gAthinAH \\
|p9       adhIyata #devarAto rikthayor ubhayor R^iShih \
          #jahnUnAM cAdhipatye daive vede ca #gAthinAm \\
|p10  tad etat paraR^ikshatagAthaM shaunaHshepam AkhyAnaM
|p11  tad dhotA rAj~Ne 'bhiShiktAyAcaShTe
|p12  hiraNyakashipAv AsIna AcaShTe, hiraNyakashipAv AsInaH pratigR^iNAti.
     yasho vai hiraNyaM, yashasaivainaM tat samardhayaty
|p13  om ity R^icaH pratigara, evaM tatheti gAthAyA.
     om iti vai daivaM, tatheti mAnuShaM.
     daivena caivainaM tan mAnuSheNa ca pApAd enasaH pramu~Ncati
|p14  tasmAd yo rAjA &0 'vijitI syAd,
     apy ayajamAna AkhyApayetaivaitac chaunaHshepam AkhyAnaM,
     na hAsminn alpaM canainaH parishiShyate
|p16  sahasram AkhyAtre dadyAc chatam pratigaritra ete caivAsane,
     shvetash cAshvatarIratho hotuH
|p17  putrakAmA hApy AkhyApayera~Ml, labhante ha putrA~Ml labhante ha putrAn

|c19 {adhyAya 34, khaNDaH 1-8}
|p1  prajApatir yaj~Nam asR^ijata, yaj~NaM sR^iShTam anu brahmakShatre asR^ijyetAm.
     brahmakShatre anu dvayyaH prajA asR^ijyanta hutAdash cAhutAdash ca,
     brahmaivAnu hutAdaH kShatram anv ahutAda.
     etA vai prajA hutAdo yad brAhmaNA,
     athaitA ahutAdo yad rAjanyo vaishyaH shUdras
|p2  tAbhyo yaj~Na udakrAmat, tam brahmakShatre anvaitAM.
     yAny eva brahmaNa AyudhAni tair brahmAnvaid, yAni kShatrasya taiH kShatram.
     etAni vai brahmaNa AyudhAni yad yaj~NAyudhAny,
     athaitAni kShatrasyAyudhAni yad ashvarathaH kavaca iShudhanva
|p3  taM kShatram ananvApya nyavartatA,yudhebhyo
     ha smAsya vijamAnaH parA.N evaity.
     athainam brahmAnvait, tam Apnot, tam AptvA parastAn nirudhyAtiShThat.
     sa AptaH parastAn niruddhas tiShTha~N j~NAtvA svAny AyudhAni brahmopAvartata.
     tasmAd dhApy etarhi yaj~No brahmaNy eva brAhmaNeShu pratiShThito
|p4  'thainat kShatram anvAgachat, tad abravId:
     upa mAsmin yaj~Ne hvayasveti.
     tat tathety abravIt, tad vai nidhAya svAny AyudhAni brahmaNa
     evAyudhair brahmaNo rUpeNa brahma bhUtvA yaj~Nam upAvartasveti. tatheti.
     tat kShatraM nidhAya svAny AyudhAni brahmaNa evAyudhair brahmaNo
     rUpeNa brahma bhUtvA yaj~Nam upAvartata.
     tasmAd dhApy etarhi kShatriyo yajamAno nidhAyaiva svAny AyudhAni
     brahmaNa evAyudhair brahmaNo rUpeNa brahma bhUtvA yaj~Nam upAvartate

|c20
|p1  athAto devayajanasyaiva yAc~Nyash.
     tad Ahur:
     yad brAhmaNo rAjanyo vaishyo dIkShiShyamANaM kShatriyaM devayajanaM yAcati,
     kaM kShatriyo yAced iti
|p2  daivaM kShatraM yAced, ity Ahur:
     #Adityo vai daivaM kShatram, #Aditya eShAm bhUtAnAm adhipatiH
|p3  sa yad ahar dIkShiShyamANo bhavati,
     tad ahaH pUrvAhNa evodyantam #Adityam upatiShThete,dam
     shreShThaM jyotiShAM jyotir uttamam \ deva savitar devayajanam me
     dehi devayajanaM iti devayajanaM yAcati
|p4  sa yat tatra yAcita uttarAM sarpaty, oM tathA dadAmIti haiva tad Aha

     ha shriyam ashnute, 'shnute ha prajAnAm aishvaryam AdhipatyaM,
     ya evam upasthAya yAcitvA devayajanam adhyavasAya dIkShate kShatriyaH san

|c21
l1 athAta iShTApUrtasyAparijyAniH kShatriyasya yajamAnasya.
     sa purastAd dIkShAyA AhutiM juhuyAc caturgR^ihItam
     Ajyam AhavanIya iShTApUrtasyAparijyAnyai
|p2  punar na indro maghavA dadAtu \ brahma punar iShTam pUrtaM dAt svAhety
|p3  athAnUbandhyAyai samiShTayajuShAm upariShTAt:
     punar no agnir jAtavedA dadAtu \ kShatram punar iShTam pUrtaM dAt svAheti
|p4  saiSheShTApUrtasyAparijyAniH kShatriyasya yajamAnasya yad ete AhutI,
     tasmAd ete hotavye

|c22
|p1  tad u ha smAha #saujAta #ArA.lhir:
     ajItapunarvaNyaM vA etad yad ete AhutI iti.
     yathA ha kAmayeta tathaite kuryAd,
     ya ito 'nushAsanaM kuryAd itIme tv eva juhuyAd
|p2  brahma prapadye brahma mAkShatrAd gopAyatu brahmaNe svAheti
|p3  tat-tad itI+~M \
|p4  brahma vA eSha prapadyate, yo yaj~Nam prapadyate.
     brahma vai yaj~No;
     yaj~NAd u ha vA eSha punar jAyate yo dIkShate.
     tam brahma prapannaM kShatraM na parijinAti.
     brahma mA kShatrAd gopAyatv ity Aha, yathainam brahma kShatrAd gopAyed.
     brahmaNe svAheti, tad enat prINAti.
     tad enat prItaM kShatrAd gopAyaty
|p5  athAnUbandhyAyai samiShTayajuShAm upariShTAt
|p6  kShatram prapadye kShatram mA brahmaNo gopAyatu kShatrAya svAheti.
     tat-tad itI+~M \ kShatraM vA eSha prapadyate, yo rAShTram prapadyate.
     kShatraM hi rAShTraM.
     taM kShatram prapannam brahma na parijinAti.
     kShatram mA brahmaNo gopAyatv ity Aha, yathainaM kShatram brahmaNo gopAyet.
     kShatrAya svAheti, tad enat prINAti.
     tad enat prItam brahmaNo gopAyati
|p7  saiSheShTApUrtasyaivAparijyAniH kShatriyasya yajamAnasya yad ete AhutI,
     tasmAd ete eva hotavye

|c23
|p1  athaindro vai devatayA kShatriyo bhavati,
     traiShTubhash chandasA, pa~NcadashaH stomena,
     somo rAjyena, rAjanyo bandhunA.
     sa ha dIkShamANa eva brAhmaNatAm abhyupaiti yat kR^iShNAjinam adhyUhati,
     yad dIkShitavrataM carati, yad enam brAhmaNA abhisaMgachante.
     tasya ha dIkShamANasyendra evendriyam Adatte, triShTub vIryam,
     pa~NcadashaH stoma AyuH, somo rAjyam, pitaro yashas kIrtim:
     anyo vA ayam asmad bhavati, brahma vA ayam bhavati,
     brahma vA ayam upAvartata iti vadantaH
|p2  sa purastAd dIkShAyA AhutiM hutvAhavanIyam upatiShTheta
|p3  nendrAd devatAyA emi, na triShTubhash chandaso, na pa~Ncadashat stomAn,
     na somAd rAj~No, na pitryAd bandhor.
     mA ma #indra indriyam Adita, mA triShTub vIryam,
     mA pa~NcadashaH stoma Ayur, mA somo rAjyam, mA pitaro yashas kIrtiM.
     sahendriyeNa vIryeNAyuShA rAjyena yashasA bandhunAgnim upaimi
     gAyatrIM chandas trivR^itaM stomaM somaM rAjAnam,
     brahma prapadye brAhmaNo bhavAmIti
|p4  tasya ha nendra indriyam Adatte na triShTub vIryaM na pa~NcadashaH
     stoma Ayur na somo rAjyaM na pitaro yashas kIrtiM,
     ya evam etAm AhutiM hutvAhavanIyam upasthAyA dIkShate kShatriyaH san

|c24
|p1  athAgneyo vai devatayA kShatriyo dIkShito bhavati,
     gAyatrash chandasA, trivR^it stomena, brAhmaNo bandhunA.
     sa hodavasyann eva kShatriyatAm abhyupaiti.
     tasya hodavasyato 'gnir eva teja Adatte, gAyatrI vIryaM,
     trivR^it stoma Ayur, brAhmaNA brahma yashas kIrtim:
     anyo vA ayam asmad bhavati, kShatraM vA ayam bhavati,
     kShatraM vA ayam upAvartata iti vadantaH
|p2  so 'nUbandhyAyai samiShTayajuShAm upariShTAd
     dhutvAhutim AhavanIyam upatiShTheta
|p3  nAgner devatAyA emi, na gAyatryAsh chandaso,
     na trivR^itaH stomAn, na brahmaNo bandhor.
     mA me 'gnis teja Adita, mA gAyatrI vIryam, mA trivR^it stoma Ayur,
     mA brAhmaNA brahma yashas kIrtiM.
     saha tejasA vIryeNAyuShA brahmaNA yashasA kIrtyendraM
     devatAm upaimi triShTubhaM chandaH pa~NcadashaM stomaM somaM rAjAnaM,
     kShatram prapadye kShatriyo bhavAmi \
     devAH pitaraH pitaro devA yo 'smi sa san yaje \
     svam ma idam iShTaM svam pUrtaM svaM shrAntaM svaM hutam \
     tasya me 'yam #agnir upadraShTAyaM #vAyur upashrotAsAv #Adityo
     'nukhyAtedam ahaM ya evAsmi so 'smIti
|p4  tasya ha nAgnis teja Adatte na gAyatrI vIryaM na trivR^it stoma Ayur
     na brAhmaNA brahma yashas kIrtiM,
     ya evam etAm AhutiM hutvAhavanIyam upasthAyodavasyati kShatriyaH san

|c25
|p1  athAto dIkShAyA Avedanasyaiva.
     tad Ahur:
     yad brAhmaNasya dIkShitasya brAhmaNo 'dIkShiShTeti dIkShAm Avedayanti,
     kathaM kShatriyasyAvedayed iti
|p2  yathaivaitad brAhmaNasya dIkShitasya:
     brAhmaNo 'dIkShiShTeti dIkShAm avedayanty,
     evam evaitat kShatriyasyAvedayet, purohitasyArSheyeNeti
|p3  tat-tad itI+~M \
|p14  nidhAya vA eSha svAny AyudhAni brahmANa evAyudhair
     brahmaNo rUpeNA brahma bhUtvA yaj~Nam upAvartata.
     tasmAt tasya purohitasyArSheyeNa dIkShAm AvedayeyuH,
     purohitasyArSheyeNa pravaram pravR^iNIran

|c26
|p1  athAto yajamAnabhAgasyaiva.
     tad AhuH:
     prAshnIyAt kShatriyo yajamAnabhAgA+m \ na prAshnIyA+t iti \
|p2  yat prAshnIyAd ahutAd dhutam prAshya pApIyAn syAd;
     yan na prAshnIyAd yaj~NAd AtmAnam antariyAd, yaj~No vai yajamAnabhAgaH
|p3  sa brahmaNe parihR^ityaH
|p4  purohitAyatanaM vA etat kShatriyasya
     yad brahmA,rdhAtmo ha vA eSha kShatriyasya yat purohita.
     upAha parokSheNaiva prAshitarUpam Apnoti,
     nAsya pratyakSham bhakShito bhavati
|p5  yaj~Na u ha vA eSha pratyakShaM yad brahmA.
     brahmaNi hi sarvo yaj~NaH pratiShThito, yaj~Ne yajamAno.
     yaj~Na eva tad yaj~Nam apyatyarjanti yathApsv Apo yathAgnAv agniM.
     tad vai nAtiricyate, tad enaM na hinasti.
     tasmAt sa brahmaNe parihR^ityo
|p6  'gnau haike juhvati:
     prajApater vibhAn nAma lokas, tasmiMs tvA dadhAmi saha yajamAnena svAheti.
     tat tathA na kuryAd.
     yajamAno vai yajamAnabhAgo, yajamAnaM ha so 'gnau pravR^iNakti.
     ya enaM tatra brUyAd:
     yajamAnam agnau prAvArkShIH, prAsyAgniH prANAn dhakShyati,
     mariShyati yajamAna iti:
     shashvat tathA syAt.
     tasmAt tasyAshAM neyAd AshAM neyAt

|c27 {adhyAya 35, khaNDaH 1-8}
|p1  vishvaMtaro ha #sauShadmanaH #shyAparNAn paricakShANo vishyAparNaM yaj~Nam Ajahre.
     tad dhAnubudhya #shyAparNAs taM yaj~Nam Ajagmus,
     te ha tadantarvedy AsAM cakrire.
     tAn ha dR^iShTvovAca:
     pApasya vA ime karmaNaH kartAra Asate 'pUtAyai vAco vaditAro yac #chyAparNA,
     imAn utthApayateme me 'ntarvedi mAsiShateti. tatheti.
     tAn utthApayAM cakrus
|p2  te hotthApyamAnA ruruvire:
     ye tebhyo #bhUtavIrebhyo 'sitamR^igAH #kashyapAnAM somapItham
     abhijigyuH #pArikShitasya #janamejayasya vikashyape yaj~Ne,
     tais te tatra vIravanta AsuH.
     kaH svit so &1 'smAko &1 'sti vIro, ya imaM somapItham abhijeShyatIty
|p3  ayam aham asmi vo vIra, iti hovAca #rAmo #mArgaveyo
|p4  #rAmo hAsa #mArgaveyo 'nUcAnaH #shyAparNIyas.
     teShAM hottiShThatAm uvAcApi nu rAjann itthaMvidaM veder utthApayantIti.
     yas tvaM kathaM vettha brahmabandhav iti

|c28
|p1  yatrendraM devatAH paryavR^i~Njan:
     #vishvarUpaM #tvAShTram abhyamaMsta, #vR^itram astR^ita,
     yatIn sAlAvR^ikebhyaH prAdAd, arurumaghAn avadhId,
     #bR^ihaspateH pratyavadhId iti:
     tatrendraH somapIthena vyArdhyatendrasyAnu vyR^iddhiM kShatraM
     somapIthena vyArdhyatApIndraH somapIthe 'bhavat #tvaShTur AmuShya somaM.
     tad vyR^iddham evAdyApi kShatraM somapIthena.
     sa yas tam bhakShaM vidyAd yaH kShatrasya somapithena
     vyR^iiddhasya yena kShatraM samR^idhyate,
     kathaM taM veder utthApayantIti
|p2  vettha brAhmaNa tvaM tam bhakShA+m \ veda hIti.
     taM vai no brAhmaNa brUhIti.
     tasmai vai te rAjann, iti hovAca

|c29
|p1  trayANAm bhakShANAm ekam AhariShyanti:
     somaM vA dadhi vApo vA
|p2  sa yadi somam, brAhmaNAnAM sa bhakSho:
     brAhmaNAMs tena bhakSheNa jinviShyasi,
     brAhmaNakalpas te prajAyAm AjaniShyata
     AdAyy ApAyy AvasAyI yathAkAmaprayApyo.
     yadA vai kShatriyAya pApam bhavati,
     brAhmaNakalpo 'sya prajAyAm AjAyata,
     Ishvaro hAsmAd dvitIyo vA tR^itIyo vA brAhmaNatAm abhyupaitoH,
     sa brahmabandhavena jijyUShito
|p3  'tha yadi dadhi, vaishyAnAM sa bhakSho:
     vaishyAMs tena bhakSheNa jinviShyasi,
     vaishyakalpas te prajAyAm AjaniShyate
     'nyasya balikR^id anyasyAdyo yathAkAmajyeyo.
     yadA vai kShatriyAya pApam bhavati,
     vaishyakalpo 'sya prajAyAm AjAyata,
     Ishvaro hAsmAd dvitIyo vA tR^itIyo vA vaishyatAm abhyupaitoH,
     sa vaishyatayA jijyUShito
|p4  'tha yady apaH, shUdrANAM sa bhakShaH:
     shUdrAMs tena bhakSheNa jinviShyasi,
     shUdrakalpas te prajAyAm AjaniShyate
     'nyasya preShyaH kAmotthApyo yathAkAmavadhyo.
     yadA vai kShatriyAya pApam bhavati,
     shUdrakalpo 'sya prajAyAm AjAyata,
     Ishvaro hAsmAd dvitIyo vA tR^itIyo vA shUdratAm abhyupaitoH,
     sa shUdratayA jijyUShitaH

|c30
|p1  ete vai te trayo bhakShA rAjann, iti hovAca,
     yeShAm AshAM neyAt kShatriyo yajamAno
|p2  'thAsyaiSha svo bhakSho:
     nyagrodhasyAvarodhAsh ca phalAni caudumbarANy AshvatthAni plAkShANy
     abhiShuNuyAt tAni bhakShayet, so 'sya svo bhakSho
|p3  yato vA adhi devA yaj~NeneShTvA svargaM lokam AyaMs,
     tatraitAMsh camasAn nyubjaMs, te nyagrodhA abhavan.
     nyubjA iti hApy enAn etarhy AcakShate #kurukShetre.
     te ha prathamajA nyagrodhAnAM, tebhyo hAnye 'dhijAtAs
|p4  te yan nya~Nco 'rohaMs tasmAn nya.N rohati nyagroho, nyagroho vai nAma.
     taM nyagrohaM santaM nyagrodha ity AcakShate parokSheNa,
     parokShapriyA iva hi devAH

|c31
|p1  teShAM yash camasAnAM raso 'vA.N ait te 'varodhA abhavann,
     atha ya Urdhvas tAni phalAny
|p2  eSha ha vAva kShatriyaH svAd bhakShAn naiti,
     yo nyagrodhasyAvarodhAMsh ca phalAni ca bhakShayaty.
     upAha parokSheNaiva somapItham Apnoti,
     nAsya pratyakSham bhakShito bhavati.
     parokSham iva ha vA eSha somo rAjA yan nyagrodhaH,
     parokSham ivaiSha brahmaNo rUpam upanigachati yat kShatriyaH:
     purodhayaiva dIkShayaiva pravareNaiva
|p3  kShatraM vA etad vanaspatInAM yan nyagrodhaH,
     kShatraM rAjanyo.
     nitata iva hIha kShatriyo rAShTre vasan bhavati pratiShThita iva,
     nitata iva nyagrodho 'varodhair bhUmyAm pratiShThita iva
|p4  tad yat kShatriyo yajamAno nyagrodhasyAvarodhAMsh ca phalAni ca bhakShayaty,
     Atmany eva tat kShatraM vanaspatInAm pratiShThApayati kShatra AtmAnaM
|p5  kShatra ha vai sa Atmani kShatraM vanaspatInAm pratiShThApayati,
     nyagrodha ivAvarodhair bhUmyAm prati rAShTre tiShThaty,
     ugraM hAsya rAShTram avyathyam bhavati
     ya evam etam bhakSham bhakShayati kShatriyo yajamAnaH

|c32
|p1  atha yad audumbarANy.
     Urjo vA eSho 'nnAdyAd vanaspatir ajAyata yad udumbaro,
     bhaujyaM vA etad vanaspatInAm;
     Urjam evAsmiMs tad annAdyaM ca bhaujyaM ca vanaspatInAM kShatre dadhAty
|p2  atha yad AshvatthAni.
     tejaso vA eSha vanaspatir ajAyata yad ashvatthaH,
     sAmrAjyaM vA etad vanaspatInAm;
     teja evAsmiMs tat sAmrAjyaM ca vanaspatInAM kShatre dadhAty
|p3  atha yat plAkShANi.
     yashaso vA eSha vanaspatir ajAyata yat plakShaH,
     svArAjyaM ca ha vA etad vairAjyaM ca vanaspatInAM;
     yasha evAsmiMs tat svArAjyavairAjye ca vanaspatInAM kShatre dadhAty
|p4  etAny asya purastAd upak.lptAni bhavanty, atha somaM rAjAnaM krInanti.
     te rAj~Na evAvR^itopavasathAt prativeshaish caranty,
     athaupavasathyam ahar etAny adhvaryuH purastAd upakalpayetAdhiShavaNaM
     carmAdhiShavaNe phalake droNakalashaM dashApavitram adrIn pUtabhR^itaM
     cAdhavanIyaM ca sthAlIm uda~NcanaM camasaM ca.
     tad yad etad rAjanam prAtar abhiShuNvanti, tad enAni dvedhA vigR^ihNIyAd:
     abhy anyAni sunuyAn, mAdhyaMdinAyAnyAni parishiMShyAt

|c33
|p1  tad yatraitAMsh camasAn unnayeyus, tad etaM yajamAnacamasam unnayet.
     tasmin dve darbhataruNake prAste syAtAM.
     tayor vaShaTkR^ite 'ntaHparidhi pUrvam prAsyed:
     dadhikrAvNo akAriShaM ity etayarcA sasvAhakArayA,nuvaShaTkR^ite 'param:
     A dadhikrAH shavasA pa~Nca kR^iShTIr iti
|p2  tad yatraitAMsh camasAn Ahareyus, tad etaM yajamAnacamasam Aharet.
     tAn yatrodgR^ihNIyus, tad enam upodgR^ihNIyAt.
     tad yade.lAM hotopahvayeta, yadA camasam bhakShayed,
     athainam etayA bhakShayed
|p3  yad atra shiShTaM rasinaH sutasya yad indro apibac chacIbhiH \
     idaM tad asya manasA shivena somaM rAjAnam iha bhakShayAmIti
|p4  shivo ha vA asmA eSha vAnaspatyaH shivena manasA bhakShito bhavaty,
     ugraM hAsya rAShTram avyathyam bhavati
     ya evam etam bhakSham bhakShayati kShatriyo yajamAnaH

     AtmanaH pratyabhimarsha
|p6  Ishvaro ha vA eSho 'pratyabhimR^iShTo manuShyasyAyuH pratyavahartor:
     anarhan mA bhakShayatIti.
     tad yad etenAtmAnam abhimR^ishaty, Ayur eva tat pratirata
|p7  A pyAyasva sam etu te, saM te payAMsi sam u yantu vAjA iti
     camasam ApyAyayaty abhirUpAbhyAM.
     yad yaj~Ne 'bhirUpaM tat samR^iddham

|c34
|p1  tad yatraitAMsh camasAn sAdayeyus, tad etaM yajamAnacamasaM sAdayet.
     tAn yatra prakampayeyus, tad enam anuprakampayed.
     athainam AhR^itam bhakShayen:
     narAshaMsapItasya deva soma te mativida UmaiH pitR^ibhir
     bhakShitasya bhakShayAmIti prAtaHsavane nArAshaMso bhakSha,
     Urvair iti mAdhyaMdine, kAvyair iti tR^itIyasavana
|p2  UmA vai pitaraH prAtaHsavana UrvA mAdhyaMdine kAvyAs tR^itIyasavAne,
     tad etat pitRn evAmR^itAn savanabhAjaH karoti
|p3  sarvo haiva so 'mR^ita, iti ha smAha #priyavrataH #somApo,
     yaH kashca savanabhAg ity
|p4  amR^itA ha vA asya pitaraH savanabhAjo bhavanty,
     ugraM hAsya rAShTram avyathyam bhavati
     ya evam etam bhakSham bhakShayati kShatriyo yajamAnaH
|p5  samAna AtmanaH pratyabhimarshaH, samAnam ApyAyanaM camasasya
|p6  prAtaHsavanasyaivAvR^itA prAtaHsavane careyur,
     mAdhyaMdinasya mAdhyaMdine, tR^itIyasavanasya tR^itIyasavane
|p7  tam evam etam bhakSham provAca #rAmo #mArgaveyo #vishvaMtarAya #sauShadmanAya
|p8  tasmin hovAca prokte:
     sahasram u ha brAhmaNa tubhyaM dadmaH, sashyAparNa u me yaj~Na ity
|p9  etam u haiva provAca #turaH #kAvaSheyo #janamejayAya #pArikShitAyaitam
     u haiva procatuH #parvatanAradau #somakAya #sAhadevyAya,
     #sahadevAya #sAr~NjayAya, #babhrave #daivAvR^idhAya, #bhimAya #vaidarbhAya,
     #nagnajite #gAndhArAyaitam u haiva &0 provAcAshniH #sanashrutAyArimdamAya,
     #kratuvide #jAnakaya, etam u haiva provAca #vasiShThaH #sudAse #paijavanAya.
     te ha te sarva eva mahaj jagmur etam bhakSham bhakShayitvA,
     sarve haiva mahArAjA Asur, #Aditya iva ha sma shriyAm
     pratiShThitAs tapanti sarvAbhyo digbhyo balim Avahanta
|p10  #Aditya iva ha vai shriyAm pratiShThitas tapati,
     sarvAbhyo digbhyo balim Avahaty, ugraM hAsya rAShTram avyathyam bhavati
     ya evam etam bhakSham bhakShayati kShatriyo yajamAno yajamAnaH

|bAB8 {pa~NcikA 8}

|c1 {adhyAya 36, khaNDaH 1-4}
|p1  athAtaH stutashastrayor evai/kAhikam
|p2  prAtaHsavanam, aikAhikaM tR^itIyasavanam.
     ete vai shAnte k.lpte pratiShThite savane yad aikAhike,
     shAntyai k.lptyai pratiShThityA apracyutyA
|p3  ukto mAdhyaMdinaH pavamAno ya ubhayasAmno
     bR^ithatpR^iShThasyobhe hi sAmanI kriyete
|p4  A tvA rathaM yathotaya, idaM vaso sutam andha iti
     rAthaMtarI pratipad rAthaMtaro 'nucaraH.
     pavamAnokthaM vA etad yan marutvatIyam.
     pavamA~Ne vA atra rathaMtaraM kurvanti bR^ihat pR^iShThaM, savIvadhatAyai.
     tad idaM rathaMtaraM stutam AbhyAm pratipadanucarAbhyAm anushaMsaty
|p5  atho brahma vai rathaMtaraM kShatraM bR^ihad,
     brahma khalu vai kShatrAt pUrvam:
     brahmapurastAn ma ugraM rAShTram avyathyam asad ity.
     athAnnaM vai rathaMtaram, annam evAsmai tat purastAt kalpayaty.
     atheyaM vai pR^ithivI rathaMtaram, iyaM khalu vai pratiShTha,
     pratiShThAm evAsmai tat purastAt kalpayati
|p6  samAna indranihavo 'vibhaktaH, so 'hnAm.
     udvAn brAhmaNaspatya ubhayasAmno rUpam, ubhe hi sAmanI kriyete
|p7  samAnyo dhAyya avibhaktAs, tA ahnAm
|p8  aikAhiko marutvatIyaH pragAthaH

|c2
|p1  janiShThA ugraH sahase turAyeti sUktam ugravat sahasvat,
     tat kShatrasya rUpam.
     mandra ojiShTha ity ojasvat, tat kShatrasya rUpam.
     bahulAbhimAna ity abhivad, abhibhUtyai rUpaM.
     tad ekAdasharcam bhavaty, ekAdashAkSharA vai triShTup,
     traiShTubo vai rAjanya.
     ojo vA indriyaM vIryaM triShTub, ojaH kShatraM vIryaM rAjanyas;
     tad enam ojasA kShatreNa vIryeNa samardhayati.
     tad gaurivItam bhavaty.
     etad vai marutvatIyaM samR^iddhaM yad gaurivItaM, tasyoktam brAhmaNaM
|p2  tvAm id dhi havAmaha iti bR^ihatpR^iShTham bhavati.
     kShatraM vai bR^ihat, kShatreNaiva tat kShatraM samardhayaty.
     atho kShatraM vai bR^ihad, AtmA yAjamAnasya niShkevalyaM.
     tad yad bR^ihatpR^iShTham bhavati, kShatraM vai bR^ihat,
     kShatreNaivainaM tat samardhayaty.
     atho jyaiShThyaM vai bR^ihaj, jyaiShThyenaivainaM tat samardhayaty.
     atho shraiShThyaM vai bR^ihac, chraiShThyenaivainaM tat samardhayaty
|p3  abhi tvA shUra nonuma iti rathaMtaram anurUpaM kurvanty.
     ayaM vai loko rathaMtaram, asau loko bR^ihad;
     asya vai lokasyAsau loko 'nurUpo, 'muShya lokasyAyaM loko 'nurUpas.
     tad yad rathaMtaram anurUpaM kurvanty,
     ubhAv eva tal lokau yajamAnAya sambhoginau kurvanty.
     atho brahma vai rathaMtaraM kShatram bR^ihad,
     brahmaNi khalu vai kShatram pratiShThitaM
     kShatre brahmAtho sAmna eva sayonitAyai
|p4  yad vAvAneti dhAyyA, tasyA uktam brAhmaNam
|p5  ubhayaM shR^iNavac ca na iti sAmapragAtha ubhayasAmno rUpam,
     ubhe hi sAmanI kriyete

|c3
|p1  tam u ShTuhi yo abhibhUtyojA iti sUktam abhivad abhibhUtyai rUpam
|p2  aShA.lham ugraM sahamAnam Abhir ity ugravat sahamAnavat,
     tat kShatrasya rUpaM
|p3  tat pa~Ncadasharcam bhavaty.
     ojo vA indriyaM vIryam pa~Ncadasha, ojaH kShatraM vIryam rAjanyas,
     tad enam ojasA kShatreNa vIryeNa samardhayati
|p4  tad bhAradvAjam bhavati.
     bhAradvAjaM vai bR^ihad, ArSheyeNa salomaisha
|p5  ha vAva kShatriyayaj~NaH samR^iddho, yo bR^ihatpR^iShThas.
     tasmAd yatra kvaca kShatriyo yajeta, bR^ihad eva tatra pR^iShThaM syAt.
     tat samR^iddham

|c4
|p1  aikAhikA hotrA.
     etA vai shAntAH k.lptAH pratiShThitA hotrA yad aikAhikAH,
     shAntyai k.lptyai pratiShThityA apracyutyai.
     tAH sarvarUpA bhavanti sarvasamR^iddhAH, sarvarUpatAyai sarvasamR^iddhyai:
     sarvarUpAbhir hotrAbhiH sarvasamR^iddhAbhiH sarvAn kAmAn avApnavAmeti.
     tasmAd yatra kvacaikAhA asarvastomA asarvapR^iShThA,
     aikAhikA eva tatra hotrAH syus.
     tat samR^iddham
|p2  ukthya evAyam pa~NcadashaH syAd, ity Ahur.
     ojo vA indriyaM vIryam pa~Ncadasha, ojaH kShatraM vIryaM rAjanyas,
     tad enam ojasA kShatreNa vIryeNa samardhayati
|p3  tasya triMshat stutashastrANi bhavanti.
     triMshadakSharA vai virAD, virAD annAdyaM,
     virAjy evainaM tad annAdye pratiShThApayati.
     tasmAt tadukthyaH pa~NcadashaH syAd, ity Ahur
|p4  jyotiShToma evAgniShTomaH syAd
|p5  brahma vai stomAnAM trivR^it kShatram pa~Ncadasho,
     brahma khalu vai kShatrAt pUrvam:
     brahmapurastAn na ugraM rAShTram avyathyam asad iti.
     vishaH saptadashaH shaudro varNa ekaviMsho,
     vishaM caivAsmai tac chaudraM ca varNam anuvartmAnau kurvanty.
     atho tejo vai stomAnAM trivR^id vIryam pa~NcadashaH prajAtiH saptadashaH
     pratiShThaikaviMshas, tad enaM tejasA vIryeNa prajAtyA
     pratiShThayAntataH samardhayati.
     tasmAj jyotiShTomaH syAt
|p6  tasya caturviMshatiH stutashastrANi bhavanti.
     caturviMsatyardhamAso vai saMvatsaraH, saMvatsare kR^itsnam annAdyaM,
     kR^itsna evainaM tad annAdye pratiShThApayati.
     tasmAj jyotiShToma evAgniShTomaH syAd agniShTomaH syAt

|c5 {adhyAya 37, khaNDaH 1-7}
|p1  athAtaH punarabhiShekasyaiva
|p2  sUyate ha vA asya kShatraM, yo dIkShate kShatriyaH san.
     sa yadAvabhR^itAd udetyAnUbandhyayeShTvodavasyaty,
     athainam udavasAnIyAyAM saMsthitAyAm punar abhiShi~Ncanti
|p3  tasyaite purastAd eva sambhArA upak.lptA bhavanty:
     audumbary AsandI.
     tasyai prAdeshamAtrAH pAdAH syur, aratnimAtrANi shIrShaNyAnUcyAni.
     mau~NjaM vivayanaM, vyAghracarmAstaraNam, audumbarash camasa, udumbarashAkhA.
     tasminn etasmiMsh camase 'ShTAtayAni niShutAni bhavanti:
     dadhi madhu sarpir AtapavarShyA ApaH shaShpANi ca tokmAni ca surA dUrvA
|p4  tad yaiShA dakShiNA sphyavartanir veder bhavati,
     tatraitAm prAcIm AsandIm pratiShThApayati.
     tasyA antarvedi dvau pAdau bhavato bahirvedi dvAv.
     iyaM vai shrIs.
     tasyA etat parimitaM rUpaM yad antarvedy,
     athaiSha bhUmAparimito yo bahirvedi.
     tad yad asyA antarvedi dvau pAdau bhavato bahirvedi dvA,
     ubhayoH kAmayor upAptyai yash cAntarvedi yash ca bahirvedi

|c6
|p1  vyAghracarmaNAstR^iNAty uttaralomnA prAcInagrIveNa.

|p1  atha yad audumbary AsandI bhavaty audumbarash camasa udumbarashAkhorg

|c10
|p1  devAsurA vA eShu lokeShu saMyetire.

|c11

|c12 {adhyAya 38, khaNDaH 1-3}
|p1  athAta aindro mahAbhiShekas
|p2  te devA abruvan saprajApatikA:
     ayaM vai devAnAm ojiShTho baliShThaH sahiShThaH sattamaH pArayiShNutama,
     imam evAbhiShi~NcAmahA iti. tatheti.
     tad vai tad #indram eva
|p3  tasmA etAm AsandIM samabharann R^icaM nAma.
     tasyai bR^ihac ca rathaMtaraM ca pUrvau pAdAv akurvan,
     vairUpaM ca vairAjaM cAparau,
     shAkvararaivate shIrShaNye, naudhasaM ca kAleyaM cAnUcye,
     R^icaH prAcInAtAnAn, sAmAni tirashcInavAyAn, yajUMShy atIkAshAn,
     yasha AstaraNaM, shriyam upabarhaNaM.
     tasyai #savitA ca #bR^ihaspatish ca pUrvau pAdAv adhArayatAM,
     #vAyush ca #pUShA cAparau, #mitrAvaruNau shIrShaNye, #ashvinAv anUcye.
     sa etAm AsandIm Arohad
|p4  #vasavas tvA gAyatreNa chandasA trivR^itA stomena rathaMtareNa sAmnArohantu,
     tAn anv ArohAmi sAmrAjyAya.
     #rudrAs tvA traiShTubhena chandasA pa~Ncadashena stomena bR^ihata sAmnArohantu,
     tAn anv ArohAmi bhaujyAyA,
     dityAs tvA jAgatena chandasA saptadashena stomena vairUpeNa sAmnArohantu,
     tAn anv ArohAmi svArAjyAya.
     #vishve tvA devA AnuShTubhena chandasaikaviMshena
     stomena vairAjena sAmnArohantu, tAn anv ArohAmi vairAjyAya.
     #sAdhyAsh ca tvAptyAsh ca devAH pA.Nktena chandasA triNavena
     stomena shAkvareNa sAmnArohantu, tAn anv ArohAmi rAjyAya.
     #marutash ca tvA.Ngirasash ca devA atichandasA chandasA trayastri.Nshena
     stomena raivatena sAmnArohantu,
     tAn anv ArohAmi pArameShThyAya mAhArAjyAyAdhipatyAya
     svAvashyAyAtiShThAyArohAmIty etAm AsandIm Arohat
|p5  tam etasyAm AsandyAm AsInaM vishve devA abruvan:
     na vA anabhyutkruShTa #indro vIryaM kartum arhaty,
     abhy enam utkroshAmeti. taitieti.
     tAM vishve devA abhyudakroshann:
     imaM devA abhyutkroshata samrAjaM sAmrAjyam bhojam bhojapitaraM
     svarAjaM svArAjyaM virAjaM vairAjyaM
     rAjAnaM rAjapitaram parameShTinam pArameShThyaM.
     kShatram ajani, kShatriyo 'jani, vishvasya bhUtasyAdhipatir ajani,
     vishAm attAjani, purAm bhettAjany,
     asurANAM hantAjani, brahmANo goptAjani, dharmasya goptAjanIti
|p6  tam abhyutkruShTam #prajApatir abhiShekShyann etayarcAbhyamantrayata

|c13
|p1  ni ShasAda dhR^itavrato varuNaH pastyAsv A \

|c14
|p1  athainam prAcyAM dishi #vasavo devAH ShaDbhish caiva pa~NcaviMshair ahobhir

     caiva pa~NcAviMshair ahobhir abhyaShi~Ncann etena ca tR^icenaitena

     ca tR^icenaitena ca yajuShaitAbhish ca vyAhR^itibhiH svArAjyAya.

     janapadA #uttatakurava #uttaramadrA iti vairAjyAyaiva te 'bhiShicyante,

     etena ca tR^icenatiena ca yajuShaitAbhish ca vyAhR^itibhI rAjyAya.
     tasmAd asyAM dhruvAyAm madhyamAyAm pratiShThAyAM disi ye keca
     #kurupa~NcAlAnAM rAjAnaH savashoshInarANAM rAjyAyaiva te 'bhiShicyante,

     ca yajuShaitAbhish ca vyAhR^itbhiH pArameShThyAya mAhArAjyAyAdhipatyAya
     svAvashyAyAtiShThAyeti.
     sa parameShThI prAjApatyo 'bhavat
|p4  sa etena mahAbhiShekeNAbhiShikta #indraH sarvA jitIr ajayat,
     sarvA~Ml lokAn avindat,
     sarveShAM devAnAM shraiShThyam atiShThAm paramAtam agachat,
     sAmrAjyam bhaujyaM svArAjyaM vairAjyam pArameShThyaM rAjyam

     'muShmin svarge loke sarvAn kAmAn AptvAmR^itaH samabhavat samabhavat

|c15 {adhyAya 39, khaNDaH 1-9}
|p1  sa ya iched evaMvit kShatriyam:
     AyaM sarvA jitIr jayetAyaM sarvA~Ml lokAn vindetAyaM sarveShAM rAj~NAM
     shraiShThyam atiShThAm paramatAM gacheta sAmrAjyam bhaujyaM svArAjyaM
     vairAjyam pArameShThyaM rAjyam mAhArAjyam Adhipatyam,
     ayaM samantaparyAyI syAt sArvabhaumaH sArvAyuSha,
     AntAd A pararArdhAt pR^ithivyai samudraparyantAyA ekarA.l iti:
     taM etenaindreNa mahAbhiShekeNa kShatriyaM shApayitvA 'bhiShi~Nced
|p2  yAM ca rAtrIm &1 ajAyathA yAM ca pretAsi, tad ubhayam antareNeShTApUrtaM
     te lokaM sukR^itam AyuH prajAM &1 vR^i~NjIya yadi me druhyer iti
|p3  sa ya iched evaMvit kShatriyo:
     'haM sarvA jitIr jayeyam, ahaM sarvAMl lokAn vindeyam,
     ahaM sarveShAM rAj~NAM shraiShThyam atiShThAm paramatAM
     gacheyaM sAmrAjyam bhaujyaM svArAjyam vairAjyam pArameShThyaM
     rAjyam mAhArAjyam Adhipatyam,
     ahaM samantaparyAyI syAM sArvabhaumaH sArvAyuSha,
     AntAd A parArdhat pR^ithivyai samudraparyantAyA ekarA.l iti:
     sa na vicikitset, sa brUyat saha shraddhayA:
     yAM ca rAtrIm ajAye 'haM yAM ca pretAsmi,
     tad ubhayam antareNeShTApUrtam me lokaM sukR^itam AyuH prajAM
     vR^i~NjIthA yadi te druhyeyam iti

|c16
|p1  atha tato brUyac:
     catuShTayAni vAnaspatyAni sambharata,
     naiyagrodhAny audumbarANy AshvatthAni plAkShANIti
|p2  kShatraM vA etad vanaspatInAM yan nyagrodho:
     yan naiyagrodhAni sambharanti, kShatram evAsmiMs tad dadhAti.
     bhaujyaM vA etad vanaspatInAM yad udumbaro:
     yad audumbarANi sambharanti, bhaujyam evAsmiMs tad dadhAti.
     sAmrAjyaM vA etad vanaspatInAM yad ashvattho:
     yad AshvatthAni sambharanti, sAmrAjyam evAsmiMs tad dadhAti.
     svArAjyaM ca ha vA etad vairAjyaM ca vanaspatInAM yat plakSho:
     yat plAkShANi sambharanti, svArAjyavairAjye evAsmiMs tad dadhAty
|p3  atha tato brUyAc:
     catuShTayAny auShadhAni sambharata,
     tokmakR^itAni vrIhINAm mahAvrIhINAm priyaMgUnAM yavAnAm iti
|p4  kShatraM vA etad oShadhInAM yad vrIhayo:
     yad vrIhINAM tokma sambharanti, kShatram evAsmiMs tad dadhAti.
     sAmrAjyaM vA etad oShadhInAM yan mahAvrIhayo:
     yan mAhAvrIhINAM tokma sambharanti, sAmrAjyam evAsmiMs tad dadhAti.
     bhaujyaM vA etad oShadhInAM yat priyaMgavo:
     yat priyaMgUnAM tokma sambharanti, bhaujyam evAsmiMs tad dadhAti.
     sainAnyaM vA etad oShadhInAM yad yavA.
     yad yavAnAM tokma sambharanti, sainAnyam evAsmiMs tad dadhAti

|c17
|p1  athAsmA audumbarIm AsandIM sambharanti, tasyA uktam brAhmaNam.
     audumbarash camaso vA pAtrI vodumbarashAkhA.
     tAn etAn sambhArAn sambhR^ityaudumbaryAm pAtryAM vA camase vA samAvapeyus,
     teShu samopteShu dadhi madhu sarpir AtapavarShyA Apo
     'bhyAnIya pratiShThApyaitam AsandIm abhimantrayeta
|p2  bR^ihac ca te rathaMtaraM ca pUrvau pAdau bhavatAM,
     vairUpaM ca vairAjaM cAparau, shAkvararaivate shIrShaNye,
     naudhasaM ca kAleyaM cAnUcye, R^icaH prAcInAtAnAh sAmAni tirashcInavAyA,
     yajUMShy atIkAshA, yasha AstaraNaM, shrIr upabarhaNaM.
     #savitA ca te #bR^ihaspatish ca pUrvau pAdau dhArayatAM,
     #vAyush ca #pUShA cAparau, #mitrAvaruNau shIrShaNye, #ashvinAv anUcye ity
|p3  athainaM etAm AsandIm Arohayed
|p4  #vasavas tvA gAyatreNa chandasA trivR^itA stomena rathaMtareNa sAmnArohantu,
     tAn anv Aroha sAmrAjyAya.
     #rudrAs tvA traiShTubhena chandasA pa~Ncadashena stomena bR^ihatA sAmnArohantu,
     tAn anv Aroha bhaujyAyA, dityAs tvA jAgatena chandasA
     saptadashena stomena vairUpeNa sAmnArohantu, tAn anv Aroha svArAjyAya.
     #vishve tvA devA AnuShTubhena chandasaikaviMshena stomena vairAjena
     sAmnArohantu, tAn anv Aroha vairAjyAya.
     #marutash ca tvA.Ngirasash ca devA atichandasA chandasA trayastriMshena
     stomena raivatena sAmnArohantu, tAn anv Aroha pArameShThyAya.
     #sAdhyAsh ca tvAptyAsh ca devAH pA.Nktena chandasA
     triNavena stomena shAkvareNa sAmnArohantu,
     tAn anv Aroha rAjyAya mAhArAjyAyAdhipatyAya svAvashyAyAtiShThAyArohety
     etAm AsandIm Arohayet
|p5  tam etasyAm AsandyAm AsInaM rAjakartAro brUyur:
     na vA anabhyutkruShTaH kShatriyo vIryaM kartum arhaty,
     abhy enam utkroshAmeti. tatheti.
     taM rAjakartAro 'bhyutkroshantI,maM janA abhyutkroshata samrAjaM
     sAmrAjyam bhojam bhojapitaraM svarAjaM svArAjyaM virAjaM vairAjyam
     parameShThinam pArameShThyaM rAjAnAM rAjapitaraM.
     kShatram ajani, kShatriyo 'jani, vishvasya bhUtasyAdhipatir ajani,
     vishAm attAjany, amitrANAM hantAjani, brAhmaNAnAm goptAjani,
     dharmasya goptAjanIti
|p6  tam abhyutkruShTam evaMvid abhiShekShyann etayarcAbhimantrayeta

|c18
|p1  ni ShasAda dhR^itavrato varuNaH pastyAsv A \
     sAmrAjyAya bhaujyAya svArAjyAya vairAjyAya pArameShThyAya
     rAjyAya mAhArAjyAyAdhipatyAya svAvashyAyAtiShThAya sukratur iti.
     tam etasyAm AsandyAm AsInam evaMvit purastAt tiShThan pratya.Nmukha
     audumbaryArdrayA shAkhayA sapalAshayA jAtarUpamayena ca
     pavitreNAntardhAyAbhiShi~NcatimA ApaH shivatamA ity etena tR^icena,
     devasya tveti ca yajuShA, bhUr bhuvaH svar ity etAbhish ca vyAhR^itibhiH

|c19
|p1  prAcyAM tvA dishi #vasavo devAH ShaDbhish caiva pa~NcaviMshair ahobhir
     abhiShi~Ncantv etena ca tR^icenaitena ca
     yajuShaitAbhish ca vyAhR^itibhiH sAmrAjyAya.
     dakShiNasyAM tvA dishi #rudrA devAH ShaDbhish caiva pa~NcaviMshair
     ahobhir abhiShi~Ncantv etena ca tR^icenaitena ca yajuShaitAbhish
     ca vyAhR^itibhir bhaujyAya.
     pratIcyAM tvA dishy #AdityA devAH ShaDbhish caiva pa~NcaviMshair ahobhir
     abhiShi~Ncantv etena ca tR^icenaitena ca yajuShaitAbhish ca vyAhR^itibhiH
     svArAjyAyo,dIcyAM tvA dishi #vishve devAH ShaDbhish
     caiva pa~Ncavinshair ahobhir abhiShi~Ncantv etena ca tR^icenaitenA ca
     yajuShaitAbhish cA vyAhR^itibhir vairAjyAyo,rdhvAyAM tvA dishi #marutash
     cA.NgirAsash ca devAH ShaDbhish caiva pa~NcaviMshair ahobhir abhiShi~Ncantv
     etena ca tR^icenaitena ca yajuShaitAbhish ca vyAhbR^itibhiH pArameShThyAyA,syAM
     tvA dhruvAyAM madhyamAyAm pratiShThAyAM dishi #sAdhyAsh cAptyAsh ca
     devAH ShaDbhish caiva pa~NcaviMshair ahobhir abhiShi~Ncantv etena
     ca tR^icenaitena ca yajuShaitAbhish ca
     vyAhR^itibhI rAjyAya mAhArAjyAdhipatyAya svAvashyAyAdhiShThAyeti.
     sa parameShThI prAjApatyo bhavati
|p2  sa etenaindrena mahAbhiShekeNAbhiShiktaH kShatriyaH sarvA jitIr jayati,
     sarvAMl lokAn vindati,
     sarveShAM rAj~NAM shraiShThyam atiShThAm paramatAM gachati,
     sAmrAjyam bhaujyaM svArAjyam pArameShThyaM
     rAjyam mAhArAjyam AdhipatyaM jitvAsmi~Ml loke svayambhUH svarA.l amR^ito,
     'muShmin svarge loke sarvAn kAmAn AptvAmR^itaH sambhavati
     yam etenanidrena mahAbhiShekeNa kShatriyaM shApayitvA bhiShi~Ncati

|c20
|p1  indriyaM vA etad asmi~Ml loke yad dadhi:
     yad dadhnAbhiShi~NcatIndriyam evAsmiMs tad dadhAti.
     raso vA eSha oShadhivanaspatiShu yan madhu:
     yan madhvAbhiShi~Ncati, rasam evAsmiMs tad dadhAti.
     tejo vA etat pashUnAM yad ghR^itaM:
     yad ghR^itenAbhiShi~Ncati, teja evAsmiMs tad dadhAty.
     amR^itaM vA etad asmi~Ml loke yad Apo:
     yad adbhir abhiShi~Ncaty, amR^itatvam evAsmiMs tad dadhAti
|p2  so 'bhiShikto 'bhiShektre brAhmaNAya hiraNyaM dadyAt,
     sahasraM dadyAt, kShetraM catuShpAd dadyAd.
     athApy Ahur:
     asaMkhyAtam evAparimitaM dadyAd;
     aparimito vai kShatriyo 'parimitasyAvaruddhyA ity
|p3  athAsmai surAkaMsaM hasta AdadhAti:
     svAdiShThayA madiShThayA pavasva soma dhArayA \
     indrAya pAtave suta iti
|p4  tAm pibed:
     yad atra shiShTaM rasinaH sutasya yad indro apibac chacIbhiH \
     idaM tad asya manasA shivena somaM rAjAnam iha bhakShAyami \\
     abhi tvA vR^iShabhA sute sutaM sR^ijAmi pItaye \
     tR^impa vy ashnuhI madam iti
|p5  yo ha vAva somapIthaH surAyAm praviShTaH,
     sa haiva tenaindreNa mahAbhiShekeNAbhiShiktasya kShatriyasya bhakShito
     bhavati na surA
|p6  tAm pItvAbhimantrayeta,pAma somaM, shaM no bhaveti
|p7  tad yathaivAdaH priyaH putraH pitaram priyA vA jAyA
     patiM sukhaM shivam upaspR^ishaty A visrasa,
     evaM haivaitenaindreNa mahAbhiShekeNAbhiShiktasya kShatriyasya surA
     vA somo vAnyad vAnnAdyaM sukhaM shivam upaspR^ishaty A visrasaH

|c21
|p1  etena ha vA aindrena mahAbhiShekeNa #turaH #kAvaSheyo #janamejayam
     #pArikShitam abhiShiSheca.
     tasmAd u #janamejayaH #pArikShitaH samantaM sarvataH pR^ithivIn
     jayan parIyAyAshvena ca medhyeneje
|p2  tad eShAbhi yaj~NagAthA gIyate \
|p3  #AsandIvati dhAnyAdaM rukmiNaM haritasrajam \
     ashvam bahandha sAra.NgaM devebhyo #janamejaya ity
|p4  etena ha vA anidreNa mahAbhiShekeNa #cyavano
     #bhArgavaH #shAryAtam #mAnavam abhiShiSheca.
     tasmAd u #shAryAto #mAnavaH samantaM sarvataH pR^ithivIM

     #shatAnIkaM #sAtrAjitam abhiShiSheca.
     tasmAd u #shatanIkaH #sAtrAjitaH samantaM sarvataH

     ar.Ngrasainyam abhiShiShicatus.

          #vishvakarman #bhauvana mAM didAsitha \
          nima.NkShye 'haM salilasya madhye
          moghas ta eSha #kashyapAyAsa saMgara
     ity
|p11  etena ha vA aindreNa mahAbhiShekeNa #vasiShThah
      #sudAsam #paijavanam abhiShiSheca.
      tasmAd u #sudAH #paijavanaH samantaM sarvataH pR^ithivIM
      jayan parIyAyAshvena ca medhyeneja

      tasmAd u #marotta #AvikShitaH samantaM
      sarvataH pR^ithivIM jayan parIyAyAshvena ca medhyeneje

|p14      #marutaH pariveShTAro #maruttasyAvasan gR^ihe \
          #AvikShitasya #kAmaprer vishve devAH sabhAsada
     iti

|c22
|p1  etena ha vA aindreNa mahAbhiShekeNodamaya #Atreyo '.Ngam abhiShiSheca.
     tasmAd v #A.NgaH samantaM sarvataH pR^ithivIM
     jayan parIyAyAshvena ca medhyeneje
|p2  sa hovAcAlopA.Ngo:
     dasha nAgasahasrANi dasha dAsIsahasrANi dadAmi te brAhmaNopa
     mAsmin yaj~Ne hvayasveti

|c23
|p1  #etena ha vA aindreNa mahAbhiShekeNa #dIrghatamA
     #mAmateyo #bharataM #dauHShantim abhiShiSheca.
     tasmAd u #bharato #dauHShantiH samantaM sarvataH pR^ithivIM
     jayan parIyAyAshvair u ca medhyair Ije

          #maShNAre #bharato 'dadAc chatam badvAni sapta ca \\

          #ga.NgAyAM #vR^itraghne 'badhnAt pa~Ncapa~NcAshataM hayAn \\
|p6       trayastriMshacchataM rAjAshvAn baddhvAya medhyAn \
          #dauHShantir atyagAd rAj~No &0 'mAyAn &0 mAyavattaraH \\

          divam martya iva hastAbhyAM nodApuH pa~Nca mAnavA

|p8  etaM ha vA aindram mahAbhiShekam #bR^ihaduktha
     R^iShir #durmukhAya #pA~NcAlAya provAca.
     tasmAd u #durmukhaH #pA~NcAlo rAjA san vidyayA samantaM
     sarvataH pR^ithivIM jayan parIyAyai/taM
|p9  ha vA aindram mahAbhiShekaM #vAsiShThaH #sAtyahavyo
     'tyarAtaye #jAnaMtapaye provAca.
     tasmAd v #atyatrAtir #jAnaMtapir arAjA san vidyayA
     samantaM sarvataH pR^ithivIM jayan parIyAya

     'jaiShIr vai samantaM sarvataH pR^ithivIm, mahan mA gamayeti.
     sa hovAcAtyarAtir #jAnaMtapir:
     yadA brAhmaNottarakurU~N jayeyam,
     atha tvam u haiva pR^ithivyai rAjA syAH,
     senApatir eva te 'haM syAm iti.
     sa hovAca #vAsiShThaH #sAtyahavyo:
     devakShetraM vai tan, na vai tan martyo jetum arhaty:
     adrukSho vai ma, Ata idaM dada iti.
     tato hAtyarAtiM #jAnaMtapim AttavIryaM niHshukram #amitratapanaH
     #shuShmiNaH #shaibyo rAjA jaghAna
|p11  tasmAd evaM viduShe brAhmaNAyaivaM cakruShe na kShatriyo druhyen:
     ned rAShTrad &1 avapadyeya, ned vA mA prANo jahad iti jahad iti

|c24 {adhyAya 40, khaNDaH 1-5}
|p1  athAtaH purodhAyA eva
|p2  na ha vA apurohitasya raj~No devA annam adanti.
     tasmAd rAjA yakShyamANo brAhmaNam purodadhIta:
     devA me 'nnam adann ity
|p3  agnIn vA eSha svargyAn rAjoddharate yat purohitaM
|p4  tasya purohita evAhavanIyo bhavati,
     jAyA gArhapatyaH, putro 'nvAhAryapacanaH.
     sa yat purohitAya karoty AhavanIya eva taj juboty,
     atha yaj jAyAyai karoti gArhapatya eya taj juhoty,
     atha yat putrAya karoty anvAhAryapacana eva taj juhoti.
     ta enaM shAntatanavo 'bhihutA abhiprItAH svargaM lokam
     abhivahanti kShatraM ca balaM ca rAShTraM ca vishaM ca
|p5  ta evainam ashAntatanavo 'nabhibutA anabhiprItAH svargAl
     lokAn nudante kShatrAc ca balAc ca rAShTrAc ca vishash cA/gnir
|p6  vA eSha vaishvAnaraH pa~Ncamenir yat purohitas.
     tasya vAcy evaikA menir bhavati pAdayor ekA
     tvacy ekA hR^idaya ekopastha ekA.
     tAbhir jvalantIbhir dIpyamAnAbhir upodeti rAjAnaM.
     sa yad Aha:
     kva bhagavo 'vAtsIs, tR^iNAny asmA Aharateti,
     tenAsya tAM shamayati yAsya vAci menir bhavaty.
     atha yad asmA udakam Anayanti pAdyaM,
     tenAsya tAM shamayati yAsya pAdayor menir bhavaty.
     atha yad enam alaMkurvanti,
     tenAsya tAM shamayati yAsya tvaci menir bhavaty.
     atha yad enaM tarpayanti,
     tenAsya tAM shamayati yAsya hR^idaye menir bhavaty.
     atha yad asyAnAruddho veshmasu vasati,
     tenAsya tAM shamayati yAsyopasthe menir bhavati
|p7  sa enaM shAntatanur abhihuto 'bhiprItaH svargaM lokam
     abhivahati kShatraM ca balaM ca rAShTraM ca vishaM ca.
     sa evainam ashAntatanur anabhihuto 'nabhiprItaH svArgal lokAn
     nudate kShatrAc ca balAc ca rAShTrAc ca vishash ca

|c25
|p1  agnir vA eSha vaishvAnaraH pa~Ncamenir yat purohitas,
     tAbhI rAjAnam parigR^ihya tiShThati samudra iva bhUmim
|p2  ayuvamAry asya rAShTram bhavati,
     nainam purAyuShaH prANo jahAty,
     AjarasaM jIvati, sarvam Ayur eti,
     na punar mriyate yasyaivaM vidvAn brAhmaNo rAShTragopaH purohitaH
|p3  kShatreNa kShatraM jayati,
     balena balam ashnute yasyaivaM vidvAn brAhmaNo rAShTragopaH purohitas
|p4  tasmai vishaH saMjAnate sammukhA ekamanaso yasyaivaM
     vidvAn brAhmaNo rAShTragopaH purohitaH

|c26
|p1  tad apy etad R^iShiNoktaM
|p2  sa id rAjA pratijanyAni vishvA shuShmeNa tasthAv abhi vIryeNeti
|p3  sapatnA vai dviShanto, bhrAtR^ivyA janyAni,
     tAn eva tac chuShmeNa vIryeNAdhitiShThati
|p4  #bR^ihaspatiM yaH subhR^itam bibhartIti.
     #bR^ithaspatir ha vai devAnAm purohitas,
     tam anv anye manuShyarAj~NAm purohitA.
     #bR^ihaspatiM yaH subhR^itam bibhartIti yad Aha,
     purohitaM yaH subhR^itaM bibhartIty eva tad Aha
|p5  valgUyati vandate pUrvabhAjam ity,
     apacitim evAsmA etad Aha
|p6  sa it kSheti sudhita okasi sva iti.
     gR^ihA vA okaH, sveShv eva tad gR^iheShu suhito vasati
|p7  tasmA i.lA pinvate vishvadAnIm ity.
     annaM vA i.lAnnam evAsmA etad Urjasvac chashvad bhavati
|p8  tasmai vishaH svayam evA namanta iti.
     rAShTrANi vai visho,
     rAShTrANy evainaM tat svayam upanamanti
|p9  yasmin brahmA rAjani pUrva etIti.
     purohitam evaitad AhA/pratIto
|p10  jayati saM dhanAnIti.
     rAShTrANi vai dhanAni, tAny apratIto jayati
|p11  pratijanyAny uta yA sajanyeti.
     sapatnA vai dviShanto bhrAtR^ivyA janyAni,
     tAn apratIto jayaty
|p12  avasyave yo varivaH kR^iNotIti yad AhAvasIyase
     yo vasIyaH karotIty eva tad Aha
|p13  brahmaNe rAjA tam avanti devA iti,
     purohitam evaitad abhivadati

|c27
|p1  yo na vai trIn purohitAMs trIn purodhAtRn veda,
     sa brAhmaNaH purohitaH.
     sa vadeta purodhAyA:
     #agnir vAva purohitaH pR^ithivI purodhAtA,
     #vAyur vAva purohito 'ntarikSham purodhAtAdityo vAva purohito
     dyauH purodhAtai,Sha ha vai purohito
     ya evaM vedAtha sa tirohito ya evaM na veda
|p2  tasya rAjA mitram bhavati,
     dviShantam apabAdhate yasyaivaM vidvAn
     brAhmaNo rAShTragopaH purohitaH
|p3  kShatreNa kShatraM jayati,
     balena balam ashnute yasyaivaM vidvAn brAhmaNo rAShTragopaH purohitas.
     tasmai vishaH saMjAnate sammukhA ekamanaso
     yasyaivaM vidvAn brAhmaNo rAShTragopaH purohito
|p4  bhUr bhuvaH svar om, amo 'ham asmi sa tvaM sa tvaM asy amo 'haM,
     dyaur aham pR^ithivI tvaM, sAmAham R^ik tvaM, tAv eha saMvahAvahai \
     &5 purA &5 aNyasmAt mahAbhayAt \ tanUr asi tanvam me pAhi \
|p5  yA oShadhiH somarAj~NIr bahvIH shatavicakShaNAh \
     tA mahyam asminn Asane 'chidraM sharma yachata \\
|p6  yA oShadhIH somarAj~NIr viShThitAH pR^ithivIm anu \
     tA mahyam asminn Asane 'chidraM sharma yachata \\
|p7  asmin rAShTre shriyam A veshayAmy ato devIH prati pashyAmy ApaH \\
|p8  dakShiNam pAdam ava nenije 'smin rAShTra indriyaM dadhAmi \
     savyam pAdam ava nenije 'smi rAShTra indriyaM vardhayAmi \
     pUrvam anyam aparam anyam pAdAv ava nenije \
     devA rAShTrasya guptyA abhayasyAvaruddhyai \\
|p9  ApaH pAdAvanejanIr dviShantaM nir dahantu me

|c28
|p1  athAto brahmanaH parimaro.
     yo ha vai brahmaNaH parimaraM veda,
     pary enaM dviShanto bhrAtR^ivyAH pari sapatnA mriyante
|p2  'yaM vai brahma yo 'yam pavate.
     tam etAH pa~Nca devatAH parimriyante:
     vidyud vR^iShTish candramA Adityo 'gnir
|p3  vidyud vai vidyutya vR^iShTim anupravishati,
     sAntardhIyate, tAM na nirjAnanti
|p4  yadA vai mriyate, 'thAntardhIyate,
     'thainAM na nirjAnanti
|p5  sa brUyAd vidyuto maraNe:
     dviShan me mriyatAM, so 'ntardhIyatAM, tam mA nirj~NasiShur iti
|p6  kShipraM haivainaM na nirjAnanti
|p7  vR^iShTir vai vR^iShTvA candramasam anupravishati,
     sAntardhIyate, tAM na nirjAnanti.
     yadA vai mriyate, 'thAntardhIyate, 'thainaM na nirjAnanti.
     sa brUyAd vR^iShTer maraNe:
     dviShan me mriyatAM, so 'ntardhIyatAM, tam mA nirj~NAsiShur iti.
     kShipraM haivainaM na nirjAnanti
|p8  candramA vA amAvAsyAyAm Adityam anupravishati,
     so 'ntardhIyatAM, taM na nirjAnanti.
     yadA vai mriyate, 'thAntardhIyate, 'thainaM na nirjAnanti.
     sa brUyAc candramaso maraNe:
     dviShan me mriyatAM, so 'ntardhIyatAM, tam mA nirj~NAsiShur iti.
     kShipraM haivainaM na nirjAnanty
|p9  Adityo vA astaM yann agnim anupravishati, so 'ntardhIyate,
     taM na nirjAnanti.
     yadA vai mriyatc, 'thAntardhIyate, 'thainAm na nirjAnanti.
     sa brUyAd Adityasya maraNe:
     dviShan me mriyatAM, so 'ntardhIyatAM, tam mA nirj~NAsiShur iti.
     kShipraM haivainaM nA nirjAnanty
|p10  Agnir vA udvAn vAyum anupravishati, so 'ntardhiyate, taM na nirjAnanti.
     yadA vai mriyate, 'thAntardhIyate, 'thainaM na nirjAnanti.
     sa brUyAd agner marANe:
     dviShan me mriyatAM, so 'ntardhIyatAM, tam mA nirj~NAsiShur iti.
     kShipraM haivainaM na nirjAnanti
|p11  tA vA etA devatA ata eva punar jAyante
|p12  vAyor agnir jAyate, prANAd dhi balAn mathyamAno 'dhijAyate.
     taM dR^iShTvA brUyAd:
     agnir jAyatAm, mA me dviSha~N jany, ata eva parA.N prajighyatv iti.
     ato haiva parA.N prajighyaty
|p13  agner vA Adityo jAyate.
     taM dR^iShTvA brUyAd:
     Adityo jAyatAm, mA me dviSha~N jany, ata eva parA.N prajighyatv ity.
     ato haiva parA.N prajighyaty
|p14  AdityAd vai candramA jAyate.
     taM dR^iShTvA brUyAc:
     candramA jAyatAm, mA me dviSha~N jany, ata eva parA.N prajighyatv iti.
     ato haiva parA.N prajighyati
|p15  candramaso vai vR^iShTir jAyate.
     tAM dR^iShTvA brUyAd:
     vR^iShTir jAyatAm, mA me &8 dviSha~N jany, ata eva parA.N prajighyatv ity.
     ato haiva parA.N prajighyati
|p16  vR^iShTer vai vidyuj jAyate.
     tAM dR^iShTvA brUyAd:
     vidyuj jAyatAm, mA me dviSha~N jany, ata eva parA.N prajighyatv ity.
     ato baiva parAn prajighyati
|p17  sa eSha brahmaNaH parimaras
|p18  tam etam brahmaNaH parimaram
     #maitreyaH #kauShAravaH #sutvane #kairishaye #bhArgAyaNAya rAj~Ne provAca,
     taM ba pa~Nca rAjAnaH parimamrus, tataH #sutvA mahaj jagAma
|p19  tasya vrataM:
     na dviShataH pUrva upavished; yadi tiShThantam manyeta, tiShThetaiva.
     na dviShataH pUrvaH saMvished; yady AsInam manyetAsItaiva.
     na dviShataH pUrvaH prasvapyAd:
     yadi jAgratam manyeta, &1 jAgR^iyAd evA/pi
|p20  ha yady asyAshmamUrdhA dviShan bhavati,
     kShipraM haivainaM stR^iNute stR^iNute
